    <div class="panel" data-panel="behavior">
      <div class="card">
        <h3>Personality</h3>
        <div class="note">Where the character sits on each dial — the model's tone follows these, and the centre is neutral. (Perchance's model exposes no temperature, so "heat" lives in sarcasm + playfulness.)</div>
        <div id="dials" style="margin-top:10px"></div>
        <div class="row" style="margin-top:8px"><button class="btn" id="dialsReset">Reset to neutral</button></div>

        <div class="toggle" style="border:none;padding-top:10px"><input type="checkbox" id="modEnabled"><div><div class="tl">Enable the content gate</div><div class="td">the character won’t draw anything matching a blocked term</div></div></div>
        <textarea id="modPhrases" rows="3" placeholder="one blocked phrase per line — e.g.&#10;gore&#10;bad*word" style="margin-top:6px"></textarea>

      </div>
      <div class="card">

        <div class="note">Show a small read of the character’s mood beside each reply, inferred from their own words. It’s just a display touch — it never changes what they say.</div>
        <div class="toggle" style="border:none;padding-top:10px"><input type="checkbox" id="emoToggle"><div><div class="tl">Show mood on each reply</div><div class="td">e.g. a soft \uD83D\uDE0A when warm, \uD83D\uDE0F when teasing</div></div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="note" style="margin:4px 0 8px">These are the parts of the character’s mind you can turn on and off. They all run locally in your browser, and changes take effect immediately.</div>
      <div id="behaviorToggles"></div>
    </div>

          <span class="status" id="accentNote"></span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="row" style="margin-top:4px"><button class="btn" id="appearanceReset">Reset appearance</button></div>

    <!-- MEMORY & DATA -->
    <div class="panel" data-panel="about">

        <div class="note">A standalone, in-browser AI companion built on the Chloe cognitive engine — facts, insights, episodic and semantic memory, reflection, and feedback learning, all running locally with no server and no account.       </div>
      <div class="note">Open <b>Thoughts</b> any time to watch a character think, and slow the pace down to read along.</div>

<script>
/* ============================================================================
   Weld bundle — self-hosted. Davie's own audited Weld plugins, inlined verbatim
   from their doc pages instead of {import:weld-*-plugin}. Each installs window.weld.<name>.
   Source: github.com/therealwestninja  ·  perchance.org/weld-ui-index
   ============================================================================ */
(function(){ if (!window.weld) window.weld = {}; })();

/* ---- weld.markdown ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.markdown) return; // already loaded

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// HTML escape -- the foundation of safety
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function escapeHtml(s) {
  return String(s)
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// URL sanitization -- reject javascript:, vbscript:, data: (except images)
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
var SAFE_URL_RE = /^(?:https?:|mailto:|tel:|\/|#|\.\/|\.\.\/|[a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+\.)/;
var SAFE_IMG_URL_RE = /^(?:https?:|data:image\/(?:png|jpe?g|gif|webp|svg\+xml);|\/|\.\/|\.\.\/)/;

function safeUrl(url, forImg) {
  url = String(url).trim();
  var re = forImg ? SAFE_IMG_URL_RE : SAFE_URL_RE;
  return re.test(url) ? url : '#';
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Inline formatting: bold, italic, strikethrough -- applied to text
// where no HTML has been injected yet
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function applyFormatting(text) {
  // Bold first (longer marker wins)
  text = text.replace(/\*\*([^*\n]+)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
  text = text.replace(/__([^_\n]+)__/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
  // Italic (single marker)
  text = text.replace(/(^|[^*])\*([^*\n]+)\*(?!\*)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>');
  text = text.replace(/(^|[^_])_([^_\n]+)_(?!_)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>');
  // Strikethrough
  text = text.replace(/~~([^~\n]+)~~/g, '<del>$1</del>');
  return text;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Inline parsing -- code, images, links, auto-links, then formatting
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function parseInline(text) {
  var slots = [];
  function slot(html) {
    slots.push(html);
    return '\u0001S' + (slots.length - 1) + '\u0001';
  }

  // 1. Code spans -- extract first, content escaped, no further processing
  text = text.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, function(_, code) {
    return slot('<code>' + escapeHtml(code) + '</code>');
  });

  // 2. Images:  exclamation + label-in-brackets + paren-url
  text = text.replace(/!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)\s]+)(?:\s+"([^"]*)")?\)/g, function(_, alt, url, title) {
    var t = title ? ' title="' + escapeHtml(title) + '"' : '';
    return slot('<img src="' + safeUrl(url, true) + '" alt="' + escapeHtml(alt) + '"' + t + '>');
  });

  // 3. Links: label-in-brackets followed by paren-url
  text = text.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)\s]+)(?:\s+"([^"]*)")?\)/g, function(_, label, url, title) {
    var t = title ? ' title="' + escapeHtml(title) + '"' : '';
    // Allow inline formatting inside link label
    var inner = applyFormatting(escapeHtml(label));
    return slot('<a href="' + safeUrl(url) + '"' + t + ' target="_blank" rel="noopener">' + inner + '</a>');
  });

  // 4. Auto-links: bare URLs (not already inside a slot)
  text = text.replace(/\b(https?:\/\/[^\s<]+[^\s<.,;:?!])/g, function(url) {
    return slot('<a href="' + safeUrl(url) + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">' + escapeHtml(url) + '</a>');
  });

  // 5. Escape any remaining HTML in the plain text
  text = escapeHtml(text);

  // 6. Apply bold/italic/strikethrough on the now-safe text
  text = applyFormatting(text);

  // 7. Restore slot placeholders
  text = text.replace(/\u0001S(\d+)\u0001/g, function(_, idx) {
    return slots[parseInt(idx, 10)];
  });

  return text;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Block-level parsing
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function render(input, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  if (typeof input !== 'string') input = String(input == null ? '' : input);

  // Normalize line endings
  input = input.replace(/\r\n?/g, '\n');

  var lines = input.split('\n');
  var out = [];
  var i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    var line = lines[i];

    // Fenced code block: ``` or ~~~
    var fence = line.match(/^(```|~~~)\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_-]*)\s*$/);
    if (fence) {
      var marker = fence[1];
      var lang = fence[2] || '';
      i++;
      var code = [];
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].indexOf(marker) !== 0) {
        code.push(lines[i]);
        i++;
      }
      i++;
      var langAttr = lang ? ' class="language-' + escapeHtml(lang) + '"' : '';
      out.push('<pre><code' + langAttr + '>' + escapeHtml(code.join('\n')) + '</code></pre>');
      continue;
    }

    // ATX header: # to ######
    var hdr = line.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.+)$/);
    if (hdr) {
      var n = hdr[1].length;
      out.push('<h' + n + '>' + parseInline(hdr[2]) + '</h' + n + '>');
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Horizontal rule
    if (/^\s*([-*_])\s*\1\s*\1[\s\1]*$/.test(line)) {
      out.push('<hr>');
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Blockquote
    if (line.charAt(0) === '>') {
      var quote = [];
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].charAt(0) === '>') {
        quote.push(lines[i].replace(/^>\s?/, ''));
        i++;
      }
      out.push('<blockquote>' + render(quote.join('\n')) + '</blockquote>');
      continue;
    }

    // Unordered list
    if (/^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(line)) {
      var items = [];
      while (i < lines.length && /^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(lines[i])) {
        items.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*[-*+]\s+/, ''));
        i++;
      }
      out.push('<ul>' + items.map(function(it) { return '<li>' + parseInline(it) + '</li>'; }).join('') + '</ul>');
      continue;
    }

    // Ordered list
    if (/^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line)) {
      var oitems = [];
      while (i < lines.length && /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(lines[i])) {
        oitems.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/, ''));
        i++;
      }
      out.push('<ol>' + oitems.map(function(it) { return '<li>' + parseInline(it) + '</li>'; }).join('') + '</ol>');
      continue;
    }

    // Empty line: skip
    if (line.trim() === '') {
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Paragraph: gather consecutive non-empty lines
    var para = [line];
    i++;
    while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim() !== '' && !/^(#{1,6}\s|```|~~~|>|\s*[-*+]\s|\s*\d+\.\s)/.test(lines[i])) {
      para.push(lines[i]);
      i++;
    }
    out.push('<p>' + parseInline(para.join(' ')) + '</p>');
  }

  return out.join('\n');
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Convenience: render into an element
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function renderInto(el, input, opts) {
  if (typeof el === 'string') el = document.querySelector(el);
  if (!el) throw new Error('weld.markdown.renderInto: element not found');
  el.innerHTML = render(input, opts);
  return el;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Sanitize an arbitrary HTML string -- only allow safe tags/attrs
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
var ALLOWED_TAGS = {
  p: 1, br: 1, hr: 1,
  h1: 1, h2: 1, h3: 1, h4: 1, h5: 1, h6: 1,
  strong: 1, em: 1, del: 1, b: 1, i: 1, u: 1, s: 1,
  ul: 1, ol: 1, li: 1,
  blockquote: 1, pre: 1, code: 1,
  a: 1, img: 1,
  table: 1, thead: 1, tbody: 1, tr: 1, th: 1, td: 1,
  div: 1, span: 1
};
var ALLOWED_ATTRS = {
  a: { href: 1, title: 1, target: 1, rel: 1 },
  img: { src: 1, alt: 1, title: 1, width: 1, height: 1 },
  '*': { 'class': 1 }
};

function sanitize(html) {
  var tmp = document.createElement('template');
  tmp.innerHTML = String(html);
  walk(tmp.content);
  return tmp.innerHTML;
}

function walk(node) {
  var children = Array.prototype.slice.call(node.childNodes);
  for (var i = 0; i < children.length; i++) {
    var child = children[i];
    if (child.nodeType === 1) { // element
      var tag = child.tagName.toLowerCase();
      if (!ALLOWED_TAGS[tag]) {
        // Replace with its text content
        var text = document.createTextNode(child.textContent);
        child.parentNode.replaceChild(text, child);
        continue;
      }
      // Strip unsafe attributes
      var attrs = Array.prototype.slice.call(child.attributes);
      for (var j = 0; j < attrs.length; j++) {
        var attr = attrs[j];
        var tagAllowed = ALLOWED_ATTRS[tag] && ALLOWED_ATTRS[tag][attr.name];
        var globalAllowed = ALLOWED_ATTRS['*'][attr.name];
        if (!tagAllowed && !globalAllowed) {
          child.removeAttribute(attr.name);
          continue;
        }
        // URL attrs: sanitize
        if (attr.name === 'href') child.setAttribute('href', safeUrl(attr.value));
        if (attr.name === 'src') {
          var isImg = tag === 'img';
          child.setAttribute('src', safeUrl(attr.value, isImg));
        }
      }
      walk(child);
    }
  }
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// API
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
window.weld.markdown = {
  render: render,
  renderInto: renderInto,
  sanitize: sanitize,
  parseInline: parseInline,
  escapeHtml: escapeHtml,
  safeUrl: safeUrl,
  version: '1.0.0'
};

})();

/* ---- weld.banlist ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.banlist) return window.weld.banlist;

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// weld.banlist: the explicit deny-lists every community gallery/chat
// ends up needing -- banned users, banned phrases (in prompts and in
// negative prompts), and a content-rating ceiling. weld.spamguard
// handles "this looks like copy-paste spam"; weld.banlist handles
// "this exact thing is not allowed here".
//
//   var list = weld.banlist.create({ users, phrases, negativePhrases, rating });
//   list.checkUser(name)               -> { ok, reason }
//   list.check(text)                   -> { ok, matched, reason }
//   list.checkPrompt(prompt, negative) -> { ok, reasons }
//   list.allowedRating(itemRating)     -> bool   (item <= configured ceiling)
//   list.filter(items, getText)        -> items that pass
//
// Phrases support plain substring and "*" wildcards, case-insensitive.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------

var RATINGS = ['g', 'pg', 'pg13', 'r', 'x'];

function normalize(s) { return String(s == null ? '' : s).toLowerCase(); }

// Compile a phrase (with optional "*" wildcards) into a tester.
function compile(phrase) {
  var p = normalize(phrase).trim();
  if (!p) return null;
  if (p.indexOf('*') === -1) {
    return { raw: p, test: function (text) { return text.indexOf(p) !== -1; } };
  }
  // Wildcard: escape regex, turn * into .*
  var esc = p.replace(/[.+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&').replace(/\*/g, '.*');
  var re = new RegExp(esc);
  return { raw: p, test: function (text) { return re.test(text); } };
}

function compileList(arr) {
  var out = [];
  (arr || []).forEach(function (p) { var c = compile(p); if (c) out.push(c); });
  return out;
}

function ratingRank(r) {
  var i = RATINGS.indexOf(normalize(r));
  return i === -1 ? RATINGS.length : i; // unknown = most restrictive (treated as above x)
}

function create(config) {
  config = config || {};
  var users = {};
  (config.users || []).forEach(function (u) { users[normalize(u)] = true; });
  var phrases = compileList(config.phrases);
  var negPhrases = compileList(config.negativePhrases);
  var ceiling = config.rating != null ? normalize(config.rating) : 'x'; // default: allow all

  function checkUser(name) {
    var ok = !users[normalize(name)];
    return { ok: ok, reason: ok ? null : 'banned user' };
  }

  function matchIn(text, list) {
    var t = normalize(text);
    for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) if (list[i].test(t)) return list[i].raw;
    return null;
  }

  function check(text) {
    var m = matchIn(text, phrases);
    return { ok: !m, matched: m, reason: m ? ('banned phrase: ' + m) : null };
  }

  function checkPrompt(prompt, negative) {
    var reasons = [];
    var m1 = matchIn(prompt, phrases);
    if (m1) reasons.push('banned phrase: ' + m1);
    if (negative != null) {
      var m2 = matchIn(negative, negPhrases);
      if (m2) reasons.push('banned negative phrase: ' + m2);
    }
    return { ok: reasons.length === 0, reasons: reasons };
  }

  function allowedRating(itemRating) {
    return ratingRank(itemRating) <= ratingRank(ceiling);
  }

  // Filter a list of items. getText(item) -> the text to check; items may
  // also carry { user, rating } which are checked when present.
  function filter(items, getText) {
    getText = getText || function (x) { return x && (x.text || x.prompt || x); };
    return (items || []).filter(function (it) {
      if (it && it.user != null && !checkUser(it.user).ok) return false;
      if (it && it.rating != null && !allowedRating(it.rating)) return false;
      return check(getText(it)).ok;
    });
  }

  return {
    checkUser: checkUser,
    check: check,
    checkPrompt: checkPrompt,
    allowedRating: allowedRating,
    filter: filter,
    banUser: function (u) { users[normalize(u)] = true; },
    unbanUser: function (u) { delete users[normalize(u)]; },
    addPhrase: function (p) { var c = compile(p); if (c) phrases.push(c); },
    addNegativePhrase: function (p) { var c = compile(p); if (c) negPhrases.push(c); },
    setRating: function (r) { ceiling = normalize(r); },
    rating: function () { return ceiling; },
    users: function () { return Object.keys(users); }
  };
}

window.weld.banlist = {
  create: create,
  ratings: RATINGS.slice(),
  version: '1.0.0'
};

return window.weld.banlist;
})();

/* ---- weld.gallery ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.gallery) return; // already loaded

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// weld.gallery: Image grid with IndexedDB blob storage.
// Manifest tracks metadata per image (prompt, seed, timestamp, fav).
// Integrates with weld.ui.lightbox for fullscreen viewing.
// Eviction: when full, drop oldest non-favorited first.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------

var DB_STORE = 'blobs';

function uid() {
  return 'img_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6);
}

function createGallery(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var dbName = opts.dbName || 'weld-gallery';
  var maxItems = opts.maxItems || 200;
  var manifest = [];
  var dbInstance = null;
  var dbPromise = null;
  var container = null;
  var lightboxInstance = null;
  var sortMode = opts.sortMode || 'newest';
  var favOnly = false;
  var changeListeners = [];

  // -------- IndexedDB for blobs --------
  function openDb() {
    if (dbInstance) return Promise.resolve(dbInstance);
    if (dbPromise) return dbPromise;
    dbPromise = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      var req = indexedDB.open(dbName, 1);
      req.onupgradeneeded = function(e) {
        var db = e.target.result;
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(DB_STORE)) {
          db.createObjectStore(DB_STORE);
        }
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('meta')) {
          db.createObjectStore('meta');
        }
      };
      req.onsuccess = function(e) { dbInstance = e.target.result; resolve(dbInstance); };
      req.onerror = function(e) { dbPromise = null; reject(e.target.error); };
    });
    return dbPromise;
  }

  function idbOp(store, mode, fn) {
    return openDb().then(function(db) {
      return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
        var tx = db.transaction(store, mode);
        var s = tx.objectStore(store);
        var req = fn(s);
        if (req && req.onsuccess !== undefined) {
          req.onsuccess = function() { resolve(req.result); };
          req.onerror = function() { reject(req.error); };
        } else {
          tx.oncomplete = function() { resolve(); };
          tx.onerror = function() { reject(tx.error); };
        }
      });
    });
  }

  function saveManifest() {
    return idbOp('meta', 'readwrite', function(s) { return s.put(manifest, 'manifest'); });
  }

  function loadManifest() {
    return idbOp('meta', 'readonly', function(s) { return s.get('manifest'); }).then(function(m) {
      manifest = m || [];
    });
  }

  function emit() {
    for (var i = 0; i < changeListeners.length; i++) {
      try { changeListeners[i](manifest); } catch (e) {}
    }
  }

  // -------- Core operations --------
  function store(blob, meta) {
    if (!(blob instanceof Blob)) {
      return Promise.reject(new Error('gallery.store: expected a Blob'));
    }
    meta = meta || {};
    var id = uid();
    var entry = {
      id: id,
      prompt: meta.prompt || '',
      seed: meta.seed != null ? meta.seed : null,
      resolution: meta.resolution || null,
      createdAt: Date.now(),
      favorited: false,
      metadata: meta.metadata || null
    };

    return idbOp(DB_STORE, 'readwrite', function(s) { return s.put(blob, id); }).then(function() {
      // Eviction
      while (manifest.length >= maxItems) {
        var evictIdx = -1;
        for (var i = 0; i < manifest.length; i++) {
          if (!manifest[i].favorited) { evictIdx = i; break; }
        }
        if (evictIdx === -1) evictIdx = 0;
        var removed = manifest.splice(evictIdx, 1)[0];
        // Best-effort blob cleanup
        idbOp(DB_STORE, 'readwrite', function(s) { return s.delete(removed.id); }).catch(function() {});
      }
      manifest.push(entry);
      return saveManifest();
    }).then(function() {
      emit();
      return id;
    });
  }

  function remove(id) {
    manifest = manifest.filter(function(e) { return e.id !== id; });
    return Promise.all([
      idbOp(DB_STORE, 'readwrite', function(s) { return s.delete(id); }).catch(function() {}),
      saveManifest()
    ]).then(function() { emit(); return true; });
  }

  function removeMany(ids) {
    var idSet = {};
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) idSet[ids[i]] = true;
    manifest = manifest.filter(function(e) { return !idSet[e.id]; });
    var chain = Promise.resolve();
    ids.forEach(function(id) {
      chain = chain.then(function() {
        return idbOp(DB_STORE, 'readwrite', function(s) { return s.delete(id); }).catch(function() {});
      });
    });
    return chain.then(saveManifest).then(function() { emit(); });
  }

  function clear() {
    var ids = manifest.map(function(e) { return e.id; });
    manifest = [];
    return removeMany(ids).then(saveManifest).then(function() { emit(); });
  }

  function toggleFavorite(id) {
    var entry = manifest.find(function(e) { return e.id === id; });
    if (!entry) return Promise.resolve(null);
    entry.favorited = !entry.favorited;
    return saveManifest().then(function() { emit(); return entry.favorited; });
  }

  function getBlob(id) {
    return idbOp(DB_STORE, 'readonly', function(s) { return s.get(id); });
  }

  function getBlobUrl(id) {
    return getBlob(id).then(function(blob) {
      return blob ? URL.createObjectURL(blob) : null;
    });
  }

  // -------- Sorted/filtered view --------
  function getView() {
    var view = manifest.slice();
    if (favOnly) view = view.filter(function(e) { return e.favorited; });
    switch (sortMode) {
      case 'oldest':
        view.sort(function(a, b) { return (a.createdAt || 0) - (b.createdAt || 0); });
        break;
      case 'favorites':
        view.sort(function(a, b) {
          if (a.favorited !== b.favorited) return a.favorited ? -1 : 1;
          return (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0);
        });
        break;
      default:
        view.sort(function(a, b) { return (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0); });
    }
    return view;
  }

  function setSort(mode) { sortMode = mode; emit(); }
  function setFavOnly(v) { favOnly = !!v; emit(); }

  // -------- Rendering --------
  function render(targetEl) {
    container = typeof targetEl === 'string' ? document.querySelector(targetEl) : targetEl;
    if (!container) return Promise.reject(new Error('gallery.render: container not found'));
    return loadManifest().then(function() { return renderView(); });
  }

  function renderView() {
    if (!container) return Promise.resolve();
    var view = getView();
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (view.length === 0) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--weld-muted,#7d8590);font:13px var(--weld-mono,monospace);padding:40px;text-align:center;">No images yet.</div>';
      return Promise.resolve();
    }
    var promises = [];
    view.forEach(function(entry) {
      var cell = document.createElement('div');
      cell.className = 'w-gallery-item' + (entry.favorited ? ' is-fav' : '');
      cell.dataset.id = entry.id;
      cell.innerHTML = '<div class="w-gallery-loading"></div>';
      container.appendChild(cell);
      var p = getBlobUrl(entry.id).then(function(url) {
        if (!url) { cell.innerHTML = '<div class="w-gallery-empty">missing</div>'; return; }
        var img = document.createElement('img');
        img.src = url;
        img.alt = entry.prompt || '';
        img.addEventListener('click', function() { openLightbox(entry.id); });
        cell.innerHTML = '';
        cell.appendChild(img);
        // Seed tag
        if (entry.seed != null) {
          var tag = document.createElement('div');
          tag.className = 'w-gallery-seed';
          tag.textContent = 'seed ' + entry.seed;
          cell.appendChild(tag);
        }
      });
      promises.push(p);
    });
    return Promise.all(promises);
  }

  function openLightbox(startId) {
    if (!window.weld || !window.weld.ui || !window.weld.ui.lightbox) return;
    if (!lightboxInstance) lightboxInstance = window.weld.ui.lightbox();
    var view = getView();
    var items = [];
    var startIdx = 0;
    view.forEach(function(entry, i) {
      items.push({ src: '', id: entry.id, meta: entry.prompt || '', alt: entry.prompt || '' });
      if (entry.id === startId) startIdx = i;
    });
    // Resolve blob URLs
    var chain = Promise.resolve();
    items.forEach(function(item, idx) {
      chain = chain.then(function() {
        return getBlobUrl(item.id).then(function(url) { items[idx].src = url || ''; });
      });
    });
    chain.then(function() {
      lightboxInstance.open(items, { index: startIdx });
    });
  }

  // -------- Download --------
  function downloadImage(id, filename) {
    return getBlob(id).then(function(blob) {
      if (!blob) return false;
      var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      var a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = filename || (id + '.jpg');
      document.body.appendChild(a);
      a.click();
      document.body.removeChild(a);
      setTimeout(function() { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1000);
      return true;
    });
  }

  // -------- Init --------
  function init() {
    return loadManifest();
  }

  function onChange(fn) {
    changeListeners.push(fn);
    return function() {
      var idx = changeListeners.indexOf(fn);
      if (idx >= 0) changeListeners.splice(idx, 1);
    };
  }

  return {
    init: init,
    store: store,
    remove: remove,
    removeMany: removeMany,
    clear: clear,
    toggleFavorite: toggleFavorite,
    getBlob: getBlob,
    getBlobUrl: getBlobUrl,
    getView: getView,
    getManifest: function() { return manifest.slice(); },
    setSort: setSort,
    setFavOnly: setFavOnly,
    render: render,
    renderView: renderView,
    downloadImage: downloadImage,
    onChange: onChange,
    count: function() { return manifest.length; },
    maxItems: function() { return maxItems; }
  };
}

// Inject gallery grid CSS
function injectGalleryCss() {
  if (window.__weldGalleryCss) return;
  window.__weldGalleryCss = true;
  var s = document.createElement('style');
  s.textContent =
    '.w-gallery{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(160px,1fr));gap:10px;}' +
    '.w-gallery-item{aspect-ratio:1;background:var(--weld-faint,#21262d);' +
      'border:1px solid var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));border-radius:6px;' +
      'overflow:hidden;position:relative;cursor:pointer;}' +

window.weld.gallery = {
  create: function(opts) {
    injectGalleryCss();
    return createGallery(opts);
  },
  version: '1.0.0'
};

})();

/* ---- weld.toast ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.toast) return; // already loaded

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// CSS injection -- once
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function injectCss() {
  if (window.__weldToastCss) return;
  window.__weldToastCss = true;

    '.weld-toast .weld-toast-close{cursor:pointer;color:var(--weld-muted,#7d8590);' +

      'border-color:var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));}' +

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Toast host management
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
var config = {
  position: 'top-right',
  duration: 4000,
  max: 5
};
var hosts = {};
var activeToasts = [];

function getHost(position) {
  if (hosts[position]) return hosts[position];
  var h = document.createElement('div');
  h.className = 'weld-toast-host ' + position;
  document.body.appendChild(h);
  hosts[position] = h;
  return h;
}

function configure(opts) {
  if (!opts) return;
  if (opts.position) config.position = opts.position;
  if (opts.duration != null) config.duration = opts.duration;
  if (opts.max != null) config.max = opts.max;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Toast notification
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
var ICONS = {
  info:    'i',
  success: '\u2713',
  warn:    '!',
  error:   'x'
};

function show(message, opts) {
  injectCss();
  opts = opts || {};
  var type = opts.type || 'info';
  var duration = opts.duration != null ? opts.duration : config.duration;
  var position = opts.position || config.position;
  var dismissible = opts.dismissible !== false;

  var host = getHost(position);

  var toast = document.createElement('div');
  toast.className = 'weld-toast ' + type;

  var icon = document.createElement('div');
  icon.className = 'weld-toast-icon';
  icon.textContent = ICONS[type] || ICONS.info;
  toast.appendChild(icon);

  var msg = document.createElement('div');
  msg.className = 'weld-toast-msg';
  msg.textContent = String(message);
  toast.appendChild(msg);

  if (dismissible) {
    var close = document.createElement('button');
    close.className = 'weld-toast-close';
    close.textContent = '\u00d7';
    close.setAttribute('aria-label', 'close');
    close.addEventListener('click', function() { dismiss(handle); });
    toast.appendChild(close);
  }

  // Enforce max
  while (activeToasts.length >= config.max) {
    var oldest = activeToasts.shift();
    if (oldest) dismiss(oldest, true);
  }

  host.appendChild(toast);
  // Trigger CSS transition
  setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.add('shown'); }, 10);

  var timer = null;
  var handle = { toast: toast, host: host, dismissed: false, _t: null };
  activeToasts.push(handle);

  if (duration > 0) {
    handle._t = setTimeout(function() { dismiss(handle); }, duration);
  }

  return handle;
}

function dismiss(handle, immediate) {
  if (!handle || handle.dismissed) return;
  handle.dismissed = true;
  if (handle._t) clearTimeout(handle._t);
  var idx = activeToasts.indexOf(handle);
  if (idx !== -1) activeToasts.splice(idx, 1);

  if (immediate) {
    if (handle.toast.parentNode) handle.toast.parentNode.removeChild(handle.toast);
    return;
  }
  handle.toast.classList.remove('shown');
  setTimeout(function() {
    if (handle.toast.parentNode) handle.toast.parentNode.removeChild(handle.toast);
  }, 240);
}

function clearAll() {
  while (activeToasts.length) {
    dismiss(activeToasts[0], true);
  }
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Modal helpers: prompt, confirm
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
function buildBackdrop() {
  injectCss();
  var bg = document.createElement('div');
  bg.className = 'weld-toast-backdrop';
  document.body.appendChild(bg);
  setTimeout(function() { bg.classList.add('shown'); }, 10);
  return bg;
}

function teardown(bg) {
  bg.classList.remove('shown');
  setTimeout(function() {
    if (bg.parentNode) bg.parentNode.removeChild(bg);
  }, 200);
}

function confirmDialog(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var title = opts.title || 'Confirm';
  var message = opts.message || 'Are you sure?';
  var okLabel = opts.okLabel || 'OK';
  var cancelLabel = opts.cancelLabel || 'Cancel';
  var danger = opts.danger === true;

  return new Promise(function(resolve) {
    var bg = buildBackdrop();
    var modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.className = 'weld-toast-modal';

    var h = document.createElement('h4');
    h.textContent = title;
    modal.appendChild(h);

    var p = document.createElement('p');
    p.textContent = message;
    modal.appendChild(p);

    var actions = document.createElement('div');
    actions.className = 'weld-toast-actions';

    var cancel = document.createElement('button');
    cancel.className = 'weld-toast-btn ghost';
    cancel.textContent = cancelLabel;
    cancel.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(false); });
    actions.appendChild(cancel);

    var ok = document.createElement('button');
    ok.className = 'weld-toast-btn ' + (danger ? 'danger' : 'primary');
    ok.textContent = okLabel;
    ok.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(true); });
    actions.appendChild(ok);

    modal.appendChild(actions);
    bg.appendChild(modal);
    setTimeout(function() { ok.focus(); }, 100);
  });
}

function promptDialog(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var title = opts.title || 'Prompt';
  var message = opts.message || '';
  var placeholder = opts.placeholder || '';
  var defaultValue = opts.defaultValue || '';
  var multiline = opts.multiline === true;
  var okLabel = opts.okLabel || 'OK';
  var cancelLabel = opts.cancelLabel || 'Cancel';

  return new Promise(function(resolve) {
    var bg = buildBackdrop();
    var modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.className = 'weld-toast-modal';

    var h = document.createElement('h4');
    h.textContent = title;
    modal.appendChild(h);

    if (message) {
      var p = document.createElement('p');
      p.textContent = message;
      modal.appendChild(p);
    }

    var input;
    if (multiline) {
      input = document.createElement('textarea');
    } else {
      input = document.createElement('input');
      input.type = 'text';
    }
    input.placeholder = placeholder;
    input.value = defaultValue;
    modal.appendChild(input);

    var actions = document.createElement('div');
    actions.className = 'weld-toast-actions';

    var cancel = document.createElement('button');
    cancel.className = 'weld-toast-btn ghost';
    cancel.textContent = cancelLabel;
    cancel.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(null); });
    actions.appendChild(cancel);

    var ok = document.createElement('button');
    ok.className = 'weld-toast-btn primary';
    ok.textContent = okLabel;
    ok.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(input.value); });
    actions.appendChild(ok);

    modal.appendChild(actions);
    bg.appendChild(modal);
    setTimeout(function() { input.focus(); input.select(); }, 100);

    if (!multiline) {
      input.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') { teardown(bg); resolve(input.value); }
        if (e.key === 'Escape') { teardown(bg); resolve(null); }
      });
    }
  });
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// API
// -----------------------------------------------------------------
window.weld.toast = {
  show: show,
  info:    function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'info';    return show(m, o); },
  success: function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'success'; return show(m, o); },
  warn:    function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'warn';    return show(m, o); },
  error:   function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'error';   return show(m, o); },
  dismiss: dismiss,
  clear:   clearAll,
  configure: configure,
  confirm: confirmDialog,
  prompt:  promptDialog,
  version: '1.0.0'
};

})();

/* ---- weld.spamguard ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.spamguard) return; // already loaded

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// Multi-channel chat spam guard.
// Detects copy-paste spam across channels using:
//   1. Normalised text fingerprint (lowercase, NFKD, emoji + punct stripped,
//      char-repeat dampened, whitespace collapsed)
//   2. Token-set Jaccard similarity for near-identical messages
// Cross-channel threshold + sliding time window controls ban trigger.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------

function fingerprint(text) {
  if (typeof text !== 'string') return '';
  return text
    .toLowerCase()
    .normalize('NFKD')
    .replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '')
    .replace(/[\p{Emoji_Presentation}\p{Extended_Pictographic}]/gu, '')
    .replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}\s]/gu, ' ')
    .replace(/(.)\1{2,}/g, '$1$1')
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
    .trim();
}

// Jaccard similarity on word-token sets, 0 (disjoint) to 1 (identical)
function jaccard(a, b) {
  if (a === b) return 1;
  if (!a || !b) return 0;
  var A = new Set(a.split(' '));
  var B = new Set(b.split(' '));
  var inter = 0;
  var itr = A.values();
  var step;
  while (!(step = itr.next()).done) {
    if (B.has(step.value)) inter++;
  }
  var union = A.size + B.size - inter;
  return union === 0 ? 0 : inter / union;
}

function similarEnough(a, b, threshold) {
  if (a === b) return true;
  return jaccard(a, b) >= threshold;
}

function createGuard(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var DEFAULTS = {
    channelThreshold: 3,
    windowMs: 60000,
    similarityThreshold: 0.92,
    minMessageLength: 5,
    maxHistoryPerUser: 50,
    autoBan: true,
    autoDelete: true,
    banDurationMs: 0,
    whitelistUserIds: [],
    banFn: null,
    deleteFn: null,
    onSpamDetected: null,
    onBan: null
  };
  var merged = Object.assign({}, DEFAULTS, opts);

  var history = new Map();   // userId -> array of message records
  var banned  = new Map();   // userId -> ban record (reason / bannedAt / expiresAt)
  var stats   = { tracked: 0, banned: 0, totalReports: 0, totalBans: 0, totalDeletes: 0 };

  function pruneOld(userId, now) {
    var arr = history.get(userId);
    if (!arr) return;
    var cutoff = now - merged.windowMs;
    var i = 0;
    while (i < arr.length && arr[i].timestamp < cutoff) i++;
    if (i > 0) arr.splice(0, i);
    if (arr.length > merged.maxHistoryPerUser) {
      arr.splice(0, arr.length - merged.maxHistoryPerUser);
    }
  }

  function checkBanExpiry(userId, now) {
    var b = banned.get(userId);
    if (b && b.expiresAt && b.expiresAt <= now) {
      banned.delete(userId);
      return false;
    }
    return !!b;
  }

  function classify(userId, fp, now) {
    var arr = history.get(userId) || [];
    var matchedByChannel = new Map();
    for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
      var m = arr[i];
      if (similarEnough(m.fp, fp, merged.similarityThreshold)) {
        if (!matchedByChannel.has(m.channel)) matchedByChannel.set(m.channel, m);
      }
    }
    if (matchedByChannel.size >= merged.channelThreshold) {
      var matches = Array.from(matchedByChannel.values());
      return {
        fingerprint: fp,
        channels: Array.from(matchedByChannel.keys()),
        messages: matches,
        firstSeen: Math.min.apply(null, matches.map(function(m) { return m.timestamp; })),
        lastSeen: now
      };
    }
    return null;
  }

  // -------- PUBLIC: report a new message --------
  function report(input) {
    return Promise.resolve().then(function() {
      stats.totalReports++;
      if (!input || !input.userId || !input.channel) {
        return { ok: false, reason: 'missing userId or channel' };
      }
      var channel = input.channel;
      var userId = input.userId;
      var messageId = input.messageId;
      var text = input.text;

      if (merged.whitelistUserIds.indexOf(userId) !== -1) {
        return { ok: true, whitelisted: true };
      }

      var now = input.timestamp || Date.now();
      if (checkBanExpiry(userId, now)) {
        return { ok: false, banned: true };
      }

      if (typeof text !== 'string' || text.length < merged.minMessageLength) {
        return { ok: true };
      }
      var fp = fingerprint(text);
      if (!fp) return { ok: true };

      pruneOld(userId, now);
      if (!history.has(userId)) history.set(userId, []);
      var arr = history.get(userId);
      arr.push({ channel: channel, fp: fp, text: text, messageId: messageId, timestamp: now });
      stats.tracked = history.size;

      var spam = classify(userId, fp, now);
      if (!spam) return { ok: true };

      // Include the triggering message itself
      var alreadyHas = false;
      for (var i = 0; i < spam.messages.length; i++) {
        if (spam.messages[i].channel === channel) { alreadyHas = true; break; }
      }
      if (!alreadyHas) {
        spam.channels.push(channel);
        spam.messages.push({ channel: channel, fp: fp, text: text, messageId: messageId, timestamp: now });
      }

      var verdict = Promise.resolve(true);
      if (typeof merged.onSpamDetected === 'function') {
        verdict = Promise.resolve(merged.onSpamDetected(spam));
      }

      return verdict.then(function(v) {
        if (v === false) return { ok: true, vetoed: true, spam: spam };

        var actions = Promise.resolve();
        if (merged.autoBan) {
          var expiresAt = merged.banDurationMs > 0 ? now + merged.banDurationMs : null;
          banned.set(userId, { reason: 'cross-channel-spam', bannedAt: now, expiresAt: expiresAt });
          stats.banned++;
          stats.totalBans++;
          if (typeof merged.banFn === 'function') {
            actions = actions.then(function() {
              return Promise.resolve(merged.banFn(userId, { reason: 'cross-channel-spam', spam: spam }))
                .catch(function(e) { console.error('[weld.spamguard] banFn threw:', e); });
            });
          }
          if (typeof merged.onBan === 'function') {
            actions = actions.then(function() {
              return Promise.resolve(merged.onBan(userId, { reason: 'cross-channel-spam', spam: spam }))
                .catch(function() {});
            });
          }
        }

        if (merged.autoDelete && typeof merged.deleteFn === 'function') {
          spam.messages.forEach(function(m) {
            actions = actions.then(function() {
              return Promise.resolve(merged.deleteFn(m.messageId, m.channel))
                .then(function() { stats.totalDeletes++; })
                .catch(function(e) { console.error('[weld.spamguard] deleteFn threw:', e, m); });
            });
          });
        }

        return actions.then(function() {
          history.delete(userId);
          return { ok: false, banned: true, spam: spam };
        });
      });
    });
  }

  function ban(userId, reason) {
    banned.set(userId, { reason: reason || 'manual', bannedAt: Date.now(), expiresAt: null });
    stats.banned++;
    stats.totalBans++;
  }

  function unban(userId) {
    if (banned.delete(userId)) stats.banned = Math.max(0, stats.banned - 1);
  }

  function isBanned(userId) {
    return checkBanExpiry(userId, Date.now());
  }

  function bannedUsers() {
    var now = Date.now();
    return Array.from(banned.keys()).filter(function(id) { return checkBanExpiry(id, now); });
  }

  function getHistory(userId) {
    return (history.get(userId) || []).slice();
  }

  function flush() {
    history.clear();
    stats.tracked = 0;
  }

  function getStats() {
    return Object.assign({}, stats, {
      tracked: history.size,
      banned: bannedUsers().length
    });
  }

  return {
    report: report,
    ban: ban,
    unban: unban,
    isBanned: isBanned,
    bannedUsers: bannedUsers,
    history: getHistory,
    flush: flush,
    options: merged,
    stats: getStats,
    fingerprint: fingerprint,
    jaccard: jaccard
  };
}

window.weld.spamguard = {
  create: createGuard,
  fingerprint: fingerprint,
  jaccard: jaccard,
  version: '1.0.0'
};

})();

/* ---- weld.comments (self-hosted: per-page discussion thread via comments-plugin embed) ---- */
(function(){
'use strict';

if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
if (window.weld.comments) return window.weld.comments;

// -----------------------------------------------------------------
// weld.comments: per-item discussion threads.
//
// Perchance hosts a comments-plugin embed. The reusable trick is to
// give every item (image, post, scene...) its own channel by hashing a
// stable key, theme the embed to match your app, and present it either
// as an overlay modal or inline. weld.comments wraps all of that:
//
//   channel(key)            -> a stable channel id for that key
//   open({ key, title, ... })  themed overlay with the thread
//   inline(target, opts)       embed into an element
//   close()
//
// No app identity is baked in -- you pass your app slug and (optional)
// admin hash. Defaults are sensible and generic.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------

var EMBED_BASE = 'https://comments-plugin.perchance.org/embed/';
var STYLE_ID = 'weld-comments-style';
var overlay = null;

// Stable short hash (djb2 -> base36) for deriving a channel from any key.
function hash(text) {
  text = String(text == null ? '' : text);
  var h = 5381;
  for (var i = 0; i < text.length; i++) h = ((h << 5) + h + text.charCodeAt(i)) | 0;
  return Math.abs(h).toString(36);
}

// A channel id for an item. prefix groups channels under your app.
function channel(key, prefix) {
  prefix = prefix || defaultApp();
  return prefix + '-' + hash(key);
}

function defaultApp() {
  try { if (window.generatorName) return String(window.generatorName); } catch (e) {}
  return 'weld';
}

function resolveTheme(theme) {
  if (theme === 'light' || theme === 'dark') return theme;
  try { if (document.body && document.body.classList.contains('light-theme')) return 'light'; } catch (e) {}
  return 'dark';
}

function defaultConfig() {
  return {
    loadFonts: 'Open Sans, Inter',
    containerStyle: 'width:100%;height:100%;',
    inputAreaStyle: 'height:68px;',
    commentPlaceholderText: 'Add a comment...',
    submitButtonText: 'comment',
    allowBots: false
  };
}

// Build the embed src. app = generator slug the thread lives under.
function buildSrc(app, chan, config) {
  config = config || {};
  var merged = {};
  var d = defaultConfig();
  for (var k in d) merged[k] = d[k];
  for (var k2 in config) merged[k2] = config[k2];
  merged.channel = chan;
  var adminHash = merged.adminPasswordHash || '';
  var encoded = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(merged));
  var src = EMBED_BASE + app + '+' + chan + '?';
  if (adminHash) src += 'adminPasswordHash=' + adminHash;
  return src + '#' + encoded;
}

function ensureStyle() {
  if (typeof document === 'undefined' || document.getElementById(STYLE_ID)) return;
  var st = document.createElement('style');
  st.id = STYLE_ID;
  st.textContent =
    '.weld-comments-ov{z-index:99999;position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.72);display:none;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:14px;box-sizing:border-box;}'
    + '.weld-comments-card{width:min(980px,100%);height:min(760px,92dvh);background:var(--background-color,var(--bg-color,#111));color:var(--text-color,#eee);border:1px solid var(--border-color,#444);border-radius:12px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;overflow:hidden;box-shadow:0 12px 40px rgba(0,0,0,.35);}'
    + '.weld-comments-head{display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:8px;padding:9px 10px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border-color,#444);}'
    + '.weld-comments-title{font-weight:700;font-size:14px;min-width:0;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;}'
    + '.weld-comments-x{border:1px solid var(--border-color,#444);background:var(--input-bg,#222);color:var(--text-color,#eee);border-radius:8px;width:30px;height:30px;cursor:pointer;}'
    + '.weld-comments-layout{display:grid;grid-template-columns:minmax(180px,34%) 1fr;min-height:0;flex:1;}'
    + '.weld-comments-preview{border-right:1px solid var(--border-color,#444);background:var(--input-bg,#151515);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;min-height:0;padding:10px;}'
    + '.weld-comments-preview img{max-width:100%;max-height:100%;object-fit:contain;border-radius:8px;}'
    + '.weld-comments-wrap{position:relative;min-width:0;min-height:0;}'
    + '.weld-comments-frame{width:100%;height:100%;border:none;background:transparent;}'
    + '.weld-comments-loading{position:absolute;inset:0;z-index:2;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;gap:8px;background:var(--background-color,var(--bg-color,#111));color:var(--text-color,#eee);font:13px/1.4 Open Sans,sans-serif;transition:opacity .18s ease;pointer-events:none;}'
    + '.weld-comments-spin{width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:999px;border:2px solid rgba(128,128,128,.35);border-top-color:currentColor;animation:weldCommentsSpin .8s linear infinite;}'
    + '@keyframes weldCommentsSpin{to{transform:rotate(360deg);}}'
    + '@media (max-width:700px){.weld-comments-card{width:calc(100vw - 24px);max-width:calc(100vw - 24px);height:min(720px,calc(100dvh - 32px));}.weld-comments-layout{grid-template-columns:1fr;}.weld-comments-preview{display:none;}}';
  document.head.appendChild(st);
}

function ensureOverlay() {
  if (overlay) return overlay;
  ensureStyle();
  overlay = document.createElement('div');
  overlay.className = 'weld-comments-ov';
  overlay.innerHTML =
    '<div class="weld-comments-card">'
    + '<div class="weld-comments-head"><div class="weld-comments-title" data-title>Comments</div>'
    + '<button class="weld-comments-x" data-close>x</button></div>'
    + '<div class="weld-comments-layout">'
    + '<div class="weld-comments-preview" data-preview><img data-img></div>'
    + '<div class="weld-comments-wrap">'
    + '<div class="weld-comments-loading" data-loading><div class="weld-comments-spin"></div><div>Loading comments...</div></div>'
    + '<iframe class="weld-comments-frame" data-frame allow="clipboard-read *; clipboard-write *"></iframe>'
    + '</div></div></div>';
  overlay.addEventListener('click', function (e) { if (e.target === overlay) close(); });
  overlay.querySelector('[data-close]').addEventListener('click', close);
  var frame = overlay.querySelector('[data-frame]');
  var loading = overlay.querySelector('[data-loading]');
  frame.addEventListener('load', function () {
    loading.style.opacity = '0';
    setTimeout(function () { if (loading.style.opacity === '0') loading.style.display = 'none'; }, 200);
  });
  document.body.appendChild(overlay);
  return overlay;
}

// open(opts):
//   key       (required) anything stable -> derives the channel
//   title     header text
//   image     optional preview image url
//   app       generator slug the thread lives under (default generatorName)
//   theme     'auto' | 'light' | 'dark'
//   prefix    channel prefix (default app)
//   disabled  if true, show a "comments disabled" notice instead
//   config    passthrough to the comments embed (placeholder, submitButtonText,
//             allowBots, adminPasswordHash, ...)
function open(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  if (opts.disabled) { notifyDisabled(); return; }
  if (typeof document === 'undefined') return;
  var app = opts.app || defaultApp();
  var chan = channel(opts.key, opts.prefix || app);
  var cfg = {};
  var base = opts.config || {};
  for (var k in base) cfg[k] = base[k];
  cfg.forceColorScheme = resolveTheme(opts.theme);
  var src = buildSrc(app, chan, cfg);

  var ov = ensureOverlay();
  ov.querySelector('[data-title]').textContent = opts.title || 'Comments';
  var preview = ov.querySelector('[data-preview]');
  var img = ov.querySelector('[data-img]');
  if (opts.image) { preview.style.display = ''; img.src = opts.image; }
  else { preview.style.display = 'none'; }

  var frame = ov.querySelector('[data-frame]');
  var loading = ov.querySelector('[data-loading]');
  ov.style.display = 'flex';
  if (frame.getAttribute('data-src') !== src) {
    loading.style.display = 'flex'; loading.style.opacity = '1';
    frame.setAttribute('data-src', src);
    frame.src = src;
  }
  return chan;
}

function close() { if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none'; }

// inline(target, opts): embed the thread into an element instead of a modal.
function inline(target, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var el = (typeof target === 'string') ? document.querySelector(target) : target;
  if (!el) return null;
  var app = opts.app || defaultApp();
  var chan = channel(opts.key, opts.prefix || app);
  var cfg = {};
  var base = opts.config || {};
  for (var k in base) cfg[k] = base[k];
  cfg.forceColorScheme = resolveTheme(opts.theme);
  var frame = document.createElement('iframe');
  frame.style.cssText = opts.style || 'width:100%;height:100%;border:none;background:transparent;';
  frame.setAttribute('allow', 'clipboard-read *; clipboard-write *');
  frame.src = buildSrc(app, chan, cfg);
  el.appendChild(frame);
  return frame;
}

function notifyDisabled() {
  if (window.weld && window.weld.toast) { window.weld.toast.show('Comments are disabled for this item.', 'info'); return; }
  if (typeof document === 'undefined') return;
  var p = document.createElement('div');
  p.style.cssText = 'z-index:100000;position:fixed;left:50%;bottom:18px;transform:translateX(-50%);max-width:min(360px,calc(100vw - 28px));padding:10px 13px;border-radius:10px;border:1px solid var(--border-color,#444);background:var(--input-bg,#222);color:var(--text-color,#eee);box-shadow:0 8px 28px rgba(0,0,0,.35);font:13px/1.45 Open Sans,sans-serif;opacity:0;transition:opacity .18s ease;pointer-events:none;';
  p.textContent = 'Comments disabled for this item.';
  document.body.appendChild(p);
  requestAnimationFrame(function () { p.style.opacity = '1'; });
  setTimeout(function () { p.style.opacity = '0'; setTimeout(function () { p.remove(); }, 250); }, 2400);
}

// ---- secure datastore: comments-plugin as an append store, optionally
//      end-to-end encrypted (the pattern behind anonymous-inbox apps) ----
var attachedSecret = null;
function attach(deps) { if (deps && deps.secret) attachedSecret = deps.secret; return window.weld.comments; }
function resolveSecret() {
  var sp = attachedSecret || (window.weld && window.weld._secret) || window.secret;
  if (!sp || typeof sp.encrypt !== 'function') throw new Error('weld.comments: secret-plugin not attached -- call weld.comments.attach({ secret: secretPlugin })');
  return sp;
}

var CIPHER_RE = /^ENCRYPTED_[0-9]+_[\s\S]+_ENCRYPTED_END$/;
function isCiphertext(text) { return typeof text === 'string' && CIPHER_RE.test(text); }

function sha256Hex(text) {
  var bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(String(text == null ? '' : text));
  return Promise.resolve(crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', bytes)).then(function (buf) {
    var arr = new Uint8Array(buf), out = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) out += arr[i].toString(16).padStart(2, '0');
    return out;
  });
}

// Public-key crypto helpers (wrap secret-plugin). decrypt() is normalized
// through String() so a boxed-string return can never break === checks.
var cryptoApi = {
  generateKeyPair: function () { var k = resolveSecret().generateKeyPair(); return { publicKey: k.public || k.publicKey, privateKey: k.private || k.privateKey }; },
  encrypt: function (text, publicKey) { return String(resolveSecret().encrypt(String(text), publicKey)); },
  decrypt: function (ciphertext, privateKey) { return String(resolveSecret().decrypt(ciphertext, privateKey)); },
  keyPairMatches: function (publicKey, privateKey) { try { var sp = resolveSecret(), probe = 'weld:' + Date.now() + ':' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2); return String(sp.decrypt(sp.encrypt(probe, publicKey), privateKey)) === probe; } catch (e) { return false; } },
  publicKeyHash: function (publicKey) { return sha256Hex(String(publicKey)); },
  isCiphertext: isCiphertext
};

// Build a comments-plugin channel string with the storage modifiers:
//   channelString(id)                          -> "id+ids:channel"   (inter-channel anonymity)
//   channelString(id, { u: 'name' })           -> "id+u:name,ids:channel"
//   channelString(id, { auth: hash })          -> "id+auth:hash,ids:channel"  (ownership via key)
//   channelString(id, { ids: false })          -> "id"
function channelString(id, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var base = String(id == null ? '' : id), mods = [];
  if (opts.u) mods.push('u:' + String(opts.u).toLowerCase());
  else if (opts.auth) mods.push('auth:' + String(opts.auth));
  if (opts.ids !== false) mods.push('ids:channel');
  return mods.length ? base + '+' + mods.join(',') : base;
}

// store(opts): treat a comments-plugin controller as an append-only store.
//   opts.controller : the comments-plugin controller (submit(); optional
//                     setNicknameForNextComment(), getComments()/comments, onUpdate())
//   opts.keys       : { publicKey, privateKey } -> encrypt on post, decrypt on list
//   opts.anonymous  : post with no nickname (default true)
function store(opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  var ctrl = opts.controller;
  if (!ctrl || typeof ctrl.submit !== 'function') throw new Error('weld.comments.store: a comments-plugin controller with submit() is required');
  var keys = opts.keys || null, anon = opts.anonymous !== false;
  function post(record) {
    var payload = (typeof record === 'string') ? record : JSON.stringify(record);
    if (keys) payload = cryptoApi.encrypt(payload, keys.publicKey);
    var pre = Promise.resolve();
    if (anon && typeof ctrl.setNicknameForNextComment === 'function') pre = Promise.resolve(ctrl.setNicknameForNextComment(''));
    return pre.then(function () { return ctrl.submit(payload); });
  }
  function rawComments() { if (typeof ctrl.getComments === 'function') return ctrl.getComments() || []; if (Array.isArray(ctrl.comments)) return ctrl.comments; return []; }
  function list(o) {
    o = o || {}; var blocked = o.blocked || {}, out = [];
    rawComments().forEach(function (c) {
      if (!c || typeof c.message !== 'string') return;
      var msg = c.message.trim(), uid = (c.user && typeof c.user.id === 'string') ? c.user.id : '';
      if (uid && blocked[uid]) return;
      var value = msg;
      if (keys) { if (!isCiphertext(msg)) return; try { value = cryptoApi.decrypt(msg, keys.privateKey); } catch (e) { return; } }
      if (o.parse !== false) { try { value = JSON.parse(value); } catch (e) {} }
      out.push({ value: value, userId: uid, time: Number((c.time || c.createdAt || 0)), raw: c });
    });
    if (o.sort !== false) out.sort(function (a, b) { return b.time - a.time; });
    return out;
  }
  function onNew(cb) { if (typeof ctrl.onComment === 'function') return ctrl.onComment(cb); if (typeof ctrl.onUpdate === 'function') return ctrl.onUpdate(function () { cb(list()); }); return function () {}; }
  return { post: post, list: list, onNew: onNew, channel: opts.channel || null };
}

window.weld.comments = {
  channel: channel,
  hash: hash,
  buildSrc: buildSrc,
  open: open,
  inline: inline,
  close: close,
  attach: attach,
  crypto: cryptoApi,
  channelString: channelString,
  isCiphertext: isCiphertext,
  store: store,
  version: '1.1.0'
};

return window.weld.comments;
})();

/* chloe-bridge — T0 presence engine (pure logic).
 *
 * Read-only presence: poll a channel, parse messages, build the roster (per-user partitions),
 * speaker ring, channel rhythm, and lastSeen. NO replies, NO moderation — T0 only.
 *
 * This file is the single source of truth for the loop logic. It is deliberately free of GM_*,
 * DOM, and network code: it takes a `transport`, a `store`, and a `clock` as dependencies, so it
 * runs identically under Node (mocks, for tests) and inside the userscript bridge (GM adapters).
 *
 * Data architecture (spec 3): the store is the system of record. Partitions are keyed `u:{authorId}`
 * and are prunable in one operation. The engine holds no durable state of its own — everything that
 * must survive a reload goes through `store`.
 */
(function (root, factory) {
  'use strict';
  var api = factory();
  if (typeof module !== 'undefined' && module.exports) module.exports = api; // Node / harness
  root.ChloeT0 = api;                                                        // userscript / window
})(typeof globalThis !== 'undefined' ? globalThis : this, function () {
  'use strict';

  // ---- snowflake helpers ------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Discord IDs are snowflakes: monotonically increasing, but longer than Number can hold, so
  // compare as BigInt. Ordering by id is the reliable chronological order.
  function snowflakeCmp(a, b) {
    var x = BigInt(a), y = BigInt(b);
    return x < y ? -1 : x > y ? 1 : 0;
  }
  function maxSnowflake(a, b) {
    if (a == null) return b;
    if (b == null) return a;
    return snowflakeCmp(a, b) >= 0 ? a : b;
  }
  // A Discord snowflake encodes its own creation time: (id >> 22) + the Discord epoch. So any message
  // id is an authoritative UTC clock reading from Discord's servers — usable to ground the bot's sense
  // of time and as a fallback when no device clock is being pushed. Returns ms since the Unix epoch.
  var DISCORD_EPOCH = 1420070400000;
  function snowflakeTime(id) {
    try { return Number(BigInt(id) >> 22n) + DISCORD_EPOCH; } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  // ---- engine -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // deps: { transport, store, clock, config, log }
  //   transport.getMessagesAfter(channelId, afterId|null, limit) -> Promise<Array<msg>>
  //     msg = { id, author: { id, username }, content, timestamp }
  //   store.get(key) / set(key, value) / del(key) / listIndex() / setIndex(arr)  (all async-ok)
  //   clock.now() -> ms epoch
  //   config = { channelId, botUserId, recentWindow, speakerRingSize, pollIntervalMs }
  //   log(...)  -> console-like
  function createEngine(deps) {
    var transport = deps.transport;
    var store = deps.store;
    var clock = deps.clock || { now: function () { return Date.now(); } };
    var log = deps.log || function () {};
    var cfg = Object.assign({
      channelId: null,
      botUserId: null,        // drop the bot's own messages by author id
      botName: null,          // for name-addressing ("chloe, ...")
      botAliases: [],         // extra nicknames she answers to (the short form of botName is added automatically)
      recentWindow: 25,       // rolling lines kept per user partition (distilled+window, spec dec #2)
      speakerRingSize: 8,     // last N distinct posters
      pollIntervalMs: 5000,
      onPoll: null,           // optional (summary) -> any; runs after EVERY poll (loop or manual)
      adaptivePolling: true,  // back off when quiet, snap to fast when active (spec 7.10)
      pollFloorMs: 4000,      // fastest cadence (active / pending work)
      pollCeilMs: 30000,      // slowest cadence (long quiet)
      // Pace core (DESIGN-pace.md): one Jacobson rhythm estimator drives debounce, polling, quiet
      // detection, and an AI-cadence floor. Every consumer falls back to its fixed constant when
      // pace is off or too few samples. NO new AI calls.
      adaptivePace: true,
      paceMinSamples: 5,            // need this many gap observations before rhythm drives timing
      paceGapBeta: 0.25,           // deviation EWMA weight (mirrors the brain meter)
      paceDebounceWgap: 0.5,       // debounce ≈ avgGap*Wgap + gapVar*Wdev ...
      paceDebounceWdev: 1.0,
      debounceFloorMs: 800,        // ... clamped: never interrupt-fast (the ceiling is debounceMs itself, see currentDebounce)
      pollAdditiveStepMs: 4000,    // AIMD additive increase per silent poll (default = floor)
      pollBusyCeilMs: 12000,       // busy room: relax polling only PARTWAY to here (passive ingest, still mention-responsive) — not the full pollCeilMs
      paceQuietZ: 3,               // silence counts as "quiet" at this many deviations past typical
      paceMinAIIntervalMs: 90000,  // a background AI pass won't re-run faster than this wall-clock floor (anti cost-multiplier)
      // ---- T1 reply path (all optional; absent => pure T0 read-only) ----
      respond: null,          // async (context) -> { ok, value:text }   (the brain; runs in the generator page)
      send: null,             // async (channelId, text) -> any           (POST to Discord; runs in the userscript)
      addressMode: 'both',    // 'mention' | 'name' | 'both' | 'always' (DM)
      cooldownMs: 8000,       // per-AUTHOR reply cooldown (don't spam the same person)
      globalCooldownMs: 2500, // min gap between ANY two of her sends (lets different people be answered promptly)
      debounceMs: 2500,       // wait for a lull before replying (don't reply mid-burst)
      contextLines: 12,       // recent channel lines handed to the brain (hard upper bound)
      conversationMemory: true,   // give her a TWO-SIDED, legible transcript: include her OWN recent messages (so she sees the back-and-forth she's part of) and resolve <@id>/<#id>/<@&id> refs to readable @names / #channels in what she reads, instead of dropping her turns and stripping every mention. Correctness; off == legacy one-sided view.
      ownLinesMax: 12,        // cap on her own recent messages kept per channel for the transcript
      requestTokenBudget: 5000,// TOTAL tokens per request to the backend — must cover EVERYTHING:
                              // persona + instructions + intention + anti-repeat list + addressed
                              // message + the transcript. The transcript gets whatever's left after
                              // the rest is measured/reserved.
      promptOverheadTokens: 320,// fixed reserve for the page's persona block + instruction scaffolding
                              // (measured: persona ~95 + respond/guidance scaffolding ~200, with margin)
      minTranscriptTokens: 200,// never starve the transcript below this, even if other parts are large

      backgroundText: false,  // when on, the text lane is fire-and-forget (poll loop never blocks on generation)
      keepActionLog: true,    // T4: keep a separate, purge-surviving record of mod actions (decision #5)
      modLogContextLines: 5,  // #11: snapshot of the target's most recent lines captured with each mod action
      typing: null,           // optional async (channelId) -> POST typing; pulsed before a generation
      recapFn: null,          // optional async (ctx) -> { ok, value } channel summary for !chloe recap
      // ---- T5 presence depth ----
      greet: false,                  // opt-in: greet first-ever speakers and long-absent returners
      greetFn: null,                 // async (ctx) -> { ok, value } greeting line from the brain
      greetReturnAfterMs: 172800000, // gap >= 2d counts as "been a while" (shorter gaps stay silent)
      greetCooldownMs: 43200000,     // >=12h between greetings for one person (one per crossing, not per msg)
      greetDebounceMs: 4000,         // settle before greeting (people fire 2-3 lines on arrival)
      greetSettleMs: 60000,          // after Start, don't greet for this long (people already here aren't "arrivals")
      quietAfterMs: 86400000,        // active -> quiet once a user ages out of ~1d of attention
      decayAfterMs: 604800000,       // a return after >=7d quiet decays familiarity (warmth follows recency)
      decayFactor: 0.5,              // interactionCount *= this on a decayed return (never below 0)
      backfill: false,               // one-time: walk history backward to seed the roster
      backfillPageSize: 100, backfillMaxPages: 8,  // bounded + checkpointed; ingest only, never greets/replies
      // On a cold start / after Reset State the cursor is empty, so the first poll pulls a chunk of
      // recent history. Without a clamp, EVERY image request in that backlog fires at once. So on the
      // startup batch, image generation is limited to the few most-recent user messages; normal image
      // handling resumes on every poll after.
      startupImageMax: 5,            // most-recent user messages eligible for image gen on the startup batch
      startupBacklogThreshold: 8,    // a cold-start first poll bigger than this is treated as a history backlog (observe-only)
      maintenanceEveryPolls: 10      // run the quiet-sweep (active->quiet) every Nth poll, not every poll
    }, deps.config || {});
    // globalStore is a top-level dep (the root-prefix store shared across channels). Bind it onto cfg
    // so the helpers that look for it — blockStore() (global blocklist) and the DM public-profile
    // merge — actually find it. Without this it stayed null and blockStore()/merge silently fell back
    // to the per-channel store, so a ban or a public fact never reached secondary/DM engines.
    if (deps.globalStore) cfg.globalStore = deps.globalStore;

    var CURSOR_KEY = 'cursor:' + cfg.channelId;
    var INDEX_KEY = 'roster:index';
    // GDPR / ethereal mode. A user who asks to be forgotten becomes invisible to memory in THIS
    // bucket: no partition, no facts, no roster/summary/episode contribution, no image tracking —
    // but the bot can still reply to them in the moment. Per-context by design: the public bucket
    // (globalStore for any public channel) and each DM bucket hold their own flag, so a user can be
    // ethereal in public while still on the record in a DM, or vice versa. The forget-floor is a
    // per-user timestamp that survives `remember me`, so re-enabling memory never lets backfill or a
    // cold start reach back and re-learn the history they erased.
    var ETHEREAL_KEY = 'ethereal';        // { ids: { id: { at, name } } }  (in etherealStore())
    var FORGETFLOOR_KEY = 'forgetfloor';  // { id: ts }                     (in etherealStore())
    var GOALS_KEY = 'goals';   // goals are USER data: shared across PUBLIC channels, but kept LOCAL to each DM
    var CHARMEM_KEY = 'charmem';   // CROSS-CHANNEL (via globalStore): the installed character's own respooled memories (background context)
    // charmem is the BOT's own character background (operator-authored, not user data), so it lives in
    // globalStore and is identical everywhere. Goals, by contrast, are the user's — so they go through
    // goalStore(): shared across public channels (globalStore) but isolated to the local bucket inside a
    // DM, so a goal set in a DM can NEVER surface in a public channel or in another user's DM. (Same
    // per-context rule as etherealStore.)
    function crossStore() { return cfg.globalStore || store; }
    function goalStore() { return cfg.isDM ? store : (cfg.globalStore || store); }
    var CONSOLIDATE_KEY = 'consolidate:' + cfg.channelId;   // { lastSweepAt, sliceCursor } for the idle “sleep” pass
    var RING_KEY = 'speaker:ring:' + cfg.channelId;
    var RHYTHM_KEY = 'rhythm:' + cfg.channelId;
    var MOOD_KEY = 'mood:' + cfg.channelId;   // G6: decayed room-tenor read (energy + playfulness)
    var CHANSUM_KEY = 'chansum:' + cfg.channelId;   // rolling recursive summary of the channel's arc
    var EPI_KEY = 'epi:' + cfg.channelId;           // episodic memory ring (experiences as events)
    var AFFECT_KEY = 'affect:' + cfg.channelId;     // her own internal state {curiosity, confidence, warmth}
    var WORK_KEY = 'work:' + cfg.channelId;         // volatile cognitive workspace {topic, participants, goal, recentDecisions, mood, at}
    var DELIB_KEY = 'delib:' + cfg.channelId;       // { lastAt } — min-gap floor between deliberations
    var PROC_KEY = 'procmode:' + cfg.channelId;     // active procedural mode { mode, until, by, emoji }
    var POLL_KEY = 'poll:' + cfg.channelId;         // active reaction poll { messageId, question, options, endsAt }
    var INTENT_KEY = 'intent:' + cfg.channelId;   // Sweetie set_goal pattern: a standing intention that
    // survives across polls and rides in every response context, so she holds a thread of purpose
    // ("getting to know the new folks", "keeping it light after that argument") rather than reacting
    // to each message in isolation. The brain may set it; it decays if not reaffirmed.
    var REMIND_KEY = 'reminders:' + cfg.channelId;   // poll-driven scheduled reminders (front-end only,
    // no AI call). Checked each poll rather than via setTimeout, because background tabs throttle
    // timers to ~1/min — a poll-driven check fires reliably on the first poll after the due time.
    var AFK_KEY = 'afk:' + cfg.channelId;   // user-set away state (front-end only, no AI call): set on
    // "!chloe afk", auto-cleared when the person speaks again, surfaced when others ping them.
    var HILITE_KEY = 'highlights:' + cfg.channelId;   // pinned notable messages (front-end only): saved
    // for recall via "!chloe highlights", and a few recent ones ride in context so she can reference
    // the channel's memorable moments — a step toward memory without the full fact-extraction build.
    var REACTTALLY_KEY = 'reacttally:' + cfg.channelId;   // running per-emoji tally of significant reactions
    var BACKFILL_KEY = 'backfill:' + cfg.channelId;
    var BEATS_KEY = 'beats:lastrun:' + cfg.channelId;   // #12: beatId -> last-fired ts (+ __lastAny)
    var FEEDBACK_KEY = 'feedback:' + cfg.channelId;     // DESIGN-feedback: per-channel EWMA over reply-style arms {len,tone}
    var OWNLINE_KEY = 'ownlines:' + cfg.channelId;   // her OWN recent messages (text + ts), captured at ingest from
    // the messages Discord echoes back, so the transcript she reads is two-sided (DESIGN-conversation-memory).
    // Bounded by ownLinesMax. Per-channel; in a DM it lives in the isolated DM bucket.
    var SELFINTENT_KEY = 'selfintents:' + cfg.channelId;   // deferred self-intents: a persistent queue of future
    // INTERNAL actions she scheduled for herself (currently: 'revisit' a deliberation subject). Poll-driven
    // like reminders, but a fired intent never sends — it drives her own later cognition. Per-channel; in a
    // DM it lives in the (isolated) DM bucket. Bounded by selfIntentMax.
    var LULL_KEY = 'lull:' + cfg.channelId;   // last time she filled a silence (lull filler throttle)
    var CHECKIN_KEY = 'checkins:' + cfg.channelId;   // { __last: ts, byUser: { id: {at,count,seenAt} } } — check-in throttle + attempt cap
    var ARCH_INDEX_KEY = 'arch:index:' + cfg.channelId;   // index of archived ("historical friend") user ids
    function archKey(id) { return 'arch:' + cfg.channelId + ':u:' + id; }   // per-user cold storage (never on the hot path)

    var running = false;
    var timer = null;

    // T1 reply state: a per-author queue (latest message per author) so one chatty user can't
    // starve replies to everyone else. A lost queue on reload is acceptable.
    var reply = { queue: {}, replying: false };
    var lastReplyAt = {};                // per-author: when she last replied to that person
    var lastLineId = null;               // most recent non-bot channel message id (forget-that fallback target)
    var lastPollIngested = false;        // activity-aware sweep: did the previous poll bring messages?
    var recentReplies = [];              // G1 anti-repetition: her own last few replies (in-memory, per channel)
    var consecutiveBotTurns = 0;         // bot-loop damper: human-authored messages reset this to 0
    var afkNoticed = {};                 // per-target throttle so an AFK heads-up doesn't repeat each ping
    var afkNoticedKeys = [];             // insertion order, to bound afkNoticed (prevent a slow leak over a long session)
    var lastSawHumanAt = 0;              // when a human last spoke here (observation, always updated)
    function noteAuthorForLoop(isBot) {
      if (isBot) consecutiveBotTurns++;
      else { consecutiveBotTurns = 0; lastSawHumanAt = clock.now(); }
    }
    // Reply probability decays as a channel becomes bot-only chatter, so two bots don't ping-pong
    // forever. 0..botLoopGrace bot turns: full chance. Beyond that, halve per extra turn, floored.
    // A human message resets consecutiveBotTurns, restoring full responsiveness immediately.
    function botLoopReplyChance() {
      var grace = cfg.botLoopGrace, hardStop = cfg.botLoopHardStop;
      if (consecutiveBotTurns <= grace) return 1;
      if (hardStop > 0 && consecutiveBotTurns >= hardStop) return 0;
      var over = consecutiveBotTurns - grace;
      return Math.max(cfg.botLoopFloor, Math.pow(0.5, over));
    }
    function rememberReply(text) {
      var t = String(text || '').trim();
      if (!t) return;
      recentReplies.push(t);
      var keep = cfg.antiRepeatWindow || 5;
      if (recentReplies.length > keep) recentReplies = recentReplies.slice(-keep);
    }
    // Standing intention: the brain may return `intent` alongside its reply text; we persist it
    // (capped + timestamped) so it rides in the next context until reaffirmed or it ages out.
    function setIntent(text) {
      var t = String(text || '').trim().slice(0, cfg.intentMaxLen);
      if (!t) return Promise.resolve(null);
      return Promise.resolve(store.set(INTENT_KEY, { text: t, at: clock.now() })).then(function () { return t; });
    }
    function getIntent() {
      return Promise.resolve(store.get(INTENT_KEY)).then(function (gi) {
        if (gi && gi.text && (clock.now() - (gi.at || 0) < cfg.intentTtlMs)) return gi;
        return null;
      });
    }
    function clearIntent() { return Promise.resolve(store.del(INTENT_KEY)); }

    // ---- goal objects (prospective memory) -------------------------------------------------
    function loadGoals() {
      return Promise.resolve(goalStore().get(GOALS_KEY)).then(function (g) { return Array.isArray(g) ? g : []; });
    }
    function saveGoals(list) {
      // newest-first cap: keep all OPEN goals, evict oldest CLOSED beyond the cap
      if (list.length > (cfg.goalsMax || 40)) {
        var open = list.filter(function (x) { return x.status === 'open'; });
        var closed = list.filter(function (x) { return x.status !== 'open'; }).sort(function (a, b) { return (b.lastTouchedAt || 0) - (a.lastTouchedAt || 0); });
        list = open.concat(closed).slice(0, cfg.goalsMax || 40);
      }
      return Promise.resolve(goalStore().set(GOALS_KEY, list)).then(function () { return list; });
    }
    function addGoal(text, owner, ownerName, source) {
      var t = String(text || '').trim().slice(0, cfg.goalTextMax || 140);
      if (!t) return Promise.resolve(null);
      return loadGoals().then(function (list) {
        var norm = normFact(t);
        var dup = list.filter(function (x) { return x.status === 'open' && x.owner === (owner || null) && normFact(x.text) === norm; })[0];
        if (dup) { dup.lastTouchedAt = clock.now(); return saveGoals(list).then(function () { return dup; }); }
        var g = { id: 'g' + clock.now().toString(36) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000).toString(36),
                  text: t, owner: owner || null, ownerName: ownerName || '', channel: cfg.channelId,
                  createdAt: clock.now(), lastTouchedAt: clock.now(), status: 'open', source: source || 'command' };
        list.push(g);
        return saveGoals(list).then(function () { log('[chloe.goal] noted a goal for ' + (ownerName || 'the channel') + ': \u201c' + t + '\u201d'); return g; });
      });
    }
    function closeGoal(id, byId, status) {
      return loadGoals().then(function (list) {
        var g = list.filter(function (x) { return x.id === id; })[0];
        if (!g) return { ok: false, reason: 'no goal with that id' };
        if (g.owner && byId && g.owner !== byId && !isMod(byId)) return { ok: false, reason: 'only the goal\u2019s owner or a mod can close it' };
        g.status = status || 'done'; g.lastTouchedAt = clock.now();
        return saveGoals(list).then(function () { return { ok: true, goal: g }; });
      });
    }
    function goalsForOwner(ownerId) {
      return loadGoals().then(function (list) {
        var now = clock.now(), changed = false;
        list.forEach(function (g) {   // lazy staleness: open goals untouched too long fade to dropped
          if (g.status === 'open' && (now - (g.lastTouchedAt || g.createdAt || 0)) > (cfg.goalStaleMs || 2592000000)) { g.status = 'dropped'; g.lastTouchedAt = now; changed = true; }
        });
        var out = list.filter(function (g) { return g.status === 'open' && g.owner === ownerId; });
