      keys.addEventListener('change', function(){ e.keys = keys.value.split(',').map(function(s){ return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); persistState(); });
      content.addEventListener('change', function(){ e.content = content.value; persistState(); });
      del.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.lorebook.splice(idx, 1); persistState(); renderLore(); });
      head.appendChild(keys); head.appendChild(del); card.appendChild(head); card.appendChild(content); box.appendChild(card);
    });
  }
  function addLore(){ if (!state.lorebook) state.lorebook = []; state.lorebook.push({ id: 'lore' + Date.now(), keys: [], content: '' }); persistState(); renderLore(); }
  function exportLore(){
    try {
      var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(state.lorebook || [], null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
      var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob); var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = url; a.download = 'chloe-lorebook.json'; document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); a.remove();
      setTimeout(function(){ URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1500); toast('Lorebook exported', 'success');
    } catch(e){}
  }
  function normalizeLore(obj){
    function mk(keys, content){ return { id: 'lore' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 5), keys: (Array.isArray(keys) ? keys : String(keys || '').split(',')).map(function(k){ return String(k).trim(); }).filter(Boolean), content: String(content || '').trim() }; }
    if (Array.isArray(obj)) return obj.map(function(e){ return mk(e.keys || e.key, e.content || e.text); }).filter(function(e){ return e.content; });
    if (obj && obj.entries && typeof obj.entries === 'object'){   // SillyTavern / AICC world-info shape
      return Object.keys(obj.entries).map(function(k){ var en = obj.entries[k] || {}; return mk(en.key || en.keys, en.content); }).filter(function(e){ return e.content; });
    }
    return [];
  }
  function importLore(file){
    var r = new FileReader();
    r.onload = function(){
      try {
        var arr = normalizeLore(JSON.parse(r.result));
        if (!arr.length){ toast('No lore entries found in that file', 'error'); return; }
        state.lorebook = (state.lorebook || []).concat(arr); persistState(); renderLore(); toast(arr.length + ' lore ' + (arr.length === 1 ? 'entry' : 'entries') + ' imported', 'success');
      } catch(e){ toast('That didn\u2019t look like a lorebook', 'error'); }
    };
    r.readAsText(file);
  }

  function renderInjList(){
    var box = byId('injList'); if (!box) return;
    while (box.firstChild) box.removeChild(box.firstChild);
    var list = state.injections || [];
    if (!list.length){ var e = document.createElement('div'); e.className='note'; e.textContent='Nothing yet — only the live date/time above.'; box.appendChild(e); return; }
    list.forEach(function(it, idx){
      var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className='memrow';
      var t = document.createElement('div'); t.className='mt'; t.textContent = it.text;
      var x = document.createElement('button'); x.className='forget'; x.title='Remove'; x.textContent='\u00d7';
      x.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.injections.splice(idx,1); persistState(); refreshClock(); renderInjList(); });
      row.appendChild(t); row.appendChild(x); box.appendChild(row);
    });
  }
  // Pre-create the user partition so memories + "about you" work from the very first moment (the
  // engine's ingest uses `if (!p)`, so it augments this rather than overwriting it).
  function ensureUserPartitionIn(st){
    return st.get('u:'+USER_ID).then(function(p){
      if (p){ if (state.userName && p.name !== state.userName){ p.name = state.userName; return st.set('u:'+USER_ID, p); } return; }
      var now = Date.now();
      return st.set('u:'+USER_ID, { id: USER_ID, name: state.userName||'You', firstSeen: now, lastSeen: now, interactionCount: 0, state:'active', lifecycle:'quiet', recent: [], facts: [] });
    });
  }
  function ensureUserPartition(){ return ensureUserPartitionIn(store); }
  function renderFactList(){
    var box = byId('factList'); var eng = viewEngine(); if (!box || !eng || !eng.getFacts) return;
    Promise.resolve(eng.getFacts(USER_ID)).then(function(facts){
      while (box.firstChild) box.removeChild(box.firstChild);
      if (!facts || !facts.length){ var e=document.createElement('div'); e.className='note'; e.textContent='Nothing yet \u2014 memories build as you talk.'; box.appendChild(e); return; }
      facts.slice().reverse().forEach(function(f){
        var row=document.createElement('div'); row.className='memrow';
        var t=document.createElement('div'); t.className='mt'; t.textContent=f.text;
        if (f.source==='operator'){ var pin=document.createElement('span'); pin.className='pin'; pin.textContent='pinned'; t.appendChild(pin); }
        var x=document.createElement('button'); x.className='forget'; x.title='Forget this'; x.textContent='\u00d7';
        x.addEventListener('click', function(){ Promise.resolve(eng.forgetFact(USER_ID, f.text)).then(renderFactList); });
        row.appendChild(t); row.appendChild(x); box.appendChild(row);
      });
    });
  }
  // surface the structures the engine builds — not just raw facts
  function renderInnerState(){
    var box = byId('innerState'); var eng = viewEngine(), st = viewStore(); if (!box || !eng) return;
    function txt(v){ return String(v == null ? '' : v); }
    function section(label, items, empty){
      var sec = document.createElement('div'); sec.style.cssText = 'margin:10px 0 2px';
      var h = document.createElement('div'); h.textContent = label; h.style.cssText = 'font-size:11px;letter-spacing:.06em;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--accent-ink);margin-bottom:4px';
      sec.appendChild(h);
      if (!items || !items.length){ var e = document.createElement('div'); e.className = 'note'; e.textContent = empty; sec.appendChild(e); }
      else items.forEach(function(it){ var r = document.createElement('div'); r.style.cssText = 'font-size:13px;color:var(--ink);padding:3px 0'; r.textContent = it; sec.appendChild(r); });
      return sec;
    }
    var get = function(fn, arg){ try { return fn ? Promise.resolve(fn(arg)) : Promise.resolve(null); } catch(e){ return Promise.resolve(null); } };
    Promise.all([
      get(st.get, 'mood:' + CH),
      get(eng.getPersonaNote),
      get(eng.getMemory, USER_ID),
      get(eng.goalsForOwner, USER_ID),
      get(eng.getSelfIntents)
    ]).then(function(r){
      var mood = r[0], persona = r[1], mem = r[2], goals = r[3], intents = r[4];
      while (box.firstChild) box.removeChild(box.firstChild);
      var moodStr = (mood && eng.moodDescriptor) ? eng.moodDescriptor(mood) : '';
      box.appendChild(section('Mood', moodStr ? ['Feeling ' + moodStr + ' right now.'] : [], 'Still settling — mood forms as you talk.'));
      box.appendChild(section('Self-image', persona ? [txt(persona)] : [], 'No self-note yet.'));
      var insights = (mem && mem.insights || []).map(function(x){ return txt(x.text); });
      box.appendChild(section('Conclusions about you', insights, 'No standing conclusions yet \u2014 just facts so far.'));
      var goalTexts = (goals || []).map(function(g){ return txt(g.text); });
      box.appendChild(section('To follow up on', goalTexts, 'Nothing on the list yet.'));
      var now = Date.now();
      var pend = (intents || []).map(function(it){
        var subj = it.subject ? (' \u2014 ' + txt(it.subject)) : '';
        var when = (it.dueAt && it.dueAt > now) ? (' (in ~' + Math.max(1, Math.round((it.dueAt - now) / 60000)) + ' min)') : '';
        return txt(it.kind) + subj + when;
      });
      box.appendChild(section('Planning to revisit', pend, 'Nothing queued to come back to.'));
    });
  }

  /* ---- LocalTransport: the chat is the message stream ---- */
  function snow(ms){ return String((BigInt(ms - SNOW_EPOCH) << 22n) + BigInt((snowSeq++) % 4096)); }
  function snowCmp(a,b){ var A=BigInt(a),B=BigInt(b); return A<B?-1:(A>B?1:0); }
  var queue = loadQueue();
  function loadQueue(){ try { var v = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(NS+'__queue__')); return Array.isArray(v)?v:[]; } catch(e){ return []; } }
  function persistQueue(){ try { localStorage.setItem(NS+'__queue__', JSON.stringify(queue.slice(-400))); } catch(e){} }
  var transport = {
    getMessagesAfter: function(chId, afterId, limit){
      var out = queue.filter(function(m){ return !afterId || snowCmp(m.id, afterId) > 0; });
      return Promise.resolve(out.slice(0, limit || 50));
    },
    getMessagesBefore: function(){ return Promise.resolve([]); }
  };
  function enqueue(authorId, name, bot, text){
    var ms = Date.now(); var m = { id: snow(ms), channelId: CH, author: { id: authorId, username: name, bot: !!bot }, content: text, timestamp: new Date(ms).toISOString() };
    queue.push(m); persistQueue();
    if (isGroup()) { try { planTurn(m); } catch(e){} }   // decide who may answer this beat (no-op when solo)
    return m;
  }

  /* ---- image relay: the brain's paint() triggers window.paintImage(req); this runs the real
   *      text-to-image plugin in THIS panel (the same scope where ai-text's broker attaches) and
   *      posts the result back on window.__chloePaint by reqId. A top-panel root.paintImage relay,
   *      if present, takes precedence (grabPaintImage checks root first). No DSL paste required:
   *      the only top-panel setup is importing the two plugins. Standalone (no plugin) -> SVG demo. ---- */
  /* ---- content moderation (weld.banlist pattern): banned phrases (substring + * wildcard) and,
     when weld.banlist is imported, a content-rating ceiling too. Default off; gates image prompts. ---- */
  var Moderation = (function(){
    function weldList(){
      try {
        if (window.weld && window.weld.banlist && window.weld.banlist.create){
          var m = state.moderation || {};
          return window.weld.banlist.create({ phrases: m.phrases || [], negativePhrases: [], users: [], rating: m.rating || 'x' });
        }
      } catch(e){}
      return null;
    }
    function checkText(text){
      var m = state.moderation; if (!m || !m.enabled) return { ok: true };
      var list = weldList();
      if (list && list.check){ var r = list.check(String(text || '')); return (r && r.ok === false) ? { ok: false, reason: (r.reason || r.matched || 'blocked') } : { ok: true }; }
      var t = String(text || '').toLowerCase();
      var phrases = m.phrases || [];
      for (var i = 0; i < phrases.length; i++){
        var p = String(phrases[i] || '').trim().toLowerCase(); if (!p) continue;
        var hit = p.indexOf('*') >= 0
          ? new RegExp(p.replace(/[.+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&').replace(/\*/g, '.*'), 'i').test(t)
          : t.indexOf(p) >= 0;
        if (hit) return { ok: false, reason: 'blocked term: ' + p };
      }
      return { ok: true };
    }
    return { checkText: checkText };
  })();

  function installPainter(){
    if (window.paintImage) return;   // a top-panel / pre-existing relay wins
    window.paintImage = function(req){
      try { if (!window.__chloePaint) window.__chloePaint = new Map(); } catch(e){ return; }
      var reqId = req && req.reqId;
      var mod = Moderation.checkText(req && req.prompt);
      if (!mod.ok){ try { window.__chloePaint.set(reqId, { ok:false, reason: mod.reason }); } catch(e){} return; }   // content gate
      var t2i = null;
      try { if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root && typeof root.textToImagePlugin === 'function') t2i = root.textToImagePlugin; } catch(e){}
      if (!t2i){ try { if (typeof window.textToImagePlugin === 'function') t2i = window.textToImagePlugin; } catch(e){} }
      if (!t2i){
        // no image plugin available (opened as a plain file): a labelled placeholder so the flow is visible
        var d = String(req && req.resolution || '512x512').split('x'), w = +d[0]||512, h = +d[1]||512;
        var label = String(req && req.prompt || '').replace(/[<&]/g,' ').slice(0,48);
        var svg = '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="'+w+'" height="'+h+'"><defs><linearGradient id="g" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="1"><stop offset="0" stop-color="#4B477E"/><stop offset="1" stop-color="#A14A34"/></linearGradient></defs><rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="url(#g)"/><text x="50%" y="48%" fill="#fff" font-family="Tahoma" font-size="20" text-anchor="middle">demo image</text><text x="50%" y="56%" fill="#ffffffcc" font-family="Tahoma" font-size="13" text-anchor="middle">'+label+'</text></svg>';
        window.__chloePaint.set(reqId, { ok:true, dataUrl:'data:image/svg+xml;base64,' + btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(svg))) });
        return;
      }
      var opts = { prompt: String(req && req.prompt || ''), resolution: req.resolution || '768x768' };
      if (req.guidanceScale != null) opts.guidanceScale = req.guidanceScale;
      if (req.removeBackground) opts.removeBackground = true;
      // canonical: await the result -> boxed String with .dataUrl (canvas.toDataURL). Let the plugin
      // inject its own broker iframe into document.body (await mode) so onFinish resolves.
      try {
        Promise.resolve(t2i(opts)).then(function(out){
          var data = (out && out.dataUrl != null) ? String(out.dataUrl)
                   : (out && out.url != null) ? String(out.url) : '';
          window.__chloePaint.set(reqId, data ? { ok:true, dataUrl:data } : { ok:false, reason:'the image plugin returned no image data' });
        }, function(e){ window.__chloePaint.set(reqId, { ok:false, reason:String((e && e.message) || e) || 'image generation failed' }); });
      } catch(e){ window.__chloePaint.set(reqId, { ok:false, reason:String((e && e.message) || e) || 'image generation failed' }); }
    };
    try { if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root && typeof root === 'object' && !root.paintImage) root.paintImage = window.paintImage; } catch(e){}
  }

  /* ---- exact tokenization: the ai-text plugin exposes countTokens via getMetaObject. Wiring it lets
   *      the engine budget context by real tokens instead of its chars/4 fallback (AICC parity). ---- */
  var pageCountTokens = null, pageMaxContextTokens = null;
  function wireTokenizer(){
    var ai = null; try { ai = window.aiTextPlugin || (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root && root.aiTextPlugin); } catch(e){}
    if (typeof ai !== 'function') return;
    try {
      var meta = ai({ getMetaObject: true });
      if (meta && typeof meta.countTokens === 'function'){ pageCountTokens = meta.countTokens; }
      if (meta && typeof meta.idealMaxContextTokens === 'number'){ pageMaxContextTokens = meta.idealMaxContextTokens; }
    } catch(e){}
  }

  /* ---- brain hooks: real aiTextPlugin on Perchance; a candid mock when opened standalone ---- */
  function installMockIfNeeded(){
    var has = false;
    try { has = !!(window.aiTextPlugin || (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.aiTextPlugin)); } catch(e){}
    if (has) { setText('herRole', 'a companion who remembers'); return; }
    setText('herRole', 'demo mode — no language model connected');
    // standalone: let the brain's root.* lookups resolve to window so the mock ai-text is found.
    try { if (typeof window.root === 'undefined') window.root = window; } catch(e){}
    var lines = [
      "I'm here, though I'm running in demo mode — there's no language model wired in yet. Drop this onto a Perchance page with the ai-text plugin and I'll answer for real.",
      "Noted. (Demo mode: I can hold the conversation and remember it, but my words are placeholders until a model is connected.)",
      "I'm following along. On Perchance, with the free ai-text plugin, this is where my real reply would be.",
      "Got it. Watch the mind panel — even in demo mode the thinking is real; only the words are stand-ins."
    ];
    var n = 0;
    window.aiTextPlugin = function(opts){
      var instr = String(opts && opts.instruction || '');
      var sw = String(opts && opts.startWith || '');
      // ---- structured cognitive passes: keep the loop running and visible ----
      if (/"action"\s*:/.test(instr)) return Promise.resolve('"action":"reply","confidence":0.9,"emoji":""'); // judge
      if (/JSON array of question strings/i.test(instr))                    // decompose -> show the think pipeline
        return Promise.resolve('["What\'s the heart of it?","What would change my view?","What\'s the next small step?"]');
      if (/Answer this one question|thinking quietly to yourself/i.test(instr)) // subanswer
        return Promise.resolve('A small consideration: it depends on what matters most here.');
      if (/"type":\s*"insight\|goal\|none"|tag it: "insight"/i.test(instr) || (sw === '{' && /synthesi|recompose|one or two sentences/i.test(instr)))
        return Promise.resolve('"text":"a quiet realisation worth keeping in mind","type":"insight"'); // reduce
      if (/durable facts|notable episodes|JSON array/i.test(instr)) return Promise.resolve('[]'); // facts/episodes/arrays
      if (/running summary|brief summary of what/i.test(instr)) return Promise.resolve('They have been getting acquainted; nothing major yet.');
      if (/tidying your memory|consolidating memories/i.test(instr)) return Promise.resolve('[]');
      if (sw === '{') return Promise.resolve('{}');
      if (sw === '[') return Promise.resolve('[]');
      // ---- conversational (respond / greet / lull / checkin / beat / recap) ----
      var m = instr.match(/Recent conversation:\n([\s\S]*?)\n\n/);
      var lastUser = ''; if (m){ var ls = m[1].trim().split('\n'); lastUser = (ls[ls.length-1]||'').replace(/^[^:]+:\s*/, ''); }
      var reply = lines[(n++) % lines.length];
      if (lastUser) reply = '“' + lastUser.slice(0,80) + '” — ' + reply;
      return Promise.resolve(reply);
    };
  }

  /* ---- streaming: her conversational replies appear token-by-token, finalized on send ----
     Conversational handlers (respond/greet/lull/checkin/beat/recap) are the ONLY ai-text calls with
     an empty startWith; every cognitive pass uses '[' or '{'. So an empty startWith is a safe gate. */
  var liveWrap = null, liveBody = null, liveText = '', liveActive = false, replyExpected = false;
  function herName(){ return state.botName || 'Chloe'; }
  function dropLiveOrphan(){ if (liveWrap && liveWrap.parentNode && liveWrap.__pending){ liveWrap.parentNode.removeChild(liveWrap); } liveWrap = null; liveBody = null; liveText = ''; }
  function beginLiveReply(){ dropLiveOrphan(); liveActive = true; }
  function ensureLiveBubble(){
    if (liveWrap) return;
    liveWrap = renderMessage('her', herName(), '', { streaming:true }); liveWrap.__pending = true;
    liveBody = liveWrap.querySelector('.body');
    try { byId('typingRow').classList.remove('on'); } catch(e){}   // words are arriving — the dots are redundant now
  }
  function updateLiveReply(t){ ensureLiveBubble(); liveText = t; if (liveBody) liveBody.textContent = t; scrollThread(false); }
  function finalizeLiveReply(finalText){
    if (!liveWrap) return false;
    if (liveBody) setBody(liveBody, finalText, true);
    liveWrap.classList.remove('streaming'); liveWrap.__pending = false;
    attachFeedback(liveWrap, finalText);
    applyEmotionCue(liveWrap, finalText);
    liveWrap = null; liveBody = null; liveText = ''; liveActive = false;
    scrollThread(false);
    return true;
  }
  // wrap whichever ai-text handle the brain will actually reach for (root first, then window)
  function wrapAiForStreaming(){
    var holders = [];
    try { if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root && typeof root.aiTextPlugin === 'function') holders.push(root); } catch(e){}
    try { if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && typeof window.aiTextPlugin === 'function' && holders.indexOf(window) < 0) holders.push(window); } catch(e){}
    holders.forEach(function(h){
      var base = h.aiTextPlugin; if (base.__streamWrapped) return;
      var wrapped = function(opts){
        // a reply uses an explicit empty startWith (''); cognitive passes either omit startWith
        // (undefined — e.g. channelSummary) or use '[' / '{'. Only '' may stream into chat.
        var conversational = opts && opts.startWith === '' && !opts.getMetaObject && !isGroup();
        if (!conversational || !replyExpected) return base(opts);   // only a real reply ever opens a chat bubble (and only solo streams)
        beginLiveReply();
        var o = {}; for (var k in opts) if (opts.hasOwnProperty(k)) o[k] = opts[k];
        var userChunk = opts.onChunk;
        o.onChunk = function(c){
          try {
            if (!(c && c.isFromStartWith)){
              var full = (c && c.fullTextSoFar != null) ? String(c.fullTextSoFar)
                       : (c && c.textChunk != null) ? (liveText + String(c.textChunk)) : null;
              if (full != null) updateLiveReply(full);
            }
          } catch(e){}
          if (typeof userChunk === 'function'){ try { userChunk(c); } catch(e){} }
        };
        return base(o);
      };
      wrapped.__streamWrapped = true; h.aiTextPlugin = wrapped;
    });
  }

  /* ---- send + typing: render her into the thread ---- */
  function scrubTokens(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/<@!?&?[0-9a-z_-]+>\s*/gi, '').replace(/<#[0-9a-z_-]+>/gi, '').replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ').trim(); }
  function soloSend(chId, body){
    setThinking(false);
    var text = scrubTokens(body);   // strip any leftover <@id>/<#id> tokens (reminders can carry one)
    if (text){
      enqueue(BOT_ID, herName(), true, text);
      if (!(liveActive && finalizeLiveReply(text))){ var w = renderMessage('her', herName(), text); if (w){ w.setAttribute('data-cid', BOT_ID); if (isGroup() || state.botColor) styleSpeaker(w, BOT_ID, state.herAvatar); } }
    }
    liveActive = false; replyExpected = false;
    return Promise.resolve(true);
  }
  function soloTyping(){ if (engineThinking) byId('typingRow').classList.add('on'); return Promise.resolve(true); }
  // she paints -> render the image in the thread (and note it for conversation memory)
  /* ---- image gallery: persist every generated image in IndexedDB and browse it.
     Mirrors Davie's weld.gallery (a `blobs` store keyed by id + a `meta` manifest);
     prefers the real weld-gallery-plugin if it's imported on the page, else the inlined store. ---- */
  var Gallery = (function(){
    var DB = 'chloe-solo-gallery', BLOBS = 'blobs', META = 'meta', MAX = 300;
    var weld = (window.weld && window.weld.gallery && window.weld.gallery.create)
      ? window.weld.gallery.create({ dbName: DB, maxItems: MAX }) : null;
    var manifest = [], dbP = null, ready = null;
    function openDb(){
      if (dbP) return dbP;
      dbP = new Promise(function(res, rej){
        var r = indexedDB.open(DB, 1);
        r.onupgradeneeded = function(e){ var db = e.target.result;
          if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(BLOBS)) db.createObjectStore(BLOBS);
          if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(META)) db.createObjectStore(META); };
        r.onsuccess = function(e){ res(e.target.result); };
        r.onerror = function(e){ dbP = null; rej(e.target.error); };
      });
      return dbP;
    }
    function op(store, mode, fn){ return openDb().then(function(db){ return new Promise(function(res, rej){
      var tx = db.transaction(store, mode), s = tx.objectStore(store), q = fn(s);
      if (q && 'onsuccess' in q){ q.onsuccess = function(){ res(q.result); }; q.onerror = function(){ rej(q.error); }; }
      else { tx.oncomplete = function(){ res(); }; tx.onerror = function(){ rej(tx.error); }; }
    }); }); }
    function uid(){ return 'img_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6); }
    function saveMan(){ return op(META, 'readwrite', function(s){ return s.put(manifest, 'manifest'); }); }
    function loadMan(){ return op(META, 'readonly', function(s){ return s.get('manifest'); }).then(function(m){ manifest = m || []; return manifest; }); }
    function init(){ if (ready) return ready; ready = weld ? Promise.resolve(weld.init()) : loadMan(); return ready; }
    function store(blob, meta){
      meta = meta || {};
      if (weld) return Promise.resolve(weld.store(blob, meta));
      var entry = { id: uid(), prompt: meta.prompt || '', resolution: meta.resolution || null, createdAt: Date.now(), favorited: false };
      return op(BLOBS, 'readwrite', function(s){ return s.put(blob, entry.id); }).then(function(){
        while (manifest.length >= MAX){ var i = manifest.findIndex(function(e){ return !e.favorited; }); if (i < 0) i = 0;
          var rm = manifest.splice(i, 1)[0]; op(BLOBS, 'readwrite', function(s){ return s.delete(rm.id); }).catch(function(){}); }
        manifest.push(entry); return saveMan();
      }).then(function(){ return entry.id; });
    }
    function getManifest(){ return weld ? Promise.resolve(weld.getManifest()) : Promise.resolve(manifest.slice()); }
    function getBlobUrl(id){ if (weld) return Promise.resolve(weld.getBlobUrl(id));
      return op(BLOBS, 'readonly', function(s){ return s.get(id); }).then(function(b){ return b ? URL.createObjectURL(b) : null; }); }
    function toggleFavorite(id){ if (weld) return Promise.resolve(weld.toggleFavorite(id));
      var e = manifest.filter(function(x){ return x.id === id; })[0]; if (!e) return Promise.resolve(null);
      e.favorited = !e.favorited; return saveMan().then(function(){ return e.favorited; }); }
    function remove(id){ if (weld) return Promise.resolve(weld.remove(id));
      manifest = manifest.filter(function(e){ return e.id !== id; });
      return Promise.all([ op(BLOBS, 'readwrite', function(s){ return s.delete(id); }).catch(function(){}), saveMan() ]).then(function(){ return true; }); }
    function clear(){ if (weld) return Promise.resolve(weld.clear());
      manifest = []; return Promise.all([ op(BLOBS, 'readwrite', function(s){ return s.clear(); }), saveMan() ]); }
    return { init:init, store:store, getManifest:getManifest, getBlobUrl:getBlobUrl, toggleFavorite:toggleFavorite, remove:remove, clear:clear, usingWeld:function(){ return !!weld; } };
  })();

  /* ---- Save/Load: rolling auto-checkpoints + manual saves, each a full snapshot of the session.
   * A snapshot is every chloeSolo: localStorage key (memory of every character, the cast, the transcript,
   * all settings). Restore writes them back and reloads — a clean, total rollback. Kept in IndexedDB so
   * many large saves fit. ---- */
  var Saves = (function(){
    var DB = 'chloe-solo-saves', SLOTS = 'slots', dbP = null;
    function openDb(){
      if (dbP) return dbP;
      dbP = new Promise(function(res, rej){
        var r = indexedDB.open(DB, 1);
        r.onupgradeneeded = function(e){ var db = e.target.result; if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(SLOTS)) db.createObjectStore(SLOTS, { keyPath:'id' }); };
        r.onsuccess = function(e){ res(e.target.result); };
        r.onerror = function(e){ dbP = null; rej(e.target.error); };
      });
      return dbP;
    }
    function op(mode, fn){ return openDb().then(function(db){ return new Promise(function(res, rej){
      var tx = db.transaction(SLOTS, mode), s = tx.objectStore(SLOTS), q = fn(s);
      if (q && 'onsuccess' in q){ q.onsuccess = function(){ res(q.result); }; q.onerror = function(){ rej(q.error); }; }
      else { tx.oncomplete = function(){ res(); }; tx.onerror = function(){ rej(tx.error); }; }
    }); }); }
    return {
      list: function(){ return op('readonly', function(s){ return s.getAll(); }).then(function(a){ return sortSlotsNewestFirst(a || []); }); },
      put:  function(slot){ return op('readwrite', function(s){ return s.put(slot); }); },
      del:  function(id){ return op('readwrite', function(s){ return s.delete(id); }); },
      get:  function(id){ return op('readonly', function(s){ return s.get(id); }); }
    };
  })();
  // pure helpers (unit-tested): newest-first ordering, and which auto-saves to drop past the keep-count.
  function sortSlotsNewestFirst(a){ return a.slice().sort(function(x, y){ return (y.ts || 0) - (x.ts || 0); }); }
  function autosToPrune(all, keep){ var autos = sortSlotsNewestFirst(all.filter(function(s){ return s.kind === 'auto'; })); return autos.slice(Math.max(1, keep || 1)).map(function(s){ return s.id; }); }

  function snapshotNS(){ var d = {}; try { for (var i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++){ var k = localStorage.key(i); if (k && k.indexOf(NS) === 0) d[k] = localStorage.getItem(k); } } catch(e){} return d; }
  function makeSlot(kind, label){ return { id: kind.charAt(0) + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 5), kind: kind, label: String(label || '').slice(0, 80), ts: Date.now(), msgCount: (queue ? queue.length : 0), version: SOLO_VERSION, data: snapshotNS() }; }
  function saveSlot(kind, label){ var slot = makeSlot(kind, label); return Saves.put(slot).then(function(){ return (kind === 'auto') ? pruneAuto().then(function(){ return slot; }) : slot; }); }
  function pruneAuto(){ return Saves.list().then(function(all){ return Promise.all(autosToPrune(all, state.autoSaveKeep || 10).map(function(id){ return Saves.del(id); })); }); }
  function restoreSlot(id){
    return Saves.get(id).then(function(slot){
      if (!slot || !slot.data) return false;
      var del = []; try { for (var i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++){ var k = localStorage.key(i); if (k && k.indexOf(NS) === 0) del.push(k); } } catch(e){}
      del.forEach(function(k){ try { localStorage.removeItem(k); } catch(e){} });
      Object.keys(slot.data).forEach(function(k){ try { localStorage.setItem(k, slot.data[k]); } catch(e){} });
      location.reload(); return true;
    });
  }
  var autoTimer = null, lastAutoCount = -1;
  function startAutoSave(){
    if (autoTimer){ clearInterval(autoTimer); autoTimer = null; }
    if (!state.autoSave) return;
    var mins = Math.max(1, state.autoSaveMins || 10);
    autoTimer = setInterval(function(){
      if (!queue || queue.length === lastAutoCount) return;   // skip if nothing new since the last checkpoint
      lastAutoCount = queue.length;
      saveSlot('auto').then(function(){ if (byId('savesBg') && byId('savesBg').classList.contains('open')) renderSaves(); }).catch(function(){});
    }, mins * 60 * 1000);
  }
  function dataUrlToBlob(dataUrl){
    try {
      var parts = String(dataUrl).split(','); var head = parts[0] || '', b64 = parts[1] || '';
      var mime = (head.match(/data:([^;]+)/) || [])[1] || 'image/png';
      var bin = atob(b64), n = bin.length, u8 = new Uint8Array(n);
      while (n--) u8[n] = bin.charCodeAt(n);
      return new Blob([u8], { type: mime });
    } catch(e){ return null; }
  }
  function extractPrompt(caption){ var m = String(caption || '').match(/[\u201c"]([^\u201d"]+)[\u201d"]/); return m ? m[1] : ''; }
  function persistImage(dataUrl, caption){
    var d = String(dataUrl || '');
    if (d.indexOf('data:image/') !== 0 || d.indexOf('data:image/svg') === 0) return;   // real raster generations only — skip SVG demo placeholders
    var blob = dataUrlToBlob(dataUrl); if (!blob) return;
    Gallery.init().then(function(){ return Gallery.store(blob, { prompt: extractPrompt(caption) }); })
      .then(function(){ toast('Saved to gallery', 'success'); if (galleryOpen) renderGallery(); }).catch(function(){});
  }

  function soloSendImage(chId, dataUrl, caption){
    setThinking(false);
    dropLiveOrphan();   // an image reply isn't streamed text; clear any half-open text bubble
    renderMessage('her', herName(), String(caption||''), { image: dataUrl });
    enqueue(BOT_ID, herName(), true, caption ? String(caption) : '(shared an image)');
    persistImage(dataUrl, caption);   // -> IndexedDB gallery
    liveActive = false; replyExpected = false;
    return Promise.resolve(true);
  }

  /* ---- the engine, built from current state; rebuilt on config change ---- */
  var engine = null, engineThinking = false;
  // the COMPLETE brain — every hook the engine calls, names exactly as the engine reads them.
  function brainHooks(){ return {
    respond: respond, judge: judge, paint: paint, recapFn: recap, editPrompt: editPrompt,
    factFn: facts, summaryFn: channelSummary, episodeFn: episodes,
    reflectFn: reflect, consolidateFn: consolidate,
    // deliberation map-reduce: decompose -> map(answer each) -> reduce(synthesise)
    decomposeFn: decompose, subAnswerFn: subanswer, reduceFn: reduce,
    mapFn: function(list){ return Promise.all((list||[]).map(function(job){ return Promise.resolve(subanswer(job)); })); },
    // self-initiated / ambient "react" behaviours
    greetFn: greet, lullFn: lull, checkinFn: checkin, beatFn: beat
  }; }
  function buildConfig(co, coStore){
    var cfg = Object.assign({
      channelId: CH, botUserId: BOT_ID, botName: state.botName || 'Chloe', isDM: true, engageMode: 'open',
      botVersion: SOLO_VERSION,
      // pacing limited ONLY by Perchance's generate latency — no artificial waits anywhere
      pollFloorMs: 100, pollCeilMs: 700, debounceMs: 0, debounceFloorMs: 0, cooldownMs: 0, globalCooldownMs: 0, adaptivePace: true, adaptivePolling: true,
      typingRefreshMs: 4000,
      // ---- image generation: answer image requests + paint on its own ----
      image: true, sendImage: soloSendImage, imageCooldownMs: 0, imageQueueMax: 4, imageMemory: state.imageMemory !== false, imageMemoryRing: 12,
      // ---- no Discord surface: no commands, moderation, @-pings, #-channels, reactions ----
      commandPrefix: null, ackCommands: false, backgroundText: false, volunteer: false,
      reactionTracking: false, reactionSummon: false, reactionAutoHighlight: false, archiveStale: false,
      // ---- single instance: runLock would block polling for its TTL after a refresh (a stale lock from
      //      the prior load); replyResume can't verify without a recentFetch. Both off. ----
      runLock: false, replyResume: false,
      // ---- the full cognitive loop — defaults on, switchable from the Behavior tab ----
      conversationMemory: state.conversationMemory !== false, selfKnowledge: state.selfKnowledge !== false,
      factMemory: state.factMemory !== false, reflection: state.reflection !== false,
      episodicMemory: state.episodicMemory !== false, channelSummary: state.channelSummary !== false,
      episodeGraph: state.episodeGraph !== false,   // connect related memories ("...reminds me of when...")
      cleanOutput: true,    // tidy her replies at the seams (stray name-tags, cut-offs, unclosed code blocks, stutters)
      idleConsolidation: state.idleConsolidation !== false, idleDeliberation: state.idleDeliberation !== false, deferredIntents: true,
      goalObjects: state.goalObjects !== false, attentionManager: state.attentionManager !== false, workingMemory: state.workingMemory !== false,
      ownAffect: state.ownAffect !== false, moodAware: state.moodAware !== false, timeAware: true, proceduralModes: true, relationshipTrust: state.relationshipTrust !== false,
      contradictionAware: state.contradictionAware, userModeling: state.userModeling,
      feedbackLearning: state.feedbackLearning, semanticRecall: state.semanticRecall,
      character: state.character || null,
      // ---- browser hookup: she knows the real local date/time/timezone/language ----
      timeAware: true, deviceTime: true, deviceClockStaleMs: 600000,
      timezoneOffsetMins: browserContext().offsetMins, deviceClock: deviceClockOf(browserContext()),
      semanticInjections: buildInjections(),
      // ---- chat is reply + image only: her self-initiated SPEECH (greet/lull/checkin) would post to the
      //      thread unprompted, so it stays off. Her self-initiated THINKING (deliberate/dream/plan) is
      //      unaffected and shows in the mind drawer. beats empty, volunteer off (set below). ----
      greet: false, lullFiller: false, checkins: false, beats: [],
      // ---- constant idle churn: she think/dream/plans continuously while you read or pause, each pass
      //      paced only by Perchance's generate latency (no artificial min-interval between passes) ----
      factEveryPolls: 2, episodeEveryPolls: 3, channelSummaryEveryPolls: 3, reflectionEveryPolls: 4,
      consolidateEveryPolls: 4, maintenanceEveryPolls: 5,
      deliberateMinGapMs: 0, selfIntentRevisitMs: 15000, volunteerCooldownMs: 8000,
      paceQuietZ: 1.2, deliberateCuriosityFloor: 0.4, deliberateCuriosityDrop: 0.07,   // keeps her thinking in sustained bursts while idle
      consolidateIdleMs: 2500,                                    // ~2.5s of quiet already counts as idle -> churn begins
      paceMinAIIntervalMs: 0,                                     // NO throttle between background passes — constant churn
      factMinInteractions: 2, factProposeGapMs: 8000, factProposeMinNew: 2, consolidateMinFacts: 3,  // learn quickly in a 1:1
      // exact token accounting when the page tokenizer is available (else the engine uses chars/4)
      countTokens: pageCountTokens || undefined,
      // operator style dials (kindness/sarcasm/curiosity/playfulness/formality/verbosity), 0..1, 0.5 = neutral
      personality: state.personality || undefined,
      lullPatienceMs: 45000, lullMinGapMs: 120000,                 // break a silence after ~45s, at most ~1/2min
      checkinGapMs: 180000, checkinPerUserGapMs: 180000,           // a check-in at most ~1/3min
      greetCooldownMs: 5000,                                       // greet when you first arrive / return
      // transport + scheduler
      send: soloSend, typing: soloTyping, defer: function(fn,ms){ return setTimeout(fn, ms||0); },
      recentFetch: function(n){ return transport.getMessagesAfter(CH, null, n||12); }
    }, brainHooks());
    // primary always carries the director hook (a no-op when solo). Extras override identity + send +
    // memory so each is its own character on its own store, reading the same shared transcript.
    cfg.engageDecide = engageDecideFor(co ? co.id : BOT_ID);
    if (co){
      cfg.botUserId = co.id; cfg.botName = co.name; cfg.isDM = false; cfg.addressMode = 'name'; cfg.engageMode = 'normal';
      cfg.character = { name: co.name, instruction: co.instruction || '', avatar: co.avatar || '' };
      cfg.send = makeSendFor(co); cfg.sendImage = undefined; cfg.image = false;   // extras are text-only for now
      cfg.greet = false; cfg.lullFiller = false; cfg.checkins = false;            // only the primary may break silence
    }
    return cfg;
  }
  /* ---- multi-character scene: a cast of engines over the one shared transcript ----
   * The primary character is the existing `engine` on the legacy store (so Chloe carries her memory).
   * Each active extra gets its own namespaced store + engine; all read the same `queue`. A director
   * decides who speaks per beat via the engine's cfg.engageDecide hook, so they never all answer at once.
   * Solo (no active extras) is byte-for-byte the old behavior: engageDecide returns undefined -> normal. */
  var extraEngines = {};                                  // id -> { engine, store, char }
  var turnPlan = { content: null, allowed: {}, depth: 0 };
  function activeExtras(){ return (state.cast || []).filter(function(c){ return c && c.active !== false; }); }
  function botInScene(){ return state.botActive !== false; }   // the default character can be taken out of the cast
  function activeMembers(){                                     // unified scene roster: default character (if present) + active extras
    var out = [];
    if (botInScene()) out.push({ id: BOT_ID, name: herName(), aliases: state.botAliases || [], isBot: true });
    activeExtras().forEach(function(c){ out.push({ id: c.id, name: c.name, aliases: c.aliases || [], isBot: false, ref: c }); });
    return out;
  }
  function primaryIdEff(){                                      // who answers when no one is named; survives removals
    var act = activeMembers();
    if (state.primaryId && act.some(function(m){ return m.id === state.primaryId; })) return state.primaryId;
    return act.length ? act[0].id : BOT_ID;
  }
  function isGroup(){ return activeMembers().length > 1 || !botInScene(); }
  // Titles aren't names — so "Doctor Vane" answers to "Vane", not to "the doctor said…".
  var NAME_TITLES = { doctor:1, dr:1, captain:1, capt:1, mr:1, mrs:1, ms:1, miss:1, lady:1, lord:1, sir:1, madam:1, madame:1, professor:1, prof:1, master:1, mistress:1, the:1, king:1, queen:1, prince:1, princess:1, saint:1, st:1, general:1, commander:1, agent:1, officer:1 };
  // The names a character answers to: their full name, their personal name (first word that isn't a
  // title), and any explicit aliases. Used for BOTH @mentions and bare-name scanning.
  function nameTokens(name, aliases){
    var full = String(name || '').trim(); if (!full) return [];
    var out = [full], words = full.split(/\s+/), personal = null;
    for (var i = 0; i < words.length; i++){ if (!NAME_TITLES[words[i].toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '')]){ personal = words[i]; break; } }
    if (personal && personal.length >= 2 && personal.toLowerCase() !== full.toLowerCase()) out.push(personal);
    (aliases || []).forEach(function(a){ a = String(a || '').trim(); if (a) out.push(a); });
    var seen = {}, dedup = []; out.forEach(function(t){ var k = t.toLowerCase(); if (!seen[k]){ seen[k] = 1; dedup.push(t); } });
    return dedup;
  }
  function castRoster(){
    var pid = primaryIdEff();
    return activeMembers().map(function(m){ return { id: m.id, name: m.name, primary: m.id === pid, tokens: nameTokens(m.name, m.aliases) }; });
  }
  function namedIn(text, name){ try { return new RegExp('(^|[^a-z0-9_])' + name.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '([^a-z0-9_]|$)', 'i').test(String(text || '')); } catch(e){ return false; } }
  // Addressed if @-mentioned (<@id>) OR any of their names appears in the text (@Aria and bare "Aria"
  // both land, since the leading @ is just a non-word boundary in namedIn).
  function addressedBy(content, member){
    var c = String(content || '');
    if (member.id && c.indexOf('<@' + member.id + '>') >= 0) return true;
    var toks = member.tokens || nameTokens(member.name, member.aliases);
    return toks.some(function(t){ return namedIn(c, t); });
  }
  // recompute who may answer THIS message. Human turn: addressed characters, else the primary. A
  // character's turn: bounded follow-up only if it named someone (so chains end and control returns to you).
  function planTurn(msg){
    var roster = castRoster(), fromHuman = !(msg.author && msg.author.bot), content = String(msg.content || ''), allowed = {};
    var named = roster.filter(function(r){ return r.id !== msg.author.id && addressedBy(content, r); });
    var maxSp = Math.max(1, state.castMaxSpeakers || 2);
    if (fromHuman){
      turnPlan.depth = 0;
      if (named.length) named.slice(0, maxSp).forEach(function(r){ allowed[r.id] = 1; });
      else allowed[primaryIdEff()] = 1;                   // unaddressed -> the primary (your always-on companion)
    } else {
      if (turnPlan.depth < (state.castMaxFollowups || 2) && named.length){
        turnPlan.depth++;
        named.slice(0, maxSp).forEach(function(r){ allowed[r.id] = 1; });
      }
    }
    turnPlan = { content: content, allowed: allowed, depth: turnPlan.depth };
  }
  function engageDecideFor(charId){
    return function(content){
      if (charId === BOT_ID && !botInScene()) return false;   // default character removed -> stays silent
      if (!isGroup()) return undefined;                   // sole companion -> fall through to normal addressing
      if (String(content || '') !== turnPlan.content) return false;   // only ever answer the latest planned beat
      return !!turnPlan.allowed[charId];
    };
  }
  // a stable, readable color per character (so a 3-way scene is followable at a glance)
  var CAST_PALETTE = ['#2E7DD1', '#2E9E7B', '#C0562B', '#8A5BD0', '#B8902A', '#C2417A', '#3C8C8C', '#6B7A2E', '#5B62E0', '#A23E8C'];
  function castColor(seed){ var h = 0; seed = String(seed || ''); for (var i = 0; i < seed.length; i++) h = (h * 31 + seed.charCodeAt(i)) >>> 0; return CAST_PALETTE[h % CAST_PALETTE.length]; }
  function styleSpeaker(wrap, cid, avatar){
    if (!wrap) return;
    var color = colorFor(cid);   // user override -> auto palette -> default accent (primary)
    wrap.classList.add('hascolor');
    wrap.style.setProperty('--speaker', color || 'var(--accent-ink)');
    var who = wrap.querySelector('.who'); if (who) who.style.color = color || '';
    if (avatar && who && !who.querySelector('.spk-av')){ var img = document.createElement('img'); img.className = 'spk-av'; img.src = avatar; img.alt = ''; who.insertBefore(img, who.firstChild); }
  }
  function makeSendFor(c){
    return function(chId, body){
      setThinking(false);
      var text = scrubTokens(body);
      if (text){ enqueue(c.id, c.name, true, text); var w = renderMessage('her', c.name, text); if (w){ w.setAttribute('data-cid', c.id); styleSpeaker(w, c.id, c.avatar); } }
      return Promise.resolve(true);
    };
  }
  // which character's memory the views inspect (session-only; resets to the primary). Each character
  // keeps its own memory store, so this selects which store the fact/state/budget views read from.
  var memViewId = BOT_ID;
  function viewEngine(){ var e = extraEngines[memViewId]; return (memViewId && memViewId !== BOT_ID && e) ? e.engine : engine; }
  function viewStore(){ var e = extraEngines[memViewId]; return (memViewId && memViewId !== BOT_ID && e) ? e.store : store; }
  function viewChar(){ return (memViewId === BOT_ID) ? (state.character || null) : ((state.cast || []).filter(function(x){ return x.id === memViewId; })[0] || null); }
  function viewName(){ var c = viewChar(); return (memViewId === BOT_ID) ? herName() : (c ? c.name : herName()); }
  function buildEngine(){
    if (engine && engine.stop) { try { engine.stop(); } catch(e){} }
    Object.keys(extraEngines).forEach(function(id){ var e = extraEngines[id]; if (e && e.engine && e.engine.stop) { try { e.engine.stop(); } catch(x){} } });
    extraEngines = {};
    engine = ChloeT0.createEngine({ transport: transport, store: store, clock: { now: Date.now }, log: onEngineLog, config: buildConfig() });
    registerLorebook(engine);
    if (botInScene()) engine.start();   // built for internal reads, but dormant when the default character is removed
    activeExtras().forEach(function(c){
      try {
        var st = makeStore(NS + 'c:' + c.id + ':');
        var ex = ChloeT0.createEngine({ transport: transport, store: st, clock: { now: Date.now }, log: function(){}, config: buildConfig(c, st) });
        registerLorebook(ex);
        ensureUserPartitionIn(st);   // so this character can remember you from the first message
        ex.start();
        extraEngines[c.id] = { engine: ex, store: st, char: c };
      } catch(e){ pushThought('[scene] could not start ' + (c && c.name) + ': ' + (e && e.message)); }
    });
    if (!activeMembers().some(function(m){ return m.id === memViewId; })) memViewId = primaryIdEff();   // don't strand the memory view on a removed character
  }
  function slugId(name){ return 'c-' + String(name || 'char').toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').slice(0, 24) + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6); }
  function addToScene(ch){
    if (!ch || !ch.name) return false;
    if (!state.cast) state.cast = [];
    state.cast.push({ id: slugId(ch.name), name: String(ch.name).slice(0, 60), instruction: String(ch.instruction || '').slice(0, 8000), avatar: String(ch.avatar || ''), active: true });
    persistState(); buildEngine(); renderRoster(); updateCharLabel();
    toast(ch.name + ' joined the scene', 'success');
    return true;
  }
  function renderRoster(){
    var box = byId('rosterList'); if (!box) return; box.innerHTML = '';
    var pid = primaryIdEff(), activeCount = activeMembers().length;
    function avatarEl(name, color, src){
      if (src){ var im = document.createElement('img'); im.className = 'roster-av'; im.src = src; im.alt = ''; return im; }
      var d = document.createElement('div'); d.className = 'roster-av'; d.textContent = (String(name || '?').trim()[0] || '?').toUpperCase(); if (color) d.style.background = color; return d;
    }
    function refreshAll(){ persistState(); buildEngine(); renderRoster(); renderMemPicker(); updateCharLabel(); }
    function row(m){   // m: { id, name, isBot, ref(extra) }
      var color = colorFor(m.id);
      var src = m.isBot ? (state.herAvatar || (state.character && state.character.avatar) || '') : (m.ref.avatar || '');
      var isActive = m.isBot ? true : (m.ref.active !== false);
      var r = document.createElement('div'); r.className = 'roster-row' + (isActive ? '' : ' off');
      var top = document.createElement('div'); top.className = 'roster-top';
      top.appendChild(avatarEl(m.name, color, src));
      var n = document.createElement('input'); n.type = 'text'; n.className = 'roster-name-in'; n.value = m.name; if (color) n.style.color = color;
      n.title = 'Rename';
      n.addEventListener('change', function(){ var v = n.value.trim(); if (!v){ n.value = m.name; return; } if (m.isBot) state.botName = v; else m.ref.name = v; refreshAll(); });
      top.appendChild(n);
      if (m.id === pid){ var tag = document.createElement('span'); tag.className = 'roster-tag'; tag.textContent = 'primary'; tag.title = 'Answers when you don\u2019t name anyone'; top.appendChild(tag); }
      else { var mp = document.createElement('button'); mp.className = 'roster-mp'; mp.textContent = 'Make primary'; mp.title = 'Answers when you don\u2019t name anyone';
        mp.addEventListener('click', function(){ if (!m.isBot) m.ref.active = true; state.primaryId = m.id; refreshAll(); toast(m.name + ' now leads the scene', 'success'); });
        top.appendChild(mp); }
      var del = document.createElement('button'); del.className = 'roster-del'; del.textContent = '\u2715';
      var canRemove = activeCount > 1 || !isActive;   // never leave the scene with nobody in it
      del.disabled = !canRemove; del.title = canRemove ? (m.isBot ? 'Take the default character out of the scene' : 'Remove this character') : 'Add or enable another character first';
      del.addEventListener('click', function(){
        if (!canRemove) return;
        if (m.isBot) state.botActive = false;
        else { var i = state.cast.indexOf(m.ref); if (i >= 0) state.cast.splice(i, 1); }
        if (state.primaryId === m.id) state.primaryId = null;   // primaryIdEff() picks a new lead
        refreshAll(); toast(m.name + ' left the scene');
      });
      top.appendChild(del);
      r.appendChild(top);
      var ctrls = document.createElement('div'); ctrls.className = 'roster-ctrls';
      if (!m.isBot){
        var lab = document.createElement('label'); lab.className = 'roster-act';
        var cb = document.createElement('input'); cb.type = 'checkbox'; cb.checked = isActive;
        cb.addEventListener('change', function(){ m.ref.active = cb.checked; if (!cb.checked && state.primaryId === m.id) state.primaryId = null; refreshAll(); });
        lab.appendChild(cb); lab.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' in scene')); ctrls.appendChild(lab);
      }
      var cw = document.createElement('label'); cw.className = 'roster-color-wrap';
      var ci = document.createElement('input'); ci.type = 'color'; ci.className = 'roster-color'; ci.title = 'Highlight colour';
      ci.value = colorFor(m.id) || (m.isBot ? (state.accent || '#5B62E0') : castColor(m.id));
      ci.addEventListener('input', function(){ if (m.isBot) state.botColor = ci.value; else m.ref.color = ci.value; persistState(); recolorMessages(); renderMemPicker(); });
      cw.appendChild(ci); cw.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' colour')); ctrls.appendChild(cw);
      var al = document.createElement('input'); al.type = 'text'; al.className = 'roster-alias'; al.placeholder = 'also answers to\u2026 (comma-separated)';
      al.value = (m.isBot ? (state.botAliases || []) : (m.ref.aliases || [])).join(', ');
      al.addEventListener('change', function(){ var arr = al.value.split(',').map(function(s){ return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); if (m.isBot) state.botAliases = arr; else m.ref.aliases = arr; persistState(); buildEngine(); });
      ctrls.appendChild(al);
      r.appendChild(ctrls);
      box.appendChild(r);
    }
    if (botInScene()) row({ id: BOT_ID, name: herName(), isBot: true });
    (state.cast || []).forEach(function(c){ row({ id: c.id, name: c.name, isBot: false, ref: c }); });
    if (!botInScene()){
      var rr = document.createElement('div'); rr.className = 'roster-restore';
      var s = document.createElement('span'); s.textContent = 'The default character is out of the scene.'; rr.appendChild(s);
      var b = document.createElement('button'); b.className = 'btn'; b.textContent = 'Bring back ' + (state.botName || 'Chloe');
      b.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.botActive = true; persistState(); buildEngine(); renderRoster(); renderMemPicker(); updateCharLabel(); });
      rr.appendChild(b); box.appendChild(rr);
    }
    var ms = byId('castMaxSpeakers'), mf = byId('castMaxFollowups');
    if (ms){ ms.value = state.castMaxSpeakers || 2; if (!ms.__w){ ms.__w = 1; ms.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.castMaxSpeakers = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, parseInt(ms.value, 10) || 2)); persistState(); }); } }
    if (mf){ mf.value = (state.castMaxFollowups == null ? 2 : state.castMaxFollowups); if (!mf.__w){ mf.__w = 1; mf.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.castMaxFollowups = Math.max(0, Math.min(6, parseInt(mf.value, 10) || 0)); persistState(); }); } }
  }
  function refreshMemViews(){ renderFactList(); renderInnerState(); renderContextBudget(); }
  function renderMemPicker(){
    var card = byId('memViewCard'), box = byId('memPicker');
    if (!isGroup()){ memViewId = BOT_ID; if (card) card.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    if (!activeMembers().some(function(m){ return m.id === memViewId; })) memViewId = primaryIdEff();   // viewed character left the scene
    if (card) card.style.display = '';
    if (!box) return; box.innerHTML = '';
    var roster = activeMembers().map(function(m){ return { id: m.id, name: m.name }; });
    roster.forEach(function(m){
      var b = document.createElement('button'); b.className = 'mempick' + (m.id === memViewId ? ' on' : ''); b.textContent = m.name;
      b.style.setProperty('--speaker', colorFor(m.id) || 'var(--accent-ink)');
      b.addEventListener('click', function(){ memViewId = m.id; renderMemPicker(); refreshMemViews(); });
      box.appendChild(b);
    });
  }
  // context provider so matched entries ride the same budgeted injection path as everything else.
  function registerLorebook(eng){
    if (!eng || typeof eng.registerProvider !== 'function') return;
    var band = (eng.BANDS && eng.BANDS.SITUATION != null) ? eng.BANDS.SITUATION : 50;
    eng.registerProvider({
      id: 'lorebook',
      priority: band,
      enabled: function(){ return Array.isArray(state.lorebook) && state.lorebook.length > 0; },
      gather: function(g){
        var entries = state.lorebook || []; if (!entries.length) return null;
        var parts = [];
        if (g && g.p && g.p.content) parts.push(String(g.p.content));
        if (g && g.lines && g.lines.length) parts.push(g.lines.slice(-6).join(' '));
        var scan = parts.join(' ').toLowerCase(); if (!scan) return null;
        var hits = [];
        entries.forEach(function(e){
          var keys = loreKeysArr(e).map(function(k){ return k.toLowerCase(); });
          if (!keys.length || !e.content) return;
          if (keys.some(function(k){ return scan.indexOf(k) >= 0; })) hits.push(String(e.content).trim());
        });
        if (!hits.length) return null;
        var text = ('Relevant background (use only if it fits naturally; never recite it): ' + hits.join(' ')).slice(0, 1400);
        return { text: text, tokens: (eng.estimateTokens ? eng.estimateTokens(text) : Math.ceil(text.length / 4)) };
      }
    });
  }
  function applyConfig(patch){ Object.assign(state, patch); persistState(); buildEngine(); }

  /* ---- call() shim: the AICC importer talks to the engine through this ---- */
  function call(method, args){
    args = args || {};
    if (method === 'config.setCharacter'){
      if (args.name == null){ state.character = null; state.botName = 'Chloe'; }
      else {
        state.character = { name: String(args.name).slice(0,80), instruction: String(args.instruction||'').slice(0,8000), avatar: String(args.avatar||'').slice(0,2000) };
        state.botName = state.character.name;                 // re-theme: she becomes this character everywhere
        if (state.character.avatar) state.herAvatar = state.character.avatar;
      }
      persistState(); buildEngine(); updateCharLabel();
      toast(state.character ? ('Now chatting as ' + state.character.name) : 'Reset to default Chloe', 'success');
      var bn = byId('botNameInput'); if (bn) bn.value = state.botName;   // reflect into the Behavior field
      if (Array.isArray(args.initialMessages) && args.initialMessages.length) seedOpeningMessages(args.initialMessages);
      return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, value: { character: state.character ? { name: state.character.name } : null } });
    }
    if (method === 'character.seedMemories'){
      var mems = Array.isArray(args.memories) ? args.memories : [];
      if (!engine || !mems.length) return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, value: { seeded: 0 } });
      return Promise.resolve(engine.seedCharacterMemories(String(args.name||'this character'), mems)).then(function(nn){ return { ok:true, value:{ seeded: nn } }; });
    }
    return Promise.resolve({ ok: false, reason: 'unknown method ' + method });
  }
  /* an imported AICC character can carry initialMessages (its opening). Render + enqueue them so she
   * greets in-character on import, and so the opening rides into her context on the next poll. */
  function seedOpeningMessages(list){
    (list || []).forEach(function(m){
      var author = String((m && (m.author || m.role)) || 'ai').toLowerCase();
      var content = String((m && (m.content || m.message || m.text)) || '').trim();
      if (!content) return;
      if (author === 'ai' || author === 'assistant' || author === 'bot' || author === 'char' || author === 'character'){
        renderMessage('her', herName(), content); enqueue(BOT_ID, herName(), true, content);
      } else if (author === 'system'){ renderSystemLine(content); }
      else { renderMessage('you', userNameStr(), content); enqueue(USER_ID, userNameStr(), false, content); }
    });
    scrollThread(true);
  }
  function updateCharLabel(){ var nm = state.botName || 'Chloe'; setText('charCurrent', state.character ? state.character.name : 'default Chloe'); setText('herName', nm); setText('aboutTitle', nm + ' Solo');
    try { document.title = nm + ' Solo'; } catch(e){}
    var img = byId('herAvatar'); var av = state.herAvatar || (state.character && state.character.avatar);
    if (img){ if (av){ img.src = av; img.style.display = ''; } else { img.style.display = 'none'; } }
  }

  /* ---- the mind drawer: a throttled thought stream (the signature feature) ---- */
  var streamEl, lastIdle = true;
  /* auto-scroll that pauses when the user scrolls up, with a jump-to-latest pill */
  function makeSticky(scrollEl, btn){
    var stuck = true;
    function near(){ return (scrollEl.scrollHeight - scrollEl.scrollTop - scrollEl.clientHeight) < 80; }
    scrollEl.addEventListener('scroll', function(){ stuck = near(); if (stuck && btn) btn.classList.remove('show'); });
    function jump(){ scrollEl.scrollTop = scrollEl.scrollHeight; stuck = true; if (btn) btn.classList.remove('show'); }
    if (btn) btn.addEventListener('click', jump);
    return { notify: function(){ if (stuck) scrollEl.scrollTop = scrollEl.scrollHeight; else if (btn) btn.classList.add('show'); }, jump: jump };
  }
  var threadScroller = null, mindScroller = null;
  function scrollThread(force){ if (!threadScroller){ try { byId('thread').scrollTop = byId('thread').scrollHeight; } catch(e){} return; } force ? threadScroller.jump() : threadScroller.notify(); }
  function scrollMind(){ if (!mindScroller){ try { streamEl.scrollTop = streamEl.scrollHeight; } catch(e){} return; } mindScroller.notify(); }
  function onEngineLog(line){ pushThought(String(line)); }
  function pushThought(line){
    line = String(line);
    // routine poll ticks are transport heartbeat, not cognition — they'd bury the real thoughts.
    if (/^\[chloe\.T0\]\s*poll(?!\s*error)/.test(line)) return;
    renderThought(line);
  }
  var CATMAP = { ctx:'cog', T0:'flow', T1:'flow', T2:'flow', T3:'flow', tok:'cog', lock:'flow', poll:'io',
    fact:'mem', episode:'mem', mem:'mem', summary:'mem', goal:'mem', trust:'mem', reflect:'mem', consolidate:'mem', semantic:'mem',
    persona:'cog', character:'cog', think:'cog', affect:'cog', mood:'cog', intent:'cog', feedback:'cog',
    mode:'flow', work:'flow', remind:'io', greet:'io', lull:'io', checkin:'io', note:'page' };
  function renderThought(line){
    if (!streamEl) return;
    if (lastIdle){ streamEl.innerHTML = ''; lastIdle = false; }
    var tag = 'page', txt = line, m = String(line).match(/^\[chloe\.?([a-zA-Z0-9]*)\]\s*([\s\S]*)$/);
    if (m){ tag = m[1] || 'flow'; txt = m[2]; }
    var cls = CATMAP[tag] || 'flow';
    var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'thought';
    var t = document.createElement('span'); t.className = 'tag ' + cls; t.textContent = tag || '·';
    var x = document.createElement('span'); x.className = 'txt'; x.textContent = txt;
    row.appendChild(t); row.appendChild(x); streamEl.appendChild(row);
    while (streamEl.children.length > 400) streamEl.removeChild(streamEl.firstChild);
    scrollMind();
  }

  /* ---- chat rendering ---- */
  var threadCol, emptyState;
  function setThinking(on){ engineThinking = on; byId('pulse').classList.toggle('on', on); byId('mindTab').classList.toggle('thinking', on); if (!on) byId('typingRow').classList.remove('on'); }
  /* ---- markdown rendering for her replies (weld.markdown if imported, else a safe inline subset) ----
     Escape-first, URL-sanitized (only http/https/mailto; javascript:/data: neutered). Mirrors the
     weld.markdown surface: bold/italic/strike, inline code, fenced code, links, images, lists,
     blockquotes, h1-h3. No raw HTML pass-through. ---- */
  function mdEsc(s){ return String(s).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
  function mdSafeUrl(u){ u = String(u||'').trim(); return /^(https?:|mailto:)/i.test(u) ? u : (u.indexOf(':') < 0 ? u : '#'); }
  function mdInline(s){
    var codes = []; s = s.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, function(_, c){ codes.push(c); return '\u0001C' + (codes.length - 1) + '\u0001'; });
    s = s.replace(/!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)\s]+)\)/g, function(_, alt, u){ return '<img src="' + mdSafeUrl(u) + '" alt="' + alt + '">'; });
    s = s.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)\s]+)\)/g, function(_, t, u){ return '<a href="' + mdSafeUrl(u) + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">' + t + '</a>'; });
    s = s.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>').replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
    s = s.replace(/(^|[^*])\*([^*\n]+)\*(?!\*)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>').replace(/(^|[^_])_([^_\n]+)_(?!_)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>');
    s = s.replace(/~~([^~]+)~~/g, '<del>$1</del>');
    s = s.replace(/\u0001C(\d+)\u0001/g, function(_, i){ return '<code>' + codes[+i] + '</code>'; });
    return s;
  }
  function mdFallback(src){
    src = String(src).replace(/\r\n?/g, '\n');
    var blocks = []; src = src.replace(/```([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(_, c){ blocks.push(c.replace(/^\n/, '')); return '\u0001B' + (blocks.length - 1) + '\u0001'; });
    var lines = src.split('\n'), out = [], i = 0;
    function list(tag, items){ if (items.length) out.push('<' + tag + '>' + items.map(function(x){ return '<li>' + mdInline(mdEsc(x)) + '</li>'; }).join('') + '</' + tag + '>'); }
    while (i < lines.length){
      var ln = lines[i];
      if (/^\u0001B\d+\u0001$/.test(ln.trim())){ out.push('<pre><code>' + mdEsc(blocks[+ln.trim().replace(/[\u0001B]/g, '')]) + '</code></pre>'); i++; continue; }
      var h = ln.match(/^(#{1,3})\s+(.*)$/); if (h){ out.push('<h' + h[1].length + '>' + mdInline(mdEsc(h[2])) + '</h' + h[1].length + '>'); i++; continue; }
      if (/^\s*>\s?/.test(ln)){ var q = []; while (i < lines.length && /^\s*>\s?/.test(lines[i])){ q.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*>\s?/, '')); i++; } out.push('<blockquote>' + mdInline(mdEsc(q.join(' '))) + '</blockquote>'); continue; }
      if (/^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(ln)){ var ul = []; while (i < lines.length && /^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(lines[i])){ ul.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*[-*+]\s+/, '')); i++; } list('ul', ul); continue; }
      if (/^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(ln)){ var ol = []; while (i < lines.length && /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(lines[i])){ ol.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/, '')); i++; } list('ol', ol); continue; }
      if (ln.trim() === ''){ i++; continue; }
      var para = []; while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim() !== '' && !/^\s*[-*+]\s+|^\s*\d+\.\s+|^\s*>\s?|^#{1,3}\s+|^\u0001B\d+\u0001$/.test(lines[i])){ para.push(lines[i]); i++; }
      out.push('<p>' + mdInline(mdEsc(para.join('\n'))).replace(/\n/g, '<br>') + '</p>');
    }
    return out.join('');
  }
  function mdRender(src){
    src = String(src == null ? '' : src);
    try { if (window.weld && window.weld.markdown && window.weld.markdown.render) return window.weld.markdown.render(src); } catch(e){}
    return mdFallback(src);
  }
  function setBody(el, text, rich){ if (rich){ el.innerHTML = mdRender(text); } else { el.textContent = text; } }
  // Emotion cue: infer the character's mood from their own words and show a small glyph by their name.
  // Recency wins (the last feeling in a reply dominates), longer phrases break ties, and a few
  // punctuation tells override. Display-only — it never touches what they say.
  var EMOTION_KEYWORDS = {
    happy: 'happy,joy,smile,smiles,smiling,playful,grin,grins,grinning,laugh,laughs,laughing,laughter,giggle,giggles,giggling,haha,hehe,yay,excited,delight,delighted,beaming,thrilled,glad,hug,cuddle,adore,chuckle,chuckles,chuckling,:D,^_^',
    sad: 'sad,sadness,sob,sobs,sobbing,weep,weeping,tears,teary,cry,cries,crying,gloomy,grief,whimper,whimpering,lonely,heartbreak,devastated,miserable,melancholy,mourning,hollow,downcast',
    mischief: 'mischief,mischievous,naughty,tease,teases,teasing,smirk,smirks,smirking,sly,cheeky,prank,flirt,flirty,flirting,smug,plotting,scheming,wink,winks,winking,seductive,snicker',
    surprise: 'surprise,surprised,shock,shocked,gasp,gasps,gasping,wow,whoa,stunned,amazed,astonished,bewildered,wide-eyed',
    embarrassed: 'embarrass,embarrassed,embarrassing,shy,blush,blushes,blushing,flush,flushed,awkward,nervous,stutter,mortified,flustered,bashful,stammer,stammering',
    angry: 'angry,mad,rage,raging,furious,fury,hiss,glare,glares,glaring,snarl,snarling,irritated,irritation,livid,irate,seething,scowl,scowls,scowling,hostile'
  };
  var EMOTION_CUE = { happy:['\uD83D\uDE0A','happy'], sad:['\uD83D\uDE41','a little down'], mischief:['\uD83D\uDE0F','playful'], surprise:['\uD83D\uDE2E','surprised'], embarrassed:['\uD83D\uDE33','flustered'], angry:['\uD83D\uDE20','irritated'] };
  function detectEmotion(text){
    if (!text) return null;
    var best = null, maxIndex = -1, maxLen = 0;
    Object.keys(EMOTION_KEYWORDS).forEach(function(emotion){
      var words = EMOTION_KEYWORDS[emotion].split(',').map(function(w){ return w.trim(); }).filter(Boolean);
      if (!words.length) return;
      var safe = words.map(function(w){ return w.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&'); });
      var pattern = new RegExp('(^|[^a-zA-Z0-9_])(' + safe.join('|') + ')(?![a-zA-Z0-9_])', 'gi'), m;
      while ((m = pattern.exec(text)) !== null){
        var len = m[2].length;
        if (m.index > maxIndex){ maxIndex = m.index; best = emotion; maxLen = len; }
        else if (m.index === maxIndex && len > maxLen){ best = emotion; maxLen = len; }
      }
    });
    var symbols = { '?!':'surprise', '!?':'surprise', '~':'mischief' };
    Object.keys(symbols).forEach(function(sym){ var idx = text.lastIndexOf(sym); if (idx > maxIndex){ maxIndex = idx; best = symbols[sym]; } });
    return best;
  }
  function applyEmotionCue(wrap, text){
    if (!wrap) return;
    var who = wrap.querySelector('.who'); if (!who) return;
    var old = who.querySelector('.emocue'); if (old) old.parentNode.removeChild(old);
    if (state.showEmotion === false) return;
    var emo = detectEmotion(String(text || '')); if (!emo || !EMOTION_CUE[emo]) return;
    var span = document.createElement('span'); span.className = 'emocue'; span.textContent = ' ' + EMOTION_CUE[emo][0]; span.title = 'she seems ' + EMOTION_CUE[emo][1];
    who.appendChild(span);
  }
  function refreshEmotionCues(){
    if (!threadCol) return;
    var msgs = threadCol.querySelectorAll('.msg.her');
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(msgs, function(wrap){
      if (wrap.querySelector('.avatar')) return;   // image messages have no spoken text to read
      var body = wrap.querySelector('.body'); applyEmotionCue(wrap, body ? (body.textContent || '') : '');
    });
  }

  function renderMessage(role, who, text, opts){
    if (emptyState && emptyState.parentNode){ emptyState.parentNode.removeChild(emptyState); emptyState = null; }
    var roleCls = role === 'her' ? 'her' : (role === 'system' ? 'system' : 'you');
    var wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'msg ' + roleCls + ((opts && opts.nar) ? ' nar' : '') + ((opts && opts.streaming) ? ' streaming' : '');
    var w = document.createElement('div'); w.className = 'who'; w.textContent = who; wrap.appendChild(w);
    var b = document.createElement('div'); b.className = 'body'; setBody(b, text, role === 'her' && !(opts && opts.image)); wrap.appendChild(b);
    if (opts && opts.image){ var im = document.createElement('img'); im.className = 'avatar'; im.src = opts.image; wrap.appendChild(im); }
    var typing = byId('typingRow'); threadCol.insertBefore(wrap, typing);
    scrollThread(role === 'you');
    if (role === 'her' && !(opts && opts.image) && !(opts && opts.streaming) && text){ attachFeedback(wrap, text); applyEmotionCue(wrap, text); }
    return wrap;
  }
  // 👍/👎 on her replies -> engine.recordFeedback (feedbackLearning is on; this is the signal that activates it)
  function attachFeedback(wrap, text){
    if (!engine || typeof engine.recordFeedback !== 'function' || typeof engine.styleOf !== 'function') return;
    if (wrap.querySelector('.fb')) return;
    var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'fb';
    function mk(label, reward){
      var btn = document.createElement('button'); btn.type = 'button'; btn.textContent = label; btn.title = reward > 0 ? 'Tell her that one landed' : 'Tell her to ease off that style';
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        try { engine.recordFeedback(engine.styleOf(text), reward); } catch(e){}
        row.classList.add('voted');
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(row.children, function(c){ c.classList.remove('on'); });
        btn.classList.add('on');
      });
      return btn;
    }
    row.appendChild(mk('\ud83d\udc4d', 1)); row.appendChild(mk('\ud83d\udc4e', -1));
    if (engine && typeof engine.addHighlight === 'function'){
      var star = document.createElement('button'); star.type = 'button'; star.textContent = '\u2605'; star.title = 'Save this line to highlights';
      star.addEventListener('click', function(){ Promise.resolve(engine.addHighlight({ text: text, authorName: herName() }, USER_ID, userNameStr(), '')).then(function(){ star.classList.add('on'); }); });
      row.appendChild(star);
    }
    wrap.appendChild(row);
  }
  /* ===================== command layer: slash commands · JSON jobs · action toolbar ===================== */
  function userNameStr(){ return state.userName || 'You'; }
  function renderSystemLine(text, nar){ renderMessage('system', '', String(text), { system:true, nar: !!nar }); }
  function herContext(){
    if (engine && typeof engine.assembleContext === 'function')
      return Promise.resolve(engine.assembleContext({ authorId: USER_ID, authorName: userNameStr(), content: '' }));
    return Promise.resolve(null);
  }
  // fire a proactive handler: recap (summary) or beat (spontaneous / volunteer), rendered as her message
  function proactive(kind, idea){
    setThinking(true);
    herContext().then(function(actx){
      if (!actx){ setThinking(false); renderSystemLine('(connect a language model for that)'); return; }
      var p;
      if (kind === 'recap') p = recap({ recent: actx });
      else { actx.prompt = idea || 'Share a small, natural thought or observation right now.'; p = beat(actx); }
      Promise.resolve(p).then(function(r){
        setThinking(false);
        if (r && r.ok && r.value) soloSend(CH, String(r.value));
        else renderSystemLine('(' + ((r && r.reason) || 'nothing to say just now') + ')');
      }, function(){ setThinking(false); renderSystemLine('(that didn\u2019t work just now)'); });
    });
  }
  // AICC-style "write for me": draft the user's next message into the composer
  function writeForMe(){
    var ai = null; try { ai = window.aiTextPlugin || (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.aiTextPlugin); } catch(e){}
    if (typeof ai !== 'function'){ renderSystemLine('(connect a language model to draft for you)'); return; }
    var recent = queue.slice(-12).map(function(m){ return (m.author.bot ? herName() : userNameStr()) + ': ' + m.content; }).join('\n');
    var instr = 'You are writing as ' + userNameStr() + ', the human, in a 1:1 conversation with ' + herName() + '.\n'
      + (recent ? ('Conversation so far:\n' + recent + '\n\n') : '')
      + 'Write ' + userNameStr() + '\u2019s next message: natural, in their own voice, one short message. No name prefix, no quotation marks \u2014 just the message text.';
    var btn = byId('tbWrite'); if (btn) btn.disabled = true;
    Promise.resolve(ai({ instruction: instr, startWith: '' })).then(function(r){
      if (btn) btn.disabled = false;
      var t = String(r || '').trim().replace(/^[\s"'\u201c]+|[\s"'\u201d]+$/g, '');
      if (!t){ renderSystemLine('(couldn\u2019t draft one \u2014 try again)'); return; }
      var inp = byId('input'); inp.value = t; inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('input')); inp.focus();
    }, function(){ if (btn) btn.disabled = false; renderSystemLine('(draft failed)'); });
  }
  function doImage(args){
    var prompt = String(args && args.prompt || '').trim();
    if (prompt.length < 2){ renderSystemLine('(give me something to draw, e.g. /img a red fox in snow)'); return; }
    renderSystemLine('drawing: ' + prompt.slice(0,90), true); setThinking(true);
    Promise.resolve(paint({ prompt: prompt, resolution: args.resolution, guidanceScale: args.guidanceScale, removeBackground: !!args.removeBackground })).then(function(r){
      setThinking(false);
      if (r && r.ok && r.value) soloSendImage(CH, String(r.value), prompt);
      else renderSystemLine('(' + ((r && r.reason) || 'image failed') + ')');
    }, function(){ setThinking(false); renderSystemLine('(image failed)'); });
  }
  function addMemory(text){ text = String(text||'').trim();
    if (!text){ renderSystemLine('(what should the character remember? e.g. /mem I love sci-fi)'); return; }
    if (engine && engine.addFacts) Promise.resolve(engine.addFacts(USER_ID, [{ text: text, importance: 8 }], 'operator')).then(function(){ renderSystemLine('remembered: ' + text); try { renderFactList(); renderInnerState(); } catch(e){} });
  }
  function addSysDirective(text){ text = String(text||'').trim();
    if (/^clear$/i.test(text)){ state.injections = []; persistState(); refreshClock(); try { renderInjList(); } catch(e){} renderSystemLine('system directives cleared'); return; }
    if (!text){ renderSystemLine('(a standing directive, e.g. /sys We are aboard a starship in 2400)'); return; }
    if (!state.injections) state.injections = [];
    state.injections.push({ id: 'inj' + Date.now(), text: text }); persistState(); refreshClock(); try { renderInjList(); } catch(e){}
    renderSystemLine('system directive added: ' + text);
  }
  function addNarration(text){ text = String(text||'').trim();
    if (!text){ renderSystemLine('(a line of scene/narration, e.g. /nar Rain begins to fall outside)'); return; }
    renderSystemLine(text, true);
    enqueue(USER_ID, userNameStr(), false, '*' + text + '*');   // she reads the scene and reacts
    dropLiveOrphan(); replyExpected = true; setThinking(true);
    if (engine && engine.pollOnce){ try { engine.pollOnce(); } catch(e){} }
  }
  function addGoalCmd(text){ text = String(text||'').trim();
    if (!text){ renderSystemLine('(a goal, e.g. /goal ask how my exam went)'); return; }
    if (engine && engine.addGoal) Promise.resolve(engine.addGoal(text, USER_ID, userNameStr(), 'command')).then(function(){ renderSystemLine('noted a goal: ' + text); try { renderInnerState(); } catch(e){} });
  }
  function forgetCmd(rest){ rest = String(rest||'').trim();
    if (/^me$/i.test(rest)){ if (confirm('Forget everything the character has learned about you?') && engine && engine.getFacts){ Promise.resolve(engine.getFacts(USER_ID)).then(function(fs){ (fs||[]).forEach(function(f){ try { engine.forgetFact(USER_ID, f.text); } catch(e){} }); renderSystemLine('forgotten everything about you'); try { renderFactList(); renderInnerState(); } catch(e){} }); } return; }
    if (!rest){ renderSystemLine('(/forget <a thing>  or  /forget me)'); return; }
    if (engine && engine.forgetFact) Promise.resolve(engine.forgetFact(USER_ID, rest)).then(function(){ renderSystemLine('forgotten: ' + rest); try { renderFactList(); } catch(e){} });
  }
  function aboutMe(){ if (!(engine && engine.getMemory)) return;
    Promise.resolve(engine.getMemory(USER_ID)).then(function(m){
      var facts = (m && m.facts || []).map(function(f){ return f.text; });
      var ins = (m && m.insights || []).map(function(x){ return x.text; });
      var parts = []; if (ins.length) parts.push(ins.join('; ')); if (facts.length) parts.push(facts.join('; '));
      soloSend(CH, parts.length ? ('Here\u2019s what I know about you: ' + parts.join('. ') + '.') : 'I haven\u2019t learned much about you yet \u2014 keep talking to me.');
    });
  }
  function showGoals(){ if (!(engine && engine.goalsForOwner)) return;
    Promise.resolve(engine.goalsForOwner(USER_ID)).then(function(g){ g = g || []; soloSend(CH, g.length ? ('Things I mean to follow up on: ' + g.map(function(x){ return x.text; }).join('; ') + '.') : 'No goals on my list yet.'); });
  }
  function highlightLast(note){
    var last = null; for (var i = queue.length - 1; i >= 0; i--){ if (queue[i].author.bot){ last = queue[i]; break; } }
    if (!last) last = queue[queue.length - 1];
    if (!last){ renderSystemLine('(nothing to highlight yet)'); return; }
    if (engine && engine.addHighlight) Promise.resolve(engine.addHighlight({ text: last.content, authorName: last.author.username || herName() }, USER_ID, userNameStr(), note || '')).then(function(r){
      renderSystemLine((r && r.ok === false) ? ('(' + r.reason + ')') : ('\u2605 highlighted: \u201c' + String(last.content).slice(0,60) + '\u201d' + (note ? (' \u2014 ' + note) : '')));
    });
  }
  function showHighlights(rest){ rest = String(rest||'').trim();
    if (/^clear$/i.test(rest)){ if (engine && engine.clearHighlights) Promise.resolve(engine.clearHighlights()).then(function(n){ renderSystemLine(n ? ('cleared ' + n + ' highlight' + (n===1?'':'s')) : 'no highlights to clear'); }); return; }
    if (engine && engine.listHighlights) Promise.resolve(engine.listHighlights(10)).then(function(list){ list = list || [];
      if (!list.length){ renderSystemLine('no highlights yet \u2014 /highlight saves the last line'); return; }
