      renderSystemLine('\u2605 ' + list.map(function(h){ return '\u201c' + String(h.text).slice(0,56) + '\u201d' + (h.note ? (' (' + h.note + ')') : ''); }).join('   '));
    });
  }
  function clockAck(kind){ var d = new Date(); renderSystemLine(kind === 'date' ? d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, { weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' }) : d.toLocaleTimeString()); }
  function setLang(code){ code = String(code||'').trim(); if (!(engine && engine.setUserLang)) return;
    if (!code || /^(off|none|clear|default)$/i.test(code)){ engine.setUserLang(USER_ID, null); renderSystemLine('reply language: default'); return; }
    engine.setUserLang(USER_ID, code); renderSystemLine('reply language set to ' + code);
  }
  function statusCmd(){
    Promise.all([
      (engine && engine.getFacts) ? Promise.resolve(engine.getFacts(USER_ID)).catch(function(){ return []; }) : Promise.resolve([]),
      (engine && engine.goalsForOwner) ? Promise.resolve(engine.goalsForOwner(USER_ID)).catch(function(){ return []; }) : Promise.resolve([]),
      (engine && engine.listReminders) ? Promise.resolve(engine.listReminders(USER_ID)).catch(function(){ return []; }) : Promise.resolve([]),
      store.get('mood:' + CH).catch(function(){ return null; })
    ]).then(function(r){
      var facts = r[0]||[], goals = r[1]||[], rem = r[2]||[], mood = r[3];
      var moodStr = (mood && engine && engine.moodDescriptor) ? engine.moodDescriptor(mood) : '';
      var bits = [ queue.length + ' messages', facts.length + ' facts about you', goals.length + ' goals', rem.length + ' reminders' ];
      if (moodStr) bits.push('mood: ' + moodStr);
      renderSystemLine('status \u2014 ' + bits.join(' \u00b7 '));
    });
  }
  function personaCmd(rest){ rest = String(rest||'').trim();
    if (/^clear$/i.test(rest)){ var cl = (engine && engine.clearPersonaNote) ? engine.clearPersonaNote() : store.del('persona:note'); Promise.resolve(cl).then(function(){ renderSystemLine('persona note cleared'); }); return; }
    if (!rest){ var g = (engine && engine.getPersonaNote) ? engine.getPersonaNote() : store.get('persona:note'); Promise.resolve(g).then(function(pn){ renderSystemLine((pn && pn.text) ? ('persona note: ' + pn.text) : '(no persona note \u2014 /persona <a style note> to set one)'); }); return; }
    // set a style note in the exact record shape assembleContext reads (-> base.personaNote on her next reply)
    Promise.resolve(store.set('persona:note', { msgId: 'manual' + Date.now(), text: rest, by: userNameStr(), at: Date.now(), persona: null })).then(function(){ renderSystemLine('persona note set: ' + rest); });
  }
  function parseDur(s){ var m = String(s||'').trim().match(/^(\d+)\s*([mhd])$/i); if (!m) return null; var n = +m[1], u = m[2].toLowerCase(); return u === 'm' ? n : (u === 'h' ? n*60 : n*1440); }
  function remindCmd(rest){ rest = String(rest||'').trim();
    if (/^clear$/i.test(rest)){ if (engine && engine.clearReminders) Promise.resolve(engine.clearReminders(USER_ID)).then(function(n){ renderSystemLine(n ? ('cleared ' + n + ' reminder' + (n===1?'':'s')) : 'no reminders to clear'); }); return; }
    if (/^(list|)$/i.test(rest) && rest.indexOf(' ') < 0 && !parseDur(rest.split(' ')[0])){ if (engine && engine.listReminders) Promise.resolve(engine.listReminders(USER_ID)).then(function(list){ list = list || []; renderSystemLine(list.length ? ('reminders: ' + list.map(function(r){ return r.text; }).join(' \u00b7 ')) : 'no reminders set'); }); return; }
    var m = rest.match(/^(\S+)\s+([\s\S]+)$/); var mins = m ? parseDur(m[1]) : null;
    if (!m || !mins){ renderSystemLine('(/remind 10m drink water  \u2014  units: m, h, d)'); return; }
    if (engine && engine.scheduleReminder) Promise.resolve(engine.scheduleReminder({ minutes: mins, text: m[2], authorId: USER_ID, authorName: userNameStr() })).then(function(r){ renderSystemLine((r && r.ok === false) ? ('(' + r.reason + ')') : ('reminder set in ' + m[1] + ': ' + m[2])); });
  }
  function runJsonJob(obj){
    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object'){ renderSystemLine('(that JSON wasn\u2019t a job I recognise)'); return; }
    var type = String(obj.type || obj.cmd || (obj.prompt ? 'image' : '')).toLowerCase();
    if (type === 'image' || type === 'img'){ doImage(obj); return; }
    if (type === 'remind' || type === 'reminder'){ if (engine && engine.scheduleReminder) Promise.resolve(engine.scheduleReminder({ minutes: Number(obj.minutes || obj.mins) || 0, text: obj.text || '', authorId: USER_ID, authorName: userNameStr() })).then(function(r){ renderSystemLine((r && r.ok === false) ? ('(' + r.reason + ')') : ('reminder set: ' + (obj.text||''))); }); return; }
    if (type === 'mem' || type === 'memory'){ addMemory(obj.text); return; }
    if (type === 'goal'){ addGoalCmd(obj.text); return; }
    if (type === 'sys' || type === 'system'){ addSysDirective(obj.text); return; }
    if (type === 'nar' || type === 'narrate' || type === 'narration'){ addNarration(obj.text); return; }
    renderSystemLine('(unrecognised job type: ' + (type || 'none') + ')');
  }
  var COMMANDS = [
    { group:'Compose & scene', items:[
      ['/img <prompt>', 'generate an image now — then "make it landscape", "add a hat", "more moody", or "another one" refines the last one'],
      ['/nar <text>', 'narrate a scene line the character reacts to'],
      ['/sys <text>', 'a standing directive (/sys clear resets)'],
      ['/mem <text>', 'remember a durable fact about you'] ] },
    { group:'Make them act', items:[
      ['/recap', 'the character summarises the conversation'],
      ['/beat [idea]', 'a spontaneous in-character message'],
      ['/volunteer', 'the character speaks up on their own'],
      ['/writeforme', 'draft your next message'] ] },
    { group:'Memory & life', items:[
      ['/remind 10m <text>', 'set a reminder (m/h/d; /remind clear)'],
      ['/goal <text>', 'give the character a goal to follow up on'],
      ['/aboutme', 'what the character remembers about you'],
      ['/highlight [note]', 'save the last line to revisit'],
      ['/highlights', 'list saved lines (/highlights clear)'],
      ['/forget <thing>', '/forget me to wipe'],
      ['/persona <note>', 'set/show the character’s style note (/persona clear)'],
      ['/lang <code>', 'reply language (/lang off)'],
      ['/time   /date', 'the current time / date'] ] },
    { group:'Power', items:[
      ['/status', 'a quick diagnostic'],
      ['{ "type":"image", "prompt":"\u2026" }', 'paste JSON to run a job'],
      ['/do { \u2026json }', 'run a JSON job explicitly'],
      ['/help', 'show this list'] ] }
  ];
  function handleComposerCommand(text){
    var t = String(text||'').trim();
    if (t.charAt(0) === '{'){ var obj = null; try { obj = JSON.parse(t); } catch(e){ obj = null; } if (obj){ runJsonJob(obj); return true; } return false; }
    if (t.charAt(0) !== '/') return false;
    var sp = t.indexOf(' '); var verb = (sp < 0 ? t.slice(1) : t.slice(1, sp)).toLowerCase(); var rest = sp < 0 ? '' : t.slice(sp+1).trim();
    switch(verb){
      case 'img': case 'image':
        if (rest.charAt(0) === '{'){ var o = null; try { o = JSON.parse(rest); } catch(e){} doImage(o || { prompt: rest }); } else doImage({ prompt: rest }); return true;
      case 'mem': case 'remember': addMemory(rest); return true;
      case 'sys': case 'system': addSysDirective(rest); return true;
      case 'nar': case 'narrate': addNarration(rest); return true;
      case 'recap': proactive('recap'); return true;
      case 'beat': proactive('beat', rest); return true;
      case 'volunteer': case 'nudge': proactive('beat', 'Jump into the conversation naturally and say what\u2019s on your mind right now.'); return true;
      case 'writeforme': case 'write': writeForMe(); return true;
      case 'remind': remindCmd(rest); return true;
      case 'reminders': remindCmd(rest || 'list'); return true;
      case 'goal': addGoalCmd(rest); return true;
      case 'goals': showGoals(); return true;
      case 'forget': forgetCmd(rest); return true;
      case 'aboutme': aboutMe(); return true;
      case 'highlight': case 'star': highlightLast(rest); return true;
      case 'highlights': showHighlights(rest); return true;
      case 'status': statusCmd(); return true;
      case 'persona': personaCmd(rest); return true;
      case 'time': clockAck('time'); return true;
      case 'date': clockAck('date'); return true;
      case 'lang': setLang(rest); return true;
      case 'do': case 'job': { var oj = null; try { oj = JSON.parse(rest); } catch(e){} if (oj) runJsonJob(oj); else renderSystemLine('(/do expects JSON, e.g. /do { "type":"image", "prompt":"a fox" })'); return true; }
      case 'help': case '?': openPalette(true); return true;
      default: renderSystemLine('(unknown command: /' + verb + ' \u2014 try /help)'); return true;
    }
  }
  /* ---- command palette + action toolbar ---- */
  function buildPalette(){ var p = byId('cmdPalette'); if (!p || p.__built) return; p.__built = true;
    COMMANDS.forEach(function(g){
      var h = document.createElement('h4'); h.textContent = g.group; p.appendChild(h);
      g.items.forEach(function(it){
        var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'cmdrow';
        var c = document.createElement('span'); c.className = 'cmd'; c.textContent = it[0];
        var d = document.createElement('span'); d.className = 'desc'; d.textContent = it[1];
        row.appendChild(c); row.appendChild(d);
        row.addEventListener('click', function(){ var stub = it[0].split(' ')[0]; if (stub.charAt(0) === '/'){ var inp = byId('input'); inp.value = stub + ' '; inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('input')); inp.focus(); } openPalette(false); });
        p.appendChild(row);
      });
    });
  }
  function openPalette(on){ buildPalette(); var p = byId('cmdPalette'); if (!p) return; if (on === undefined) on = !p.classList.contains('open'); p.classList.toggle('open', on); }
  function wireToolbar(){
    byId('tbWrite').addEventListener('click', writeForMe);
    byId('tbRecap').addEventListener('click', function(){ proactive('recap'); });
    byId('tbVolunteer').addEventListener('click', function(){ proactive('beat', 'Jump into the conversation naturally and say what\u2019s on your mind right now.'); });
    byId('tbBeat').addEventListener('click', function(){ proactive('beat', 'Share a small, spontaneous thought or observation right now.'); });
    byId('tbRemind').addEventListener('click', function(){ var inp = byId('input'); inp.value = '/remind 30m '; inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('input')); inp.focus(); });
    byId('tbCmds').addEventListener('click', function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); openPalette(); });
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e){ var p = byId('cmdPalette'); if (p && p.classList.contains('open') && !p.contains(e.target) && e.target.id !== 'tbCmds'){ openPalette(false); } });
  }

  function sendUserMessage(){
    var inp = byId('input'); var text = inp.value.trim(); if (!text) return;
    if (handleComposerCommand(text)){ inp.value = ''; inp.style.height = 'auto'; byId('sendBtn').disabled = true; return; }
    inp.value = ''; inp.style.height = 'auto'; byId('sendBtn').disabled = true;
    renderMessage('you', state.userName||'You', text);
    enqueue(USER_ID, state.userName||'You', false, text);
    dropLiveOrphan(); replyExpected = true;   // a reply to this message is the only thing allowed to stream into chat
    setThinking(true);
    if (engine && engine.pollOnce) { try { engine.pollOnce(); } catch(e){} }   // read it immediately, don't wait for the poll timer
    if (engineThinking) byId('typingRow').classList.add('on');
  }

  /* ---- settings popup ---- */
  /* ---- personality dials (Behavior tab): live tone control via personaStyle banding ---- */
  function patchPersonality(){ if (engine && engine.updateConfig){ try { engine.updateConfig({ personality: state.personality }); } catch(e){} } }
  function renderDials(){
    var box = byId('dials'); if (!box) return; box.innerHTML = '';
    if (!state.personality) state.personality = {};
    DIALS.forEach(function(d){
      var key = d[0], lo = d[1], hi = d[2];
      var v = state.personality[key]; if (v == null) v = 0.5;
      var wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'dial';
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="dialhead"><span>' + lo + '</span><span class="dn">' + key + '</span><span>' + hi + '</span></div>';
      var inp = document.createElement('input'); inp.type = 'range'; inp.min = '0'; inp.max = '100'; inp.step = '1'; inp.value = String(Math.round(v * 100)); inp.id = 'dial_' + key;
      inp.addEventListener('input', function(){ state.personality[key] = (+inp.value) / 100; patchPersonality(); });   // live tone
      inp.addEventListener('change', function(){ persistState(); });                                                   // save on release
      wrap.appendChild(inp); box.appendChild(wrap);
    });
  }
  function resetDials(){ state.personality = { kindness:0.5, sarcasm:0.5, curiosity:0.5, playfulness:0.5, formality:0.5, verbosity:0.5 }; persistState(); patchPersonality(); renderDials(); }

  /* ---- behavior toggles (Behavior tab): every cognitive feature the Discord app exposed, live-patched ---- */
  function patchToggle(key, val){ var p = {}; p[key] = val; if (engine && engine.updateConfig){ try { engine.updateConfig(p); } catch(e){} } }
  function renderToggles(){
    var box = byId('behaviorToggles'); if (!box) return; box.innerHTML = '';
    TOGGLE_GROUPS.forEach(function(g){
      var card = document.createElement('div'); card.className = 'card';
      var h = document.createElement('h3'); h.textContent = g.title; card.appendChild(h);
      if (g.note){ var n = document.createElement('div'); n.className = 'note'; n.textContent = g.note; card.appendChild(n); }
      g.items.forEach(function(it){
        var key = it[0], label = it[1], desc = it[2];
        var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'toggle';
        var cb = document.createElement('input'); cb.type = 'checkbox'; cb.id = 't_' + key; cb.checked = !!state[key];
        var d = document.createElement('div'); d.innerHTML = '<div class="tl"></div><div class="td"></div>';
        d.querySelector('.tl').textContent = label; d.querySelector('.td').textContent = desc;
        cb.addEventListener('change', function(){ state[key] = cb.checked; persistState(); patchToggle(key, cb.checked); });
        row.appendChild(cb); row.appendChild(d); card.appendChild(row);
      });
      box.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  function openSettings(){ byId('settingsBg').classList.add('open'); renderAppearance(); renderMemPicker(); refreshMemStats(); renderFactList(); renderInnerState(); renderInjList(); renderLore(); renderDials(); renderToggles(); renderModeration(); renderEmotionToggle(); renderContextBudget(); refreshClock(); }
  // Context inspector: show what's in context per reply, priced with the same tokenizer the engine
  // uses (engine.estimateTokens), plus the authoritative totals.
  function renderContextBudget(){
    var box = byId('ctxBudget'); var eng = viewEngine(); if (!box) return;
    if (!eng){ box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">\u2014</div>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">measuring\u2026</div>';
    var tok = function(s){ try { return eng.estimateTokens ? eng.estimateTokens(String(s || '')) : Math.ceil(String(s || '').length / 4); } catch(e){ return Math.ceil(String(s || '').length / 4); } };
    var vc = viewChar();
    var personaStr = (vc && vc.instruction) ? vc.instruction : '';
    var injStr = (state.injections || []).map(function(x){ return x.text; }).join('\n');
    function P(fn){ return Promise.resolve().then(fn).catch(function(){ return null; }); }
    Promise.all([
      P(function(){ return eng.getMemory ? eng.getMemory(USER_ID) : null; }),
      P(function(){ return eng.getPersonaNote ? eng.getPersonaNote() : null; }),
      P(function(){ return eng.assembleContext ? eng.assembleContext({ authorId: USER_ID, authorName: userNameStr(), content: '' }) : null; })
    ]).then(function(r){
      var mem = r[0], persona = r[1], ctx = r[2];
      var factsStr = mem ? (((mem.insights || []).map(function(x){ return x.text; }).join('; ')) + ' ' + ((mem.facts || []).map(function(f){ return f.text; }).join('; '))) : '';
      var personaNoteStr = persona ? (typeof persona === 'string' ? persona : (persona.text || '')) : '';
      var budget = (eng.config && eng.config.requestTokenBudget) || 5000;
      var histTok = (ctx && ctx.contextTokens != null) ? ctx.contextTokens : 0;
      var rows = [
        ['Character & persona', tok(personaStr) + tok(personaNoteStr), '#5B62E0'],
        ['Memory — facts & insights', tok(factsStr), '#2E9E7B'],
        ['World directives', tok(injStr), '#C98A2B'],
        ['Recent conversation', histTok, '#8A5BD0']
      ];
      var total = (ctx && ctx.requestTokensEst != null) ? ctx.requestTokensEst : rows.reduce(function(a, x){ return a + x[1]; }, 0);
      var dropped = ctx ? (ctx.contextDropped || 0) : 0;
      var over = total > budget, html = '';
      rows.forEach(function(row){
        var pct = Math.max(2, Math.min(100, Math.round(row[1] / budget * 100)));
        html += '<div class="ctxrow"><div class="ctxlabel"><span>' + row[0] + '</span><span class="ctxtok">~' + row[1] + ' tok</span></div>'
              + '<div class="ctxbar"><div class="ctxfill" style="width:' + pct + '%;background:' + row[2] + '"></div></div></div>';
      });
      var usePct = Math.max(2, Math.min(100, Math.round(total / budget * 100)));
      html += '<div class="ctxtotal"><b>~' + total + '</b> / ' + budget + ' tokens' + (over ? ' <span style="color:var(--bad)">over — oldest lines dropped</span>' : '') + '</div>';
      html += '<div class="ctxbar big"><div class="ctxfill" style="width:' + usePct + '%;background:' + (over ? 'var(--bad)' : 'var(--accent)') + '"></div></div>';
      if (dropped) html += '<div class="note" style="margin-top:6px">' + dropped + ' older line' + (dropped === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' dropped to fit.</div>';
      box.innerHTML = html;
    }).catch(function(){ box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">(couldn\u2019t measure right now)</div>'; });
  }
  function renderModeration(){
    var en = byId('modEnabled'), ph = byId('modPhrases'); if (!en || !ph) return;
    var m = state.moderation || (state.moderation = { enabled:false, phrases:[], rating:'x' });
    en.checked = !!m.enabled; ph.value = (m.phrases || []).join('\n');
    function count(){ return (m.phrases || []).length; }
    function note(){ setText('modNote', m.enabled ? (count() + ' blocked term' + (count() === 1 ? '' : 's')) : 'gate off'); }
    function save(){ m.enabled = en.checked; m.phrases = ph.value.split('\n').map(function(s){ return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); persistState(); note(); }
    if (!en.__wired){ en.__wired = true; en.addEventListener('change', save); ph.addEventListener('change', save); }
    note();
  }
  function renderEmotionToggle(){
    var t = byId('emoToggle'); if (!t) return;
    t.checked = state.showEmotion !== false;
    if (!t.__wired){ t.__wired = true; t.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.showEmotion = t.checked; persistState(); refreshEmotionCues(); }); }
  }
  function closeSettings(){ byId('settingsBg').classList.remove('open'); }
  function openCharacters(){ byId('charactersBg').classList.add('open'); updateCharLabel(); renderRoster(); }
  function closeCharacters(){ byId('charactersBg').classList.remove('open'); }
  function exportSlotFile(s){
    var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify({ format:'chloe-solo', version: s.version || SOLO_VERSION, data: s.data }, null, 0)], { type:'application/json' });
    var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = 'chloe-solo-save-' + String(s.label || s.kind || 'slot').replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/gi, '-').slice(0, 30) + '.json'; a.click();
    setTimeout(function(){ URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href); }, 1500);
  }
  function renderSaves(){
    var chk = byId('autoSaveChk'); if (chk) chk.checked = state.autoSave !== false;
    var mi = byId('autoSaveMins'); if (mi) mi.value = state.autoSaveMins || 10;
    var ke = byId('autoSaveKeep'); if (ke) ke.value = state.autoSaveKeep || 10;
    var box = byId('savesList'); if (!box) return;
    box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">loading\u2026</div>';
    Saves.list().then(function(all){
      box.innerHTML = '';
      if (!all.length){ box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">No saves yet \u2014 save now, or let auto-checkpoints build up.</div>'; return; }
      all.forEach(function(s){
        var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'save-row';
        var meta = document.createElement('div'); meta.className = 'save-meta';
        var title = document.createElement('div'); title.className = 'save-title';
        var badge = document.createElement('span'); badge.className = 'save-badge ' + (s.kind === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'manual'); badge.textContent = s.kind === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'saved'; title.appendChild(badge);
        var lbl = document.createElement('span'); lbl.textContent = s.label || (s.kind === 'auto' ? 'checkpoint' : 'manual save'); title.appendChild(lbl);
        var sub = document.createElement('div'); sub.className = 'save-sub'; sub.textContent = new Date(s.ts).toLocaleString() + ' \u00b7 ' + (s.msgCount || 0) + ' messages';
        meta.appendChild(title); meta.appendChild(sub);
        var acts = document.createElement('div'); acts.className = 'save-acts';
        var load = document.createElement('button'); load.className = 'btn'; load.textContent = 'Load';
        load.addEventListener('click', function(){ if (confirm('Load this save?\n\nThis rolls the entire session \u2014 the conversation and every character\u2019s memory \u2014 back to that point. Your current state will be replaced; save it first if you want to keep it.')) restoreSlot(s.id); });
        var exp = document.createElement('button'); exp.className = 'btn'; exp.textContent = 'Export'; exp.addEventListener('click', function(){ exportSlotFile(s); });
        var del = document.createElement('button'); del.className = 'btn danger'; del.textContent = '\u2715'; del.title = 'Delete this save'; del.addEventListener('click', function(){ Saves.del(s.id).then(renderSaves); });
        acts.appendChild(load); acts.appendChild(exp); acts.appendChild(del);
        row.appendChild(meta); row.appendChild(acts); box.appendChild(row);
      });
    }).catch(function(){ box.innerHTML = '<div class="note">could not read saves.</div>'; });
  }
  function openSaves(){ byId('savesBg').classList.add('open'); renderSaves(); }
  function closeSaves(){ byId('savesBg').classList.remove('open'); }

  /* ---- gallery viewer: a Solo-styled grid over whichever backend is active ---- */
  var galleryOpen = false, gallerySort = 'newest', galleryFavOnly = false, _galUrls = [];
  function revokeGalUrls(){ _galUrls.forEach(function(u){ try { URL.revokeObjectURL(u); } catch(e){} }); _galUrls = []; }
  function openGallery(){ byId('galleryBg').classList.add('open'); galleryOpen = true; Gallery.init().then(renderGallery).catch(function(){ renderGallery(); }); }
  function closeGallery(){ byId('galleryBg').classList.remove('open'); galleryOpen = false; revokeGalUrls(); closeLightbox(); }
  function sortManifest(list){
    var a = list.slice();
    if (gallerySort === 'oldest') a.sort(function(x,y){ return x.createdAt - y.createdAt; });
    else if (gallerySort === 'favorites') a.sort(function(x,y){ return (y.favorited?1:0) - (x.favorited?1:0) || y.createdAt - x.createdAt; });
    else a.sort(function(x,y){ return y.createdAt - x.createdAt; });
    if (galleryFavOnly) a = a.filter(function(e){ return e.favorited; });
    return a;
  }
  function renderGallery(){
    var grid = byId('galleryGrid'); if (!grid) return;
    Gallery.getManifest().then(function(man){
      revokeGalUrls(); grid.innerHTML = '';
      var view = sortManifest(man || []);
      byId('galleryCount').textContent = (man && man.length) ? (man.length + ' image' + (man.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + (Gallery.usingWeld() ? ' \u00b7 weld.gallery' : '')) : '';
      byId('galleryEmpty').style.display = view.length ? 'none' : 'block';
      view.forEach(function(e){
        var tile = document.createElement('div'); tile.className = 'gtile';
        Gallery.getBlobUrl(e.id).then(function(url){
          if (!url) return; _galUrls.push(url);
          var img = document.createElement('img'); img.src = url; img.alt = e.prompt || '';
          tile.insertBefore(img, tile.firstChild);
          tile.addEventListener('click', function(ev){ if (ev.target.closest && ev.target.closest('.gact')) return; openLightbox(url, e.prompt); });
        });
        var fav = document.createElement('span'); fav.className = 'gfavmark'; fav.textContent = e.favorited ? '\u2605' : '';
        var acts = document.createElement('div'); acts.className = 'gacts';
        var bFav = document.createElement('button'); bFav.className = 'gact' + (e.favorited ? ' on' : ''); bFav.title = 'Favorite'; bFav.textContent = '\u2605';
        bFav.addEventListener('click', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); Gallery.toggleFavorite(e.id).then(renderGallery); });
        var bDl = document.createElement('button'); bDl.className = 'gact'; bDl.title = 'Download'; bDl.textContent = '\u2193';
        bDl.addEventListener('click', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); Gallery.getBlobUrl(e.id).then(function(u){ if (!u) return; var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = u; a.download = (e.id || 'image') + '.png'; document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); a.remove(); setTimeout(function(){ URL.revokeObjectURL(u); }, 1500); }); });
        var bDel = document.createElement('button'); bDel.className = 'gact'; bDel.title = 'Delete'; bDel.textContent = '\u2715';
        bDel.addEventListener('click', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); Gallery.remove(e.id).then(renderGallery); });
        acts.appendChild(bFav); acts.appendChild(bDl); acts.appendChild(bDel);
        var cap = document.createElement('div'); cap.className = 'gcap'; cap.textContent = e.prompt || '(no prompt)';
        tile.appendChild(fav); tile.appendChild(acts); tile.appendChild(cap);
        grid.appendChild(tile);
      });
    }).catch(function(){});
  }
  function openLightbox(url, prompt){ byId('lightboxImg').src = url; byId('lightboxCap').textContent = prompt || ''; byId('lightbox').style.display = 'flex'; }
  function closeLightbox(){ var lb = byId('lightbox'); if (lb){ lb.style.display = 'none'; byId('lightboxImg').src = ''; } }
  function wireGallery(){
    byId('openGallery').addEventListener('click', openGallery);
    byId('galleryClose').addEventListener('click', closeGallery);
    byId('galleryBg').addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === byId('galleryBg')) closeGallery(); });
    byId('gallerySort').addEventListener('change', function(){ gallerySort = this.value; renderGallery(); });
    byId('galleryFavOnly').addEventListener('change', function(){ galleryFavOnly = this.checked; renderGallery(); });
    byId('galleryClear').addEventListener('click', function(){ if (window.confirm('Delete all saved images? This cannot be undone.')) Gallery.clear().then(renderGallery).then(function(){ toast('Gallery cleared'); }); });
    byId('lightboxClose').addEventListener('click', closeLightbox);
    byId('lightbox').addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === byId('lightbox')) closeLightbox(); });
  }

  /* ---- community comments (weld.comments inline when imported; the plugin handles posting + moderation) ---- */
  var _communityMounted = false;
  function openCommunity(){
    byId('communityBg').classList.add('open');
    var host = byId('communityHost'), off = byId('communityOff');
    var wc = (window.weld && window.weld.comments);
    if (wc && (wc.inline || wc.open)){
      off.style.display = 'none'; host.style.display = '';
      if (!_communityMounted){
        _communityMounted = true;
        try {
          var app = (typeof window.generatorName === 'string' && window.generatorName) || 'chloe-solo';
          if (wc.inline) wc.inline('#communityHost', { key: 'chloe-solo-community', app: app });
          else wc.open({ key: 'chloe-solo-community', app: app });
        } catch(e){ _communityMounted = false; host.style.display = 'none'; off.style.display = 'block'; }
      }
    } else { host.style.display = 'none'; off.style.display = 'block'; }
  }
  function closeCommunity(){ byId('communityBg').classList.remove('open'); }
  function wireCommunity(){
    byId('openCommunity').addEventListener('click', openCommunity);
    byId('communityClose').addEventListener('click', closeCommunity);
    byId('communityBg').addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === byId('communityBg')) closeCommunity(); });
  }
  function refreshMemStats(){
    var keys = 0, bytes = 0; try { for (var i=0;i<localStorage.length;i++){ var key = localStorage.key(i); if (key && key.indexOf(NS)===0){ keys++; bytes += (localStorage.getItem(key)||'').length; } } } catch(e){}
    var msgs = queue.length;
    setText('memStats', msgs + ' message' + (msgs===1?'':'s') + ' · ' + keys + ' stored keys · ~' + Math.round(bytes/1024) + ' KB in this browser');
  }
  function wireSettings(){
    byId('openSettings').addEventListener('click', openSettings);
    byId('closeSettings').addEventListener('click', closeSettings);
    var oc = byId('openCharacters'); if (oc) oc.addEventListener('click', openCharacters);
    var cc = byId('closeCharacters'); if (cc) cc.addEventListener('click', closeCharacters);
    var cbg = byId('charactersBg'); if (cbg) cbg.addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === cbg) closeCharacters(); });
    var os2 = byId('openSaves'); if (os2) os2.addEventListener('click', openSaves);
    var cs2 = byId('closeSaves'); if (cs2) cs2.addEventListener('click', closeSaves);
    var sbg = byId('savesBg'); if (sbg) sbg.addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === sbg) closeSaves(); });
    var sn = byId('saveNowBtn'); if (sn) sn.addEventListener('click', function(){ var lbl = (byId('saveLabel').value || '').trim(); setText('saveNote', 'saving\u2026'); saveSlot('manual', lbl).then(function(){ byId('saveLabel').value = ''; setText('saveNote', 'saved.'); renderSaves(); toast('Session saved', 'success'); }).catch(function(){ setText('saveNote', 'could not save \u2014 storage may be full.'); }); });
    var asc = byId('autoSaveChk'); if (asc) asc.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.autoSave = asc.checked; persistState(); startAutoSave(); });
    var asm = byId('autoSaveMins'); if (asm) asm.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.autoSaveMins = Math.max(1, Math.min(180, parseInt(asm.value, 10) || 10)); persistState(); startAutoSave(); });
    var ask = byId('autoSaveKeep'); if (ask) ask.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.autoSaveKeep = Math.max(1, Math.min(50, parseInt(ask.value, 10) || 10)); persistState(); pruneAuto(); });
    var dr = byId('dialsReset'); if (dr) dr.addEventListener('click', resetDials);
    // behavior toggles are rendered + wired live in renderToggles() (openSettings)
    byId('settingsBg').addEventListener('click', function(e){ if (e.target === byId('settingsBg')) closeSettings(); });
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.tab'), function(tb){
      tb.addEventListener('click', function(){
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(x){ x.classList.remove('on'); });
        document.querySelectorAll('.panel').forEach(function(x){ x.classList.remove('on'); });
        tb.classList.add('on'); document.querySelector('.panel[data-panel="'+tb.getAttribute('data-tab')+'"]').classList.add('on');
      });
    });
    // behavior toggles -> live config
    var nameEl = byId('botNameInput'); nameEl.value = state.botName || 'Chloe';
    nameEl.addEventListener('change', function(){ applyConfig({ botName: (nameEl.value||'Chloe').trim() || 'Chloe' }); updateCharLabel(); });
    // You tab: your name + pinned things she should know about you
    var unEl = byId('userNameInput'); unEl.value = state.userName || 'You';
    unEl.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.userName = (unEl.value||'You').trim() || 'You'; persistState(); ensureUserPartition(); });
    byId('aboutYouBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){
      var v = (byId('aboutYouInput').value||'').trim(); if (!v) return;
      if (!engine || !engine.addFacts){ setText('aboutYouNote','one moment\u2026'); return; }
      ensureUserPartition().then(function(){ return engine.addFacts(USER_ID, [{ text: v, importance: 8 }], 'operator'); }).then(function(n){
        byId('aboutYouInput').value=''; setText('aboutYouNote', n ? 'the character will keep that in mind.' : 'already known.'); renderFactList();
      });
    });
    byId('aboutYouInput').addEventListener('keydown', function(e){ if (e.key==='Enter'){ e.preventDefault(); byId('aboutYouBtn').click(); } });
    // Context tab: always-known facts (semantic injections)
    byId('injAddBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){
      var v = (byId('injInput').value||'').trim(); if (!v) return;
      if (!state.injections) state.injections = [];
      state.injections.push({ id: 'inj' + Date.now(), text: v }); persistState();
      byId('injInput').value=''; refreshClock(); renderInjList();
    });
    byId('injInput').addEventListener('keydown', function(e){ if (e.key==='Enter'){ e.preventDefault(); byId('injAddBtn').click(); } });
    byId('loreAddBtn').addEventListener('click', addLore);
    byId('loreExportBtn').addEventListener('click', exportLore);
    byId('loreImportBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){ byId('loreFile').click(); });
    byId('loreFile').addEventListener('change', function(){ var f = this.files && this.files[0]; if (f) importLore(f); this.value = ''; });
    // Her portrait (image plugin)
    byId('portraitBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){
      setText('portraitNote', 'painting\u2026');
      var who = state.character ? state.character.name : (state.botName||'Chloe');
      var desc = (state.character && state.character.instruction) ? String(state.character.instruction).replace(/\s+/g,' ').slice(0,200) : 'a warm, thoughtful presence';
      Promise.resolve(paint({ prompt: 'portrait of ' + who + ', ' + desc + ', soft natural light, head and shoulders', resolution: '512x512' })).then(function(r){
        if (r && r.ok && r.value){ state.herAvatar = r.value; persistState(); updateCharLabel(); setText('portraitNote','done.'); toast('Portrait updated', 'success'); renderMessage('her', state.botName||'Chloe', '', { image: r.value }); }
        else setText('portraitNote', (r && r.reason) ? r.reason : 'no image \u2014 connect the image plugin on Perchance.');
      });
    });
    // data tab
    byId('wipeBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){
      if (!confirm('Erase the whole conversation and everything the character has learned? This cannot be undone.')) return;
      var del = []; try { for (var i=0;i<localStorage.length;i++){ var key = localStorage.key(i); if (key && key.indexOf(NS)===0) del.push(key); } } catch(e){}
      del.forEach(function(key){ try { localStorage.removeItem(key); } catch(e){} });
      queue = []; state = Object.assign({}, DEF_STATE); persistState();
      threadCol.innerHTML=''; threadCol.appendChild(emptyTemplate()); emptyState = byId('emptyState');
      var tr = document.createElement('div'); tr.className='typing'; tr.id='typingRow'; tr.innerHTML='<i></i><i></i><i></i>'; threadCol.appendChild(tr);
      streamEl.innerHTML = '<div class="idle">Her thoughts will appear here as she works.</div>'; lastIdle = true;
      ensureUserPartition().then(buildEngine); updateCharLabel(); refreshMemStats(); renderFactList(); renderRoster();
    });
    byId('exportBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){
      var dump = {}; try { for (var i=0;i<localStorage.length;i++){ var key = localStorage.key(i); if (key && key.indexOf(NS)===0) dump[key] = localStorage.getItem(key); } } catch(e){}
      var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify({ format:'chloe-solo', version:SOLO_VERSION, data:dump }, null, 0)], { type:'application/json' });
      var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob); a.download = 'chloe-solo-memory.json'; a.click();
      setText('dataNote', 'exported.'); toast('Memory exported', 'success');
    });
    byId('importBtn').addEventListener('click', function(){ byId('importFile').click(); });
    byId('importFile').addEventListener('change', function(){ var f = this.files && this.files[0]; if (!f) return; var r = new FileReader(); r.onload = function(){ try { var obj = JSON.parse(r.result); var d = obj && obj.data; if (!d) throw 0; Object.keys(d).forEach(function(key){ try { localStorage.setItem(key, d[key]); } catch(e){} }); state = loadState(); queue = loadQueue(); location.reload(); } catch(e){ setText('dataNote','that did not look like a Chloe Solo export.'); } }; r.readAsText(f); });
  }
  function emptyTemplate(){ var d = document.createElement('div'); d.className='empty'; d.id='emptyState'; d.innerHTML='<h2>Say hello.</h2><div>Characters remember what you tell them and think before they speak \u2014 open <b>Thoughts</b> to watch.</div>'; return d; }

  /* ---- mind drawer open/close + speed ---- */
  function wireMind(){
    streamEl = byId('stream');
    function openMind(){ byId('mind').classList.add('open'); state.mindOpen = true; persistState(); }
    function closeMindFn(){ byId('mind').classList.remove('open'); state.mindOpen = false; persistState(); }
    byId('openMind').addEventListener('click', openMind);
    byId('mindTab').addEventListener('click', openMind);
    byId('closeMind').addEventListener('click', closeMindFn);
  }

  /* ---- composer wiring ---- */
  function wireComposer(){
    var inp = byId('input'), btn = byId('sendBtn');
    function grow(){ inp.style.height='auto'; inp.style.height = Math.min(160, inp.scrollHeight) + 'px'; btn.disabled = !inp.value.trim(); }
    inp.addEventListener('input', grow);
    inp.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){ if (e.key==='Enter' && !e.shiftKey){ e.preventDefault(); sendUserMessage(); } });
    btn.addEventListener('click', sendUserMessage);
  }

  /* ---- boot ---- */
  /* ============ appearance: theme mode (system/light/dark) + accent colour, saved to state ============ */
  var ACCENT_PRESETS = [
    { name:'Indigo', hex:'#5B62E0' }, { name:'Violet', hex:'#8A5BD0' }, { name:'Rose', hex:'#C2417A' },
    { name:'Coral', hex:'#C0562B' }, { name:'Amber', hex:'#B8902A' }, { name:'Teal', hex:'#2E9E7B' },
    { name:'Ocean', hex:'#2E7DD1' }, { name:'Forest', hex:'#5C8A3A' }, { name:'Slate', hex:'#5A6478' }
  ];
  function clampN(n,a,b){ return Math.max(a, Math.min(b, n)); }
  function hexToHsl(hex){
    hex = String(hex||'').replace('#',''); if (hex.length===3) hex = hex.replace(/(.)/g,'$1$1');
    var r=parseInt(hex.slice(0,2),16)/255, g=parseInt(hex.slice(2,4),16)/255, b=parseInt(hex.slice(4,6),16)/255;
    var mx=Math.max(r,g,b), mn=Math.min(r,g,b), hh=0, s=0, l=(mx+mn)/2;
    if (mx!==mn){ var d=mx-mn; s = l>0.5 ? d/(2-mx-mn) : d/(mx+mn);
      hh = mx===r ? (g-b)/d+(g<b?6:0) : mx===g ? (b-r)/d+2 : (r-g)/d+4; hh/=6; }
    return { h:hh*360, s:s*100, l:l*100 };
  }
  function hslToHex(h,s,l){
    h=(h%360+360)%360; s=clampN(s,0,100)/100; l=clampN(l,0,100)/100;
    var c=(1-Math.abs(2*l-1))*s, x=c*(1-Math.abs((h/60)%2-1)), m=l-c/2, r=0,g=0,b=0;
    if (h<60){r=c;g=x;} else if(h<120){r=x;g=c;} else if(h<180){g=c;b=x;} else if(h<240){g=x;b=c;} else if(h<300){r=x;b=c;} else {r=c;b=x;}
    function hx(v){ return ('0'+Math.round((v+m)*255).toString(16)).slice(-2); }
    return '#'+hx(r)+hx(g)+hx(b);
  }
  function effectiveDark(){
    if (state.theme === 'dark') return true;
    if (state.theme === 'light') return false;
    try { return !!(window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches); } catch(e){ return false; }
  }
  function applyThemeMode(){
    var root = document.documentElement;
    if (state.theme === 'light' || state.theme === 'dark') root.setAttribute('data-theme', state.theme);
    else root.removeAttribute('data-theme');
  }
  function applyAccent(){
    var root = document.documentElement, props = ['--accent','--accent-ink','--accent-soft','--accent-line'];
    if (!state.accent){ props.forEach(function(p){ root.style.removeProperty(p); }); return; }
    var c = hexToHsl(state.accent), dark = effectiveDark();
    if (dark){
      root.style.setProperty('--accent',      hslToHex(c.h, c.s, clampN(c.l,58,70)));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-ink',  hslToHex(c.h, c.s, 77));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-soft', hslToHex(c.h, clampN(c.s,18,45), 16));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-line', hslToHex(c.h, clampN(c.s,18,50), 34));
    } else {
      root.style.setProperty('--accent',      hslToHex(c.h, c.s, clampN(c.l,46,60)));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-ink',  hslToHex(c.h, c.s, clampN(c.l-14,26,46)));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-soft', hslToHex(c.h, clampN(c.s,40,82), 94));
      root.style.setProperty('--accent-line', hslToHex(c.h, clampN(c.s,30,72), 84));
    }
  }
  function applyAppearance(){ applyThemeMode(); applyAccent(); }
  function renderAppearance(){
    var seg = byId('themeSeg');
    if (seg) Array.prototype.forEach.call(seg.querySelectorAll('.segbtn'), function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('on', (state.theme||'system') === b.getAttribute('data-mode'));
      if (!b.__w){ b.__w=1; b.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.theme = b.getAttribute('data-mode'); persistState(); applyAppearance(); renderAppearance(); recolorMessages(); }); }
    });
    var sw = byId('accentSwatches');
    if (sw){ sw.innerHTML='';
      ACCENT_PRESETS.forEach(function(p){
        var b=document.createElement('button'); b.className='swatch'+(((state.accent||'#5B62E0').toLowerCase()===p.hex.toLowerCase())?' on':''); b.style.background=p.hex; b.title=p.name;
        b.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.accent = p.hex; persistState(); applyAppearance(); renderAppearance(); });
        sw.appendChild(b);
      });
    }
    var cc = byId('accentCustom');
    if (cc){ cc.value = state.accent || '#5B62E0'; if (!cc.__w){ cc.__w=1;
      cc.addEventListener('input', function(){ state.accent = cc.value; persistState(); applyAppearance(); });
      cc.addEventListener('change', function(){ renderAppearance(); }); } }
    var note = byId('accentNote'); if (note) note.textContent = state.accent ? ('using ' + state.accent.toUpperCase()) : 'default';
    var rb = byId('appearanceReset'); if (rb && !rb.__w){ rb.__w=1; rb.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.theme='system'; state.accent=null; persistState(); applyAppearance(); renderAppearance(); recolorMessages(); toast('Appearance reset','success'); }); }
  }
  // a character's highlight colour: user override, else the auto palette colour (primary -> default accent)
  function colorFor(id){
    if (id === BOT_ID) return state.botColor || null;
    var c = (state.cast || []).filter(function(x){ return x.id === id; })[0];
    return (c && c.color) || castColor(id);
  }
  // restyle already-rendered messages when a character's colour changes (immediate, no reload)
  function recolorMessages(){
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('#thread .msg.her[data-cid]'), function(w){
      var color = colorFor(w.getAttribute('data-cid'));
      if (color || isGroup()){ w.classList.add('hascolor'); w.style.setProperty('--speaker', color || 'var(--accent-ink)'); var who=w.querySelector('.who'); if (who) who.style.color = color || ''; }
      else { w.classList.remove('hascolor'); w.style.removeProperty('--speaker'); var who2=w.querySelector('.who'); if (who2) who2.style.color=''; }
    });
  }
  function boot(){
    applyAppearance();   // honour saved theme + accent before first paint
    try { if (window.matchMedia){ var __mq = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)'); var __onScheme = function(){ if ((state.theme||'system')==='system'){ applyAccent(); recolorMessages(); } }; __mq.addEventListener ? __mq.addEventListener('change', __onScheme) : (__mq.addListener && __mq.addListener(__onScheme)); } } catch(e){}
    threadCol = byId('threadCol'); emptyState = byId('emptyState'); streamEl = byId('stream');
    threadScroller = makeSticky(byId('thread'), byId('jumpThread'));
    mindScroller = makeSticky(byId('stream'), byId('jumpMind'));
    // typing indicator row lives at the end of the column
    var tr = document.createElement('div'); tr.className='typing'; tr.id='typingRow'; tr.innerHTML='<i></i><i></i><i></i>'; threadCol.appendChild(tr);
    installMockIfNeeded();
    installPainter();
    wrapAiForStreaming();   // stream her replies token-by-token (idempotent; re-run post-engine for late plugin load)
    wireTokenizer();        // exact token counts from the page's tokenizer (else the engine falls back to chars/4)
    requestPersistentStorage();   // ask the browser not to evict her memory under storage pressure
    clearStaleLocks();            // remove any leftover run-lock/pending key from a prior load
    updateCharLabel();
    wireComposer(); wireMind(); wireSettings(); wireToolbar(); wireGallery(); wireCommunity();
    if (state.mindOpen == null ? window.innerWidth > 880 : state.mindOpen) byId('mind').classList.add('open');   // remembered across refreshes (first run: open on wide screens)
    // restore the visible conversation
    if (queue.length){ if (emptyState && emptyState.parentNode){ emptyState.parentNode.removeChild(emptyState); emptyState=null; } queue.forEach(function(m){ renderMessage(m.author.bot ? 'her' : 'you', m.author.bot ? (state.botName||'Chloe') : (m.author.username || state.userName || 'You'), m.content); }); }
    ensureUserPartition().then(buildEngine).then(function(){ wrapAiForStreaming(); refreshClock(); renderRoster(); startAutoSave(); });
    setInterval(refreshClock, 60000);   // keep her clock + injections current across a long session
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', boot); else boot();

  // expose a couple of shims the inlined char block reaches for (defined above as hoisted fns;
  // these assignments make them visible if the char block runs in a nested scope)
  window.__solo = { call: call, byId: byId, setText: setText, log: log, refresh: refresh, selChannel: selChannel, addToScene: addToScene };
})();
</script>
<script>
/* The AICC character importer + persona authoring, lifted from Chloe-bot (1:1 with AI Character Chat).
   It uses the shims published on window.__solo by the glue above. */
(function () {
  var S = window.__solo || {};
  function byId(id){ return S.byId ? S.byId(id) : document.getElementById(id); }
  function setText(id,t){ return S.setText ? S.setText(id,t) : (byId(id)&&(byId(id).textContent=t)); }
  function call(m,a){ return S.call ? S.call(m,a) : Promise.resolve({ok:false}); }
  function log(m){ return S.log ? S.log(m) : void 0; }
  function refresh(){ return S.refresh ? S.refresh() : void 0; }
  function selChannel(){ return S.selChannel ? S.selChannel() : 'solo'; }
  function addToScene(a){ return S.addToScene ? S.addToScene(a) : false; }
  // Pure in-browser: decompress -> decode (CBOR/JSON/scavenge) -> extract characters + their
  // thread memories. No upload, no network except the CBOR decoder CDN on first .cbor.gz.
  var CHARCBOR = null;
  function charLoadCBOR() {
    if (CHARCBOR) return Promise.resolve(CHARCBOR);
    return import('https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/cbor-x@1.6.0/dist/index.js')
      .then(function (m) { CHARCBOR = (m && m.default) ? m.default : m; return CHARCBOR; })
      .catch(function () { return null; });
  }
  function charGunzip(arrayBuffer) {
    if (typeof DecompressionStream === 'undefined') return Promise.resolve(new Uint8Array(arrayBuffer));
    try {
      var ds = new DecompressionStream('gzip');
      var blobParts = []; blobParts.push(arrayBuffer);
      return new Response(new Blob(blobParts).stream().pipeThrough(ds)).arrayBuffer()
        .then(function (buf) { return new Uint8Array(buf); })
        .catch(function () { return new Uint8Array(arrayBuffer); });
    } catch (e) { return Promise.resolve(new Uint8Array(arrayBuffer)); }
  }
  function charScavenge(text) {
    var open = String.fromCharCode(123), close = String.fromCharCode(125);
    var start = text.indexOf(open); if (start < 0) return null;
    var depth = 0, inStr = false, esc = false;
    for (var i = start; i < text.length; i++) {
      var ch = text[i];
      if (inStr) { if (esc) esc = false; else if (ch === '\\') esc = true; else if (ch === '"') inStr = false; }
      else { if (ch === '"') inStr = true; else if (ch === open) depth++; else if (ch === close) { depth--; if (depth === 0) { try { return JSON.parse(text.slice(start, i + 1)); } catch (e) { return null; } } } }
    }
    return null;
  }
  function charDecode(bytes) {
    if (CHARCBOR && typeof CHARCBOR.decode === 'function') { try { return CHARCBOR.decode(bytes); } catch (e) {} }
    var text = ''; try { text = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: false }).decode(bytes); } catch (e) {}
    if (text) { try { return JSON.parse(text); } catch (e) {} var s = charScavenge(text); if (s) return s; }
    return null;
  }
  function charExtractStores(obj) {
    var out = { characters: [], threads: [], messages: [] };
    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return out;
    // Dexie DB export — AI Character Chat's NATIVE "export characters" format (a .json.gz whose
    // formatName is "dexie"). The tables live under data.data[] as { tableName, rows }; pull the
    // character/thread/message rows straight out. This is the common AICC export and must come first.
    var dx = obj.data && obj.data.data;
    if (obj.formatName === 'dexie' || Array.isArray(dx)) {
      if (Array.isArray(dx)) dx.forEach(function (blk) {
        if (!blk || !Array.isArray(blk.rows)) return;
        if (blk.tableName === 'characters') out.characters = blk.rows;
        else if (blk.tableName === 'threads') out.threads = blk.rows;
        else if (blk.tableName === 'messages') out.messages = blk.rows;
      });
      if (out.characters.length || out.threads.length || out.messages.length) return out;
    }
    if (obj.stores && typeof obj.stores === 'object') {
      ['characters', 'threads', 'messages'].forEach(function (k) { if (Array.isArray(obj.stores[k])) out[k] = obj.stores[k]; });
      return out;
    }
    if (obj.addCharacter) { var addList = []; addList.push(obj.addCharacter); out.characters = addList; return out; }
    if (Array.isArray(obj.characters)) { ['characters', 'threads', 'messages'].forEach(function (k) { if (Array.isArray(obj[k])) out[k] = obj[k]; }); return out; }
    if (obj.name || obj.roleInstruction || obj.systemMessage) { var oneChar = []; oneChar.push(obj); out.characters = oneChar; return out; }
    return out;
  }
  function charNormalize(c) {
    if (c.roleInstruction === undefined && c.systemMessage != null) c.roleInstruction = c.systemMessage;
    if (c.roleInstruction === undefined) c.roleInstruction = '';
    if (!c.name) c.name = 'Unnamed';
    var instr = String(c.roleInstruction || '');
    // AICC parity: fold in its other persona fields when they're literal text. Skip "@preset"
    // references (e.g. "@roleplay1") — those are AICC-internal aliases that carry no meaning here.
    var gwi = String(c.generalWritingInstructions || '').trim();
    if (gwi && gwi.charAt(0) !== '@') instr += '\n\nWriting style: ' + gwi;
    var rem = String(c.reminderMessage || '').trim();
    if (rem) instr += '\n\nKeep in mind: ' + rem;
    var avatar = (c.avatar && c.avatar.url) ? c.avatar.url : (c.avatarUrl || '');
    var im = Array.isArray(c.initialMessages) ? c.initialMessages : [];
    var opening = im.map(function (m) {
      return { author: String((m && (m.author || m.role)) || 'ai'), content: String((m && (m.content || m.message || m.text)) || '') };
    }).filter(function (m) { return m.content.trim(); }).slice(0, 8);
    return { name: String(c.name), instruction: instr, avatar: avatar, initialMessages: opening, id: (c.id != null ? c.id : null), uuid: c.uuid || null };
  }
  // respool's replay-from-file: timeless memories already stored on a thread's messages.
  function charMemoriesForCharacter(stores, character) {
    var threads = (stores.threads || []).filter(function (t) {
      return t && (t.characterId === character.id || (character.id == null && (stores.characters || []).length === 1));
    });
    var threadIds = {}; threads.forEach(function (t) { threadIds[t.id] = true; });
    var texts = [], seen = {};
    (stores.messages || []).forEach(function (m) {
      if (!m || !m.memoriesEndingHere) return;
      if (threads.length && !threadIds[m.threadId]) return;
      var levels = m.memoriesEndingHere;
      Object.keys(levels).forEach(function (lvl) {
        (levels[lvl] || []).forEach(function (mem) {
          var t = (mem && mem.text) ? mem.text : (typeof mem === 'string' ? mem : null);
          if (!t) return; var k = t.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9 ]+/g, '').trim();
          if (k && !seen[k]) { seen[k] = true; texts.push(String(t).slice(0, 200)); }
        });
      });
    });
    return texts;
  }

  var CHARSTATE = { stores: null, chars: [], picked: null, memories: [] };
  function charSetStatus(msg, kind) { var el = byId('charStatus'); if (el) { el.textContent = msg; el.style.color = kind === 'er' ? 'var(--bad)' : (kind === 'ok' ? 'var(--good)' : 'var(--muted)'); } }

  // Shared sink for raw bytes from ANY source (file, fetched link). Decompress if gzipped, decode,
  // extract characters. needCbor preloads the decoder for .cbor/.gz payloads.
  function charIngestBytes(buf, label, needCbor) {
    var pre = needCbor ? charLoadCBOR() : Promise.resolve(null);
    return pre.then(function () {
      var bytes = new Uint8Array(buf);
      var gz = bytes.length > 2 && bytes[0] === 0x1f && bytes[1] === 0x8b;
      return (gz ? charGunzip(buf) : Promise.resolve(bytes));
    }).then(function (bytes) {
      var obj = charDecode(bytes);
      return charIngestObject(obj, label);
    });
  }
  // Shared sink for an already-decoded object (raw pasted JSON skips decompression).
  function charIngestObject(obj, label) {
    if (!obj) { charSetStatus('Could not read ' + (label || 'that input') + ' \u2014 it may be empty or an unsupported format.', 'er'); return false; }
    var stores = charExtractStores(obj);
    var chars = (stores.characters || []).map(charNormalize).filter(function (c) { return c.name; });
    if (!chars.length) { charSetStatus('No characters found in ' + (label || 'that input') + '.', 'er'); return false; }
    CHARSTATE.stores = stores; CHARSTATE.chars = chars; CHARSTATE.picked = null;
    charSetStatus('Found ' + chars.length + ' character' + (chars.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + '. Pick one below.', 'ok');
    charRenderList();
    return true;
  }

  function charLoadFile(file) {
    if (!file) return;
    charSetStatus('Reading ' + file.name + ' (' + Math.round(file.size / 1024) + ' KB)\u2026');
    var needCbor = /\.cbor(\.gz)?$/i.test(file.name) || /\.gz$/i.test(file.name);
    file.arrayBuffer()
      .then(function (buf) { return charIngestBytes(buf, file.name, needCbor); })
      .catch(function (e) { charSetStatus('Failed to read the file: ' + ((e && e.message) || e), 'er'); });
  }

  // Recover an AICC upload id from a share link, a direct user.uploads.dev link, or a bare hex id
  // Returns a normalized FILEID.gz, or null.
  function charExtractFileId(raw) {
    var s = String(raw || '').trim();
    var m = s.match(/[?&]data=[^~]*~([a-z0-9]{16,}(?:\.gz)?)/i);
    if (m) return m[1].replace(/\.gz$/i, '') + '.gz';
    m = s.match(/user\.uploads\.dev\/file\/([a-z0-9]{16,}(?:\.gz)?)/i);
    if (m) return m[1].replace(/\.gz$/i, '') + '.gz';
    m = s.match(/^([a-f0-9]{24,})(?:\.gz)?$/i);
    if (m) return m[1] + '.gz';
    return null;
  }

  // Resilient fetch (DESIGN-transport, roadmap #9). A bare fetch dies on the first 429 or network blip;
  // this retries transient failures (429 / 408 / 5xx / network reject) with exponential backoff + FULL
  // JITTER — the AWS "Exponential Backoff and Jitter" strategy that p-retry / cockatiel / exponential-
  // backoff all use: wait a random time in [0, min(cap, base·2^attempt)), so a rate-limited host isn't
  // hammered in lockstep. A Retry-After header (seconds) is honored as a floor. Non-retryable statuses
  // (e.g. 404 removed/quarantined) fail fast — the final non-ok response is handed back to the caller.
  // fetchImpl/sleep are injectable for testing; they default to the real fetch + setTimeout.
  function fetchRetry(url, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var max = opts.retries == null ? 3 : opts.retries;
    var base = opts.baseMs || 500, cap = opts.capMs || 8000;
    var doFetch = opts.fetchImpl || (typeof fetch === 'function' ? fetch : null);
    var sleep = opts.sleep || function (ms) { return new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, ms); }); };
    var onRetry = opts.onRetry;
    function jitter(n) { return Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.min(cap, base * Math.pow(2, n))); }
    function retryable(st) { return st === 429 || st === 408 || (st >= 500 && st <= 599); }
    function attempt(n) {
      return Promise.resolve(doFetch(url, opts.init)).then(function (res) {
        if (res.ok || !retryable(res.status) || n >= max) return res;   // success, or hand the final non-ok back
        var wait = jitter(n);
        var ra = res.headers && res.headers.get && res.headers.get('Retry-After');
        if (ra != null) { var sec = parseFloat(ra); if (!isNaN(sec) && sec >= 0) wait = Math.max(wait, Math.ceil(sec * 1000)); }
        if (onRetry) onRetry(n + 1, max, wait, res.status);
        return sleep(wait).then(function () { return attempt(n + 1); });
      }, function (err) {
        if (n >= max) throw err;            // network error: retry until exhausted, then surface
        var wait = jitter(n);
        if (onRetry) onRetry(n + 1, max, wait, 'network');
        return sleep(wait).then(function () { return attempt(n + 1); });
      });
    }
    return Promise.resolve().then(function () { if (!doFetch) throw new Error('no fetch available in this context'); return attempt(0); });
  }

  // Load a character from pasted text: a link/file-id (fetched from user.uploads.dev) OR raw JSON.
  function charLoadText(raw) {
    var s = String(raw || '').trim();
    if (!s) { var ie = byId('charUrlInput'); if (ie) ie.focus(); return; }
    var fileId = charExtractFileId(s);
    if (fileId) {
      var url = 'https://user.uploads.dev/file/' + fileId;
      charSetStatus('Fetching ' + url + '\u2026');
      charLoadCBOR().then(function () { return fetchRetry(url, { onRetry: function (n, mx, wait, why) { charSetStatus('Fetch hit ' + (why === 'network' ? 'a network hiccup' : ('HTTP ' + why)) + ' \u2014 retry ' + n + '/' + mx + ' in ~' + Math.max(1, Math.round(wait / 1000)) + 's\u2026'); } }); })
        .then(function (res) { if (!res.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + res.status + ' \u2014 the file may have been removed or quarantined'); return res.arrayBuffer(); })
        .then(function (buf) { return charIngestBytes(buf, 'the fetched file', true); })
        .catch(function (e) { charSetStatus('Could not fetch that link: ' + ((e && e.message) || e) + '. You can also download the file and drop it here.', 'er'); });
      return;
    }
    // Not a link/id -> try to parse it as raw character JSON directly.
    var startsObj = s.charAt(0) === String.fromCharCode(123) || s.charAt(0) === '[';
    if (startsObj) {
      var obj = null; try { obj = JSON.parse(s); } catch (e) { obj = charScavenge(s); }
      if (obj) { charSetStatus('Reading pasted character data\u2026'); charIngestObject(obj, 'the pasted data'); return; }
      charSetStatus('That looked like JSON but could not be parsed. Check it is a complete character export.', 'er');
      return;
    }
    charSetStatus('Paste a share link, a user.uploads.dev link, a file ID, or raw character JSON.', 'er');
  }

  function charRenderList() {
    var box = byId('charList'); while (box.firstChild) box.removeChild(box.firstChild);
    byId('charListCard').style.display = CHARSTATE.chars.length ? '' : 'none';
    CHARSTATE.chars.forEach(function (c, idx) {
      var row = document.createElement('div'); row.className = 'urow charrow';
      var grow = document.createElement('div'); grow.className = 'ugrow';
      var nm = document.createElement('div'); nm.className = 'uname'; nm.textContent = c.name; grow.appendChild(nm);
      var meta = document.createElement('div'); meta.className = 'umeta';
      var memCount = charMemoriesForCharacter(CHARSTATE.stores, c).length;
      var st = document.createElement('span'); st.className = 'uid';
      st.textContent = (c.instruction ? (c.instruction.length + ' chars of personality') : 'no personality text') + ' \u00b7 ' + memCount + ' memor' + (memCount === 1 ? 'y' : 'ies');
      meta.appendChild(st); grow.appendChild(meta); row.appendChild(grow);
      row.addEventListener('click', function () {
        CHARSTATE.picked = c;
        var rows = box.querySelectorAll('.charrow'); for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) rows[i].className = 'urow charrow';
        row.className = 'urow charrow sel';
        charRenderPreview(c);
      });
      box.appendChild(row);
    });
  }

  function charRenderPreview(c) {
    byId('charPreviewCard').style.display = '';
    setText('charPreviewName', c.name);
    byId('charInstruction').value = c.instruction || '(this character has no role instruction)';
    CHARSTATE.memories = charMemoriesForCharacter(CHARSTATE.stores, c);
    var mh = byId('charMemHead'), ml = byId('charMemList');
    if (CHARSTATE.memories.length) {
      mh.style.display = ''; ml.style.display = '';
      while (ml.firstChild) ml.removeChild(ml.firstChild);
      CHARSTATE.memories.slice(0, 30).forEach(function (t) { var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = '\u2022 ' + t; ml.appendChild(d); });
      byId('charSeedChk').checked = true; byId('charSeedChk').disabled = false;
    } else {
      mh.style.display = 'none'; ml.style.display = 'none';
      byId('charSeedChk').checked = false; byId('charSeedChk').disabled = true;
    }
    setText('charInstallNote', '');
  }

  function charInstall() {
    var c = CHARSTATE.picked; if (!c) { setText('charInstallNote', 'pick a character first'); return; }
    var replace = byId('charReplaceChk').checked;
    var seed = byId('charSeedChk').checked && CHARSTATE.memories.length;
    var jobs = [];
    if (replace) jobs.push(call('config.setCharacter', { name: c.name, instruction: c.instruction, avatar: c.avatar, initialMessages: c.initialMessages }));
    if (seed) jobs.push(call('character.seedMemories', { name: c.name, memories: CHARSTATE.memories, channelId: selChannel() }));
    if (!jobs.length) { setText('charInstallNote', 'nothing selected to apply'); return; }
    Promise.all(jobs).then(function () {
      setText('charInstallNote', 'done \u2014 the default character is now ' + c.name + (seed ? ' (with ' + CHARSTATE.memories.length + ' memories)' : ''));
      log('character installed: ' + c.name + (replace ? ' (personality replaced)' : '') + (seed ? ', ' + CHARSTATE.memories.length + ' memories seeded' : ''));
      refresh();
    });
  }

  (function charWire() {
    var pick = byId('charPickBtn'), fileEl = byId('charFile'), drop = byId('charDrop');
    if (pick && fileEl) { pick.addEventListener('click', function () { fileEl.click(); }); fileEl.addEventListener('change', function () { if (fileEl.files && fileEl.files[0]) charLoadFile(fileEl.files[0]); }); }
    if (drop) {
      ['dragover', 'dragenter'].forEach(function (ev) { drop.addEventListener(ev, function (e) { e.preventDefault(); drop.className = 'chardrop drag'; }); });
      ['dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(function (ev) { drop.addEventListener(ev, function (e) { e.preventDefault(); drop.className = 'chardrop'; }); });
      drop.addEventListener('drop', function (e) { var f = e.dataTransfer && e.dataTransfer.files && e.dataTransfer.files[0]; if (f) charLoadFile(f); });
    }
    var ub = byId('charUrlBtn'); if (ub) ub.addEventListener('click', function () { charLoadText(byId('charUrlInput').value); });
    var ui = byId('charUrlInput'); if (ui) ui.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); charLoadText(ui.value); } });
    var pb = byId('charPasteBtn'); if (pb) pb.addEventListener('click', function () {
      if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.readText) {
        navigator.clipboard.readText().then(function (txt) { byId('charUrlInput').value = txt; charLoadText(txt); }, function () { charSetStatus('Clipboard read was blocked \u2014 paste into the box manually, then click Load.', 'er'); });
      } else { charSetStatus('This browser won\u2019t allow clipboard reads here \u2014 paste into the box manually, then click Load.', 'er'); byId('charUrlInput').focus(); }
    });
    var ib = byId('charInstallBtn'); if (ib) ib.addEventListener('click', charInstall);
    var asb = byId('charAddSceneBtn'); if (asb) asb.addEventListener('click', function () {
      var c = CHARSTATE.picked; if (!c) { setText('charInstallNote', 'pick a character first'); return; }
      if (typeof addToScene === 'function' && addToScene({ name: c.name, instruction: c.instruction, avatar: c.avatar })) setText('charInstallNote', c.name + ' added to the scene');
    });
    var aab = byId('charAuthorAddBtn'); if (aab) aab.addEventListener('click', function () {
      var nm = (byId('charAuthorName').value || '').trim(), instr = (byId('charAuthorInstr').value || '').trim();
      if (!nm) { setText('charAuthorNote', 'give your character a name first'); return; }
      if (!instr) { setText('charAuthorNote', 'write a sentence or two about who they are'); return; }
      if (typeof addToScene === 'function' && addToScene({ name: nm, instruction: instr, avatar: '' })) setText('charAuthorNote', nm + ' added to the scene');
    });
    var ab = byId('charAuthorBtn'); if (ab) ab.addEventListener('click', function () {
      var nm = (byId('charAuthorName').value || '').trim();
      var instr = (byId('charAuthorInstr').value || '').trim();
      if (!nm) { setText('charAuthorNote', 'give your character a name first'); return; }
      if (!instr) { setText('charAuthorNote', 'write a sentence or two about who they are'); return; }
      setText('charAuthorNote', '\u2026');
      call('config.setCharacter', { name: nm, instruction: instr, avatar: '' }).then(function (res) {
        if (res && res.ok) { setText('charAuthorNote', 'done \u2014 she is now ' + nm); log('character authored: ' + nm + ' (personality replaced)'); refresh(); }
        else setText('charAuthorNote', 'could not apply: ' + ((res && res.reason) || 'unknown'));
      });
    });
    var cb = byId('charClearBtn'); if (cb) cb.addEventListener('click', function () {
      call('config.setCharacter', { name: null }).then(function () { setText('charCurrent', 'default Chloe'); log('character cleared \u2014 back to default Chloe'); refresh(); });
    });
  })();

})();
</script>
